Ingredient specifications including bioburden, impurities, properties, and recommended storage conditions, should be understood. Dry solids should be stored in environments with controlled humidity and temperature. Solutes used in media and buffer formulation are usually not sterile; the solutions using these ingredients should be:

  • Sterilized
  • Stored under bacteriostatic conditions
  • Used within specified hold periods (with limited shelf life — before microbial contaminants proliferate)

Media are typically at higher risk than buffer solutions because of their growth promoting properties. The composition of media may affect their susceptibility to contamination: defined chemical media may be considered lower risk. The use of sera can affect the susceptibility to contamination. Consumables also represent potential sources of contamination.

Contamination from the environment and crossover contamination from neighboring systems can occur for open processes when these systems are in close proximity. Protecting an open system from potential contamination by operators requires effective sanitary gowning and/or other layers of system protection, including a clean environment. Enhanced gowning may help reduce bioburden levels in a suite.

Closing a system is considered an effective approach to mitigating the risk of crossover contamination or contamination from the environment. Closing a system also effectively mitigates the risk of contamination by personnel. Contamination from the environment of a closed system would require a breach of that system, typically as a result of multiple failures of mechanical systems (e.g., valve and/or filter failures) representing the layers of protection to that system. Crossover contamination of two adjacent closed systems would require the breach of integrity of both systems.

Carryover is typically a result of inadequate system preparation including cleaning and sanitization operations between manufacturing batches. Validation of the cleaning and sanitization program should adequately mitigate the risk of carryover. An effective cleaning and sanitization program should include adequate monitoring to ensure critical parameters are maintained, including:

  • Temperature
  • Time
  • Action (impingement and/or turbulent flow; pressure)
  • Chemical concentration and components
  • Sequence of cleaning steps

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Hold Period（保存期限）的科學基礎： 培養基配製後並非立即使用，必須設定「最長保存時限」（hold period）。這個時限不是任意訂定的，而是基於微生物生長動力學研究——在特定溫度和 pH 條件下，從「零污染」到「污染超出可接受範圍」需要多少時間。Hold period 到期後，培養基必須廢棄或重新滅菌。

培養基 vs 緩衝液的風險差異： 培養基（Media）含有碳源、氮源、維生素等豐富營養成分，是微生物的「五星級餐廳」，污染風險顯著高於緩衝液（Buffer）。化學限定培養基（defined chemical media）因組成明確、不含不確定的動物源成分，比複雜培養基（complex media）風險更低。

重點提示 Key Note

密閉系統的「多重失效」保護邏輯： Vol.6 明確指出，一個真正密閉的系統，要使環境污染進入，必須同時發生「多重機械失效」（multiple failures）——例如同時失效的閥門和過濾器。這種「多重失效才能污染」的設計，正是密閉系統比開放系統更安全的根本原因，也是為何密閉系統可以放置在較低等級環境中的監管依據。

CIP 的 TACT 原則： 有效清洗需要同時滿足四個要素——Temperature（溫度）、Action（機械衝擊力/湍流）、Chemical（清潔劑濃度）、Time（接觸時間）。任何一個要素不足，整體清洗效果就會大打折扣。這也是 CIP 驗證的核心評估架構。

公式與框架 Framework

CIP 有效性 = f(溫度 × 作用力 × 化學濃度 × 時間 × 步驟順序)

關鍵概念：
- 提高溫度 → 可降低化學濃度需求
- 增加機械衝擊力 → 可縮短清洗時間
- 步驟順序錯誤（如鹼洗後未充分沖洗就進行酸洗）
  → 中和反應產物可能堵塞管路或損傷設備

CIP 驗證三要素：
1. 視覺清潔（visually clean）
2. 微生物指標（bioburden limits）
3. 殘留限度（residue limits, e.g., TOC, conductivity）

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果一個 2,000L 生物反應器的 SIP 失效，但設備仍維持密閉狀態（閥門未打開），環境中的微生物是否會進入？為什麼？
  2. CDMO 承接兩個相鄰批次的不同客戶產品時，CIP 驗證需要涵蓋哪些額外的考量？
4.3 Providing Appropriate and Effective Layers of Protection to a Bioprocess Unit Operation — 保護層次：Vol.6 的知識核心

原文內容 Original Text

Different levels of bioburden and contamination control are needed for different unit operations. Different approaches and layers of protection are required to mitigate the risk of contamination from the environment for these different operations. The impact (or severity) of bioburden or particulate contamination will differ in different situations. The mitigation of risk from contamination present in the environment requires the implementation of sufficient layers of appropriate protection to a process system. The purpose of this section is to discuss possible options for closing an operation by providing appropriate layers of protection to that operation.

The use of highly classified cleanrooms for open operations can reduce the level of potential environmental contaminants. For aseptic operations, classified cleanrooms provide an environment with lower bioburden. For other bioprocesses, classified cleanrooms can lower the particulate burden and bioburden within the environment.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts — 洋蔥式保護層次模型

這是整本 Vol.6 最重要的概念。ISPE 的核心主張是：

每一層有效的保護 = 可降低一個等級的潔淨室要求

就像洋蔥一樣，越多層皮（保護層），核心（產品）越安全，外層環境的重要性也就越低。

比喻說明 Analogy

洋蔥式防護（每一層洋蔥皮 = 一層保護）：

想像產品是洋蔥的核心。每剝一層洋蔥皮（保護層），外界的「污染」都要先突破那一層才能到達核心。當洋蔥有足夠多的層（密閉設備 + 密閉傳輸管路 + 受控房間），即使最外層的環境（建築空間）並非嚴格潔淨室，產品依然安全。

洋蔥式保護層次模型（由內至外）

核心：Product (藥液)
Layer 1 — Primary Containment (初級圍堵)
密閉設備本體：焊接接頭、SIP 接口、密閉生物反應器
Layer 2 — Secondary Containment (二級圍堵)
密閉房間 / RABS / 隔離器
Layer 3 — Building Segregation (建築隔離)
不同製程區域的物理分隔，獨立 HVAC
Layer 4+ — Environmental Controls (環境管控)
潔淨室等級、更衣程序、環境監控

保護層次越多 → 外部環境等級要求越低 → 設施建設成本越低

4.3.1 Providing Appropriate Environments within Biosafety Cabinets — 生物安全櫃（BSC）的環境提供

原文內容 Original Text

Open aseptic operations require environments of extremely low bioburden, where the probability of detecting bioburden within those environments during the open operation is essentially zero/probability less than 1. Grade 5 environments, such as that found within properly managed Biosafety Cabinets (BSCs), are typically considered acceptable for open aseptic operations, as they meet this criterion. Even within BSCs, proper cleaning, operations, technique, preparation, gowning, staging, etc., and surrounding environment are required to maintain the Grade 5 condition.

Independent of the strategy used, the overall BSC management plan should include:

  • A well designed cleanroom housing the BSC. This design will consider:
    • The BSC
    • The HVAC (location of HEPA and air return) that mitigates risk of "rogue" unfiltered air currents in environment immediately surrounding the open face of the BSC
    • Adequate air change per hour rate
    • Location and design of airlock accesses
  • Restriction of the number of personnel occupying the room
  • Restriction of the amount of equipment located in room
  • Appropriate gowning of personnel
  • Proper aseptic technique in the BSC
  • Effective cleaning and sanitization of the BSC

For further information, see the ISPE Good Practice Guide: HVAC [58].

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

生物安全櫃 (Biosafety Cabinet, BSC): BSC 是細胞培養實驗室和種子準備的核心設備。它利用垂直層流（vertical laminar airflow）和 HEPA 過濾，在操作台面創造一個 Grade 5（ISO 5，等同 EU GMP A 級）的微環境。

「Rogue」空氣流的危險： 如果 HVAC 設計不當，房間內存在未受控的渦流或亂流，可能破壞 BSC 操作面附近的層流，將外部環境的微粒/微生物帶入 BSC 的開口面——這就是所謂「流氓空氣流（rogue air currents）」的危害。

重點提示 Key Note

BSC ≠ 無限等級 5 保護： 即使在 BSC 內操作，Grade 5 環境也並非自動達成——需要搭配正確的操作技術（aseptic technique）、適當更衣、定期清潔消毒，以及良好的周邊環境設計（HVAC、氣密門道）。BSC 只是提供了潛力，人員操作行為決定了實際效果。

人員數量的重要性： 每增加一個人在 BSC 所在房間內，就增加額外的微粒和微生物負荷。這就是為什麼 BSC 操作房間通常嚴格限制人員進入數量，並且在使用中盡量排除非必要人員。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果一個 BSC 所在房間的 HVAC 回風口位置設計不當（例如位於 BSC 開口正對面），可能造成什麼問題？
  2. 在 CDMO 中，種子培養（seed train）通常在 BSC 中進行。若要從 BSC 升級到封閉式搖瓶培養系統，需要考慮哪些設計改變？
4.3.2 Strategies for Closing Bioprocess Operations — 製程密閉策略

原文內容 Original Text

The goal for closing systems is to isolate the system product contact surfaces from the surrounding environment. Available technology allows systems to be closed or isolated from the environment and by default, from each other. Effective isolation can be achieved without the need for walls or segregation of the HVAC controlling the environment housing these operations. This strategy has previously been supported by regulatory agencies (e.g., process and utility piping have traditionally and typically been housed in uncontrolled interstitial spaces).

"Transfers between unit operations are considered critical to a successful bioprocess. Figures 4.2 and 4.3 show mixed piping systems that are routinely routed through uncontrolled interstitial (or 'gray') space because these critical systems can be shown to be isolated from the environment and from each other. The environment in these uncontrolled spaces represents a non-critical aspect to the transfer operation, because the critical transfer piping is closed."

The process transfer piping systems, routed through the uncontrolled interstitial spaces, represent extensions of the process equipment to which they are attached.

[Figure 4.2: Closed Piping through Non-classified Mechanical Spaces]
[Figure 4.3: Closed Piping through Non-classified Mechanical Spaces (3D Diagram)]

This strategy has been extended to closed buffer hold vessels that may be housed in Controlled Not Classified (CNC) or uncontrolled spaces. Although housed in an uncontrolled environment, buffer hold vessels are rendered closed prior to use by effective cleaning and sanitization.

Organizations should demonstrate that their process equipment is appropriately closed (and validated as such) or the agencies will continue to expect it to be housed in classified cleanrooms.

Advances in bioprocessing include technologies that provide effective isolation of process from the environment. For closed operations, the environment becomes a property or parameter with no critical aspect according to Quality Risk Management (QRM). For a process or system to be considered closed, the product contact surfaces and process environment needs to be completely isolated from the external environment during all manipulations, including setup, transfers, sampling and other process operations.

Open systems can be rendered closed with appropriate preparation, including cleaning and sanitization operations. Risk assessments would show that isolation of the product and process from the environment represents lower risk to product quality by eliminating a significant source of hazards. The elimination of the environment as a parameter having a critical aspect can have significant impact on the process design, on the process equipment layout, and on the overall facility design.

[Figure 4.4: Open versus Closed (Ease of Contamination Figure)]

This is independent of the nature of the process or classification of the environment. As an example, bioreactors and fermenters that have been properly steamed-in-place and are appropriately closed and controlled have been shown to be capable of maintaining an axenic culture for months.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Controlled Not Classified (CNC) 空間： 這是一種介於「完全潔淨室」和「未管控空間」之間的環境——有基本的環境監控和維護要求，但不需要符合特定的 ISO 潔淨室等級。密閉緩衝液儲存槽可以放置在 CNC 空間，就是因為其密閉性讓環境分類變得不關鍵。

間隙空間（Interstitial Space）的監管接受： 生物製藥廠的管路系統穿越非分類的機械夾層（灰色空間）已是長期被監管機構接受的做法。理由是：這些管路是密閉的，環境對管路內的產品沒有影響。這個「灰色空間合理性」的原則，正是 Vol.6 的密閉策略之一。

比喻說明 Analogy

密閉管路穿越灰色空間 = 自來水管穿越牆壁： 家裡的自來水管穿過牆壁、天花板，你不會要求整面牆達到食品衛生標準，因為水是在密閉管道內流動的。生物製藥廠的製程管路穿越非潔淨的機械夾層，道理完全相同——關鍵的是管道本身的密閉性，而不是周遭牆壁的潔淨程度。

設備的「延伸」概念： 每段連接在生物反應器上的密閉管路，法規上視為生物反應器本身的延伸部分——享有與生物反應器相同的密閉保護。只要管路本身密閉，外部環境分類就無關緊要。

重點提示 Key Note

「環境成為非關鍵參數」的革命性意義： Vol.6 最重要的一句話是：對於密閉操作，「環境成為品質風險管理中無關鍵性的參數」。這句話的監管意涵是：

  • 密閉設備不需要放在潔淨室 → 建設成本大幅降低
  • 環境監控需求降低 → 運營成本降低
  • 設施設計靈活性提高 → 可在更小的潔淨室中容納更多設備

但前提是： 必須有充分的文件和驗證來「證明」密閉性——否則監管機構仍會要求潔淨室環境。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 設施設計的商業意義： 如果一個 CDMO 計劃建造一個 5,000L 不鏽鋼生物反應器廠房，選擇是：

  • 方案 A（傳統思維）: 把整個生物反應器廠房設計為 Grade 8（C 級）潔淨室。建設成本極高，HVAC 系統複雜，維運成本高。
  • 方案 B（Vol.6 策略）: 生物反應器系統經過完整的密閉驗證（SIP、壓力保持測試、過濾器完整性測試），放置在 CNC 空間。只有真正需要開放操作的區域（如取樣站、種子準備室）建設 Grade 8 潔淨室。

方案 B 可節省數百萬至千萬美元的設施建設成本，這正是 Vol.6 的核心商業價值所在。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一台已通過 SIP 驗證的 2,000L 生物反應器，若放置在 CNC 空間中，需要哪些持續性監控措施來維持其「密閉」狀態的監管合規性？
  2. 如果你是監管審查員，你會要求什麼樣的文件來確認一個「密閉系統」確實達到密閉標準？
4.4 Demonstrating that Processes are Closed — 密閉性的驗證與證明

原文內容 Original Text

4.4.1 Performing a Closure Analysis

This section provides an example of how risk assessments can be used to demonstrate that a process has been successfully isolated from the surrounding environment and that the environment no longer represents a critical aspect of this process.

Changes to a process or processing strategy should be systematically evaluated, e.g., by using a risk management tool and pre-established criteria. The tool should mitigate bias influencing the risk ranking of a hazard. The primary goal of a closure analysis is to confirm that a process unit operation can and/or should be removed from a cleanroom environment of higher classification to a controlled non classified suite. Closure analysis is a type of risk assessment that should focus on the probability and severity of exposing a process system to the surrounding environment before, during, and after the process operation. The scope of the risk assessment should be restricted to potential impact by the environment and should omit other process improvement initiatives.

Closure analysis can provide an opportunity to:

  • Evaluate and improve manufacturing processes
  • Reduce risk
  • Evaluate new and improved technologies
  • Reduce failures
  • Increase productivity

These improvements can lower the cost of manufacturing, improve consistency, increase reliability and provide a more predictable level of product quality.

For a process unit operation, all penetrations and operations that can influence the integrity of the system should be considered. Figure 4.5 shows penetrations and operations that should be considered for a stainless steel bioreactor used in a cell culture operation.

[Figure 4.5: Stainless Steel Bioreactor Used in a Cell Culture Operation — 圖示所有可能影響密閉性的穿透點與操作點]

The steps listed in Figure 4.5 represent opportunities for breach of the closed integrity of the bioreactor system. The closure analysis should consider these steps and determine whether the methodology used in the step or subsequent steps adequately protects the integrity of the closed system. Stainless steel bioreactor systems require significant manual intervention during setup. The insertion of instrumentation into lower probe belts and assembly of vent and sterile gas filters can result in particulate and bioburden contamination of the vessel and system. The risk may be adequately mitigated by performing SIP on the system prior to use.

"This risk cannot be mitigated by housing an aseptic system in a Grade 8 or Grade 7 environment. Only Grade 5 should be considered acceptable for an open aseptic system."

A hot WFI rinsing and sanitizing rinse after manual insertions, but prior to SIP, may be needed to mitigate the risk of particulate contamination within the vessel chamber. Bioburden present in the system after human intervention is usually removed using thermal sanitization and particulates should be rinsed away with condensate in a self-draining system. Following SIP, the system should be maintained under constant positive pressure by supplying sterile filtered gas. Dissolved Oxygen (DO) and pH monitoring prior to inoculation can be used to confirm success of the SIP process in rendering the bioreactor closed.

This evaluation should be repeated for all unit operations in a process.

[Figure 4.6: Phases of Risk Assessment Analysis]
[Figure 4.7: Closure Analysis Risk Assessment Workflow – Phase 1 (Process understanding, PFD/P&ID assembly, system boundary definition)]
[Figure 4.8: Closure Analysis Risk Assessment Workflow – Phase 2 (Criteria listing, closure risk ranking vs. pre-established criteria)]
[Figure 4.9: Closure Analysis Risk Assessment Workflow – Phase 3 (Mitigation options for unacceptable risk)]

The workflow should be used only for process contact operations. In the program depicted:

  • Open aseptic operations would represent the operations or steps of highest risk
  • Performing controlled bioburden operations using sterile gamma irradiated single use systems would represent the lowest risk of contamination from the environment; however, other higher value options are available that also represent acceptable low risk

Phase 3 of the closure analysis evaluates options for mitigation of unacceptable risk due to insufficient product protection or process closure.

[Figure 4.10: Fault Tree Flow Diagram — 用於最終評估密閉完整性的故障樹]

At the end of this workflow, only those elements, steps, or operations representing a moderate or high risk of contamination from the environment should be further evaluated in the final assessment. Should contamination from the environment be a possibility, the fault tree approach shown in Figure 4.6 could be used for final assessment of adequate closure.

The final assessment addresses the needs of the process in a qualitative manner. The purpose is to determine whether it is more appropriate to close a process by upgrading the process system or to maintain status quo by leaving the operation open and housing it in an appropriately classified environment. A closure analysis risk assessment should show that most aseptic processes used in the manufacture of drug substances are closed. Exceptions may include inoculum preparation processes and seed cell expansion when shaker flasks are used. When closing the process is not possible, the operation should be housed in an appropriate environment.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

密閉分析（Closure Analysis）的本質： 密閉分析是一種聚焦於「環境與製程系統互動」的專項風險評估。它的獨特性在於：

  • 範疇刻意限縮為「環境影響」——不涉及其他製程改善
  • 目標是「移除環境的關鍵性」——降低潔淨室等級要求
  • 結果是「是否可以從 Grade X 降至 CNC」的決策依據

密閉分析三階段工作流程（Phase 1–3）：

  • Phase 1 — 製程理解: 收集 PFD（製程流程圖）和 P&ID（管道儀錶圖），定義系統邊界，識別所有穿透點。
  • Phase 2 — 風險排序: 建立密閉評估標準，對每個穿透點/操作進行風險排序，與預設可接受標準比較。
  • Phase 3 — 風險緩解: 針對「不可接受」的風險項目，評估升級選項（如改用密閉傳輸系統、增加 SIP 步驟等）。

比喻說明 Analogy

SIP 驗證 = 用蒸汽消毒管路接頭——無須拆解，現場驗證密閉性：

想像你家的天然氣管道接頭——你不會每次使用前都把接頭拆下來送去滅菌。你會在原位（in-place）用特殊方法（如壓力測試或洩漏偵測）確認接頭密封完好。SIP（就地蒸氣滅菌）的邏輯類似：生物反應器的整套管路系統，包含各個閥門、過濾器、取樣口，不需要拆解，直接在原位通入高壓蒸汽（121°C 以上，至少 15 分鐘），達到滅菌效果，同時也驗證了系統能承受蒸汽壓而不洩漏——這等於同時完成了密閉性確認。

重點提示 Key Note

SIP 後正壓維持的邏輯： SIP 完成後，系統立即切換為「無菌過濾氣體正壓維持」。這一步驟的目的是：即使系統有微小洩漏，也是氣體從內向外洩漏（正壓外洩），而不是外部環境的微粒從外向內進入。這是密閉系統的最後一道防線，也是密閉性持續保持的機制。

DO 和 pH 監測作為密閉確認的指標： 接種前的 DO（溶氧）和 pH 穩定性可以間接確認 SIP 的成功——如果培養基被微生物污染，DO 和 pH 的異常變化會在幾小時內出現。這是一個巧妙的「密閉性功能測試」，利用培養基的化學特性作為密閉成功的生物指示劑。

例外情況：搖瓶和種子準備： Vol.6 坦承，有些操作天生無法完全密閉——搖瓶（shaker flask）用於種子培養擴增時，本質上是半開放系統，仍需要 Grade 5（BSC）環境的保護。這是密閉策略的例外，不是規則。

密閉分析風險矩陣框架 Risk Matrix Framework

密閉分析風險評估邏輯：

每個穿透點 / 操作步驟 → 評估兩個維度：

1. 暴露機率 (Probability of Exposure)
   - 操作頻率
   - 操作持續時間
   - 人員介入程度

2. 暴露嚴重性 (Severity of Exposure)
   - 污染對製程的影響
   - 是否有後續去除步驟？
   - 對患者安全的影響

風險排序：
   高機率 × 高嚴重性 → 必須升級（密閉化）
   低機率 × 低嚴重性 → 可接受（維持現狀）
   中等風險 → Phase 3 評估緩解選項

最終決策：
   密閉升級 OR 保留開放 + 潔淨室環境

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 密閉分析的實際步驟（以 2,000L SS 生物反應器為例）：

  1. Phase 1: 從工程部取得 P&ID，標記所有穿透點（探針口 × 5、取樣口 × 3、加料口 × 4、通氣口 × 2、傳輸接口 × 6）共 20 個潛在暴露點。
  2. Phase 2: 對每個穿透點評估：是否有 SIP 覆蓋？是否有緊急切斷閥？是否有完整性測試記錄？
  3. Phase 3: 發現取樣口在取樣操作時（開放式取樣）為高風險 → 升級為密閉取樣系統（如 SureSampler® 或蒸汽阻障取樣閥）。
  4. 文件輸出: 產出密閉分析報告，支持將生物反應器移至 CNC 空間的監管申請（如 CMC 模組更新）。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. Fault Tree Analysis（故障樹分析）用於密閉性評估的邏輯是什麼？它與傳統 FMEA 有何不同？
  2. Vol.6 說「大多數無菌藥物原料製程應可證明是密閉的」——為什麼搖瓶種子培養是例外？有沒有技術解決方案可以消除這個例外？
  3. 一個生物反應器的「密閉分析」是否等同於 ICH Q9 的 QRM 工具應用？兩者有何異同？

4.3 操作系統開放程度與環境需求對照表

表格解讀 Table Analysis

關鍵規律 Key Pattern

從表格中可以清楚看到 Vol.6 的核心邏輯：密閉程度越高 → 所需環境等級越低。

最高風險的開放式無菌操作需要 ISO 5（A 級）；而完全密閉的系統只需要 CNC 甚至非分類空間——這之間的「環境等級跨越」，就是密閉化的商業回報。

監管一致性提示

此表格的邏輯與 EU GMP Annex 1（2022 年修訂版）的 CCS（污染控制策略）框架高度一致，也呼應 FDA 的 Process Validation Guidance 中強調「工程控制優先於環境控制」的原則。ISPE Vol.6 的「密閉優先」策略，已成為現代生物製藥設施設計的國際主流規範。

本節重點回顧 Section Summary — Chapter 4 Part A (4.1–4.4)

  • 製程密閉（Process Closure）是 ISPE Vol.6 的核心策略：將產品接觸面與環境完全解耦，使環境分類成為非關鍵參數，從而降低設施建設和維運成本。
  • 四大污染來源為：原料/耗材、環境因素（設備/空氣/人員/公用系統）、交叉污染（多產品/多批次/CIP 管路）、殘留攜帶（清洗不完全）——每一類均有對應的風險緩解策略。
  • 洋蔥式保護層次模型是本章的知識核心：每增加一層有效保護（初級圍堵 → 二級圍堵 → 建築隔離 → 環境管控），就可以降低一個等級的潔淨室要求，最終實現在 CNC 或非分類空間中安全操作密閉製程。
  • 密閉分析（Closure Analysis）是一種三階段（製程理解 → 風險排序 → 緩解選項評估）的專項風險評估工具，其最終產出是「是否可將設備移至低等級環境」的科學決策依據——必須有完整文件和驗證支撐，監管機構才會接受。
  • SIP + 正壓維持 + DO/pH 監測是確認密閉生物反應器密閉狀態的標準方法組合；密閉性驗證不能僅靠環境等級提升替代。
  • 例外情況：搖瓶種子培養等天生難以密閉的操作，仍需在 Grade 5（BSC）環境中進行——「密閉優先」是策略，但不是可以忽視科學現實的口號。
4B

Chapter 4B: Process Closure — Appropriate Environments

製程密閉—適當環境分級 | p42-p49

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol.6 (2nd Ed.): Biopharmaceutical Manufacturing Facilities | p42–p49

本章學習目標 Learning Objectives

  • 理解為什麼人員（Personnel）是開放無菌操作中最高風險的污染源，以及如何透過製程密閉性加以緩解
  • 區分「典型開放無菌操作」（如細胞庫製備、接種物製備）與「典型密閉無菌操作」（如細胞培養、過濾）的定義與例子
  • 掌握無菌過濾系統組態（串聯、並聯）的風險評估邏輯，了解冗餘過濾器的真正意義與限制
  • 理解「短暫暴露操作」（Briefly Exposed Operations，如離心、緩衝液配製）的概念，以及為何這類操作可設置於非管制區（CNC）
  • 了解稱量分裝（Weigh Dispense）操作的環境等級選擇原則，及集中稱量站設計的商業效益
  • 能夠將本節知識應用於新建生物製劑廠房的環境等級規劃，並具備向 FDA/EMA 說明的依據

本節內容架構 Section Structure

4.5 Overview 4.5.1 Open Aseptic Operations 4.5.2 Closed Aseptic Operations 4.5.2 Filtration Systems 4.5.3 Low Bioburden Operations Centrifugation — Briefly Exposed Weigh Dispense Section Summary
4.5 Appropriate Environments Based on Risk — Overview

原文內容 Original Text

Where equipment technology limits the ability to close operations, those operations will need to remain open. Personnel represent one of the highest risks as sources of bioburden and particulates. Open aseptic operations involving human intervention or manipulation, represent high risk conditions.

Closed processing can help mitigate the risk of contamination from the environment and from the "human risk factor."

When open aseptic operations are used, an appropriately controlled and maintained environment with sufficient layers of protection (e.g., Grade A/5) should be used to house the operation.

"Closed processing can help mitigate the risk of contamination from the environment and from the 'human risk factor.'"

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：製程密閉性的最終目的 Core Concept

Section 4.5 是第四章的「收割」章節——在前面幾節建立了保護層（Layers of Protection）框架之後，這裡正式回答一個關鍵問題：不同密閉程度的製程，需要什麼等級的環境？

最核心的邏輯是：製程越密閉 → 環境要求越低 → 設施成本越低。這不是取巧，而是有科學依據的風險管理決策。

人員（Personnel）被明確點名為最高風險污染源。這也解釋了為何 Grade A 環境的隔離器（Isolator）設計要把操作員完全排除在產品接觸區域之外。

比喻說明 Analogy

依照食物類型決定廚房等級：

你不會用同一個廚房標準來處理真空包裝罐頭與生魚片。罐頭食品（完全密封）可以在普通環境加工；生魚片（完全開放）需要在最嚴格的衛生環境處理。

生物製劑製程也是同樣邏輯——全密閉系統可以放在 CNC（非管制區），開放無菌操作才需要 Grade A/B 的環境保護。環境等級應該匹配製程暴露風險，而不是統一最高標準。

重點提示 Key Note

「人員風險因子」（Human Risk Factor）的重要性：即使是在 Grade B 背景下的 Grade A 層流罩，只要有人員在場操作，就引入了生物負荷（Bioburden）的潛在來源。因此，減少人員介入本身就是一種污染管控策略（CCS）的重要組成。

這也是現代設施設計趨向自動化、密閉化的根本驅動力之一。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若一個製程在技術上「可以」密閉但成本很高，而使用開放操作可以接受，此時你應該如何決策？風險評估應考慮哪些因素？
  2. 「人員是最高風險污染源」這個論述，在設施設計上帶來哪些具體的設計決策？（提示：想想 RABS vs. Isolator 的比較）
4.5.1 Example Open Aseptic Operations — 典型開放無菌操作範例

原文內容 Original Text

Examples of aseptic operations in biopharmaceutical manufacturing that are typically open include:

  • Cell bank preparation
  • Inoculum preparation

Cell Bank Preparation

The preparation of Master Cell Banks (MCBs) and Working Cell Banks (WCBs) are usually open operations. The process of selecting a clone and culturing it in preparation of the MCB, requires open manipulations that are normally performed in a Grade A/5 environment.

Inoculum Preparation

The initial stages in culture propagation may be performed in spinner flasks, shake flasks, roller bottles, or wave bags, etc. Depending on the cell bank configuration, the transfer of cryo-stored cells may be open or closed.

Following an incubation period, the contents of a seed culture container are transferred into a larger container for subsequent incubation and expansion of the culture. The opening of containers and transfer of materials are open operations and considered high risk.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：MCB/WCB 為何必須開放操作 Key Concepts

主細胞庫（Master Cell Bank, MCB）和工作細胞庫（Working Cell Bank, WCB）的製備，在技術上目前難以完全密閉，原因包括：

  • 克隆選擇（Clone Selection）需要個別培養皿的目視觀察與挑選，本質上是開放操作
  • 冷凍保存管（Cryovial）的分裝與標記需要人工操作
  • 初始接種量通常很小（µL 至 mL 級），難以用管路系統傳輸

因此，這類操作通常在 Grade A/5（Class 100）的生物安全操作台（BSC）或層流工作台（Laminar Flow Hood）下進行。

接種物製備（Inoculum Preparation）的風險分析

為什麼接種物製備是高風險操作？

  • Wave bags（搖擺式生物反應袋）雖然本身是密閉的，但接種時需要開口（除非使用無菌接頭）
  • 種子培養物（Seed Culture）從小容器移至大容器的「傳代」步驟，每次傳代都是一個潛在污染窗口
  • 傳代次數越多（Scale-up 步驟越多），累積的開放操作風險越高

行業趨勢：現代 CDMO 傾向於採用預先驗證的無菌連接件（Sterile Connectors）和一次性使用系統來「功能性密閉」這些操作，以降低環境等級要求。

比喻說明 Analogy

接種物製備就像是在實驗室培養珍貴菌種的研究員：你必須小心翼翼地打開培養皿、轉移菌落，每一次打開都是一次暴露機會。這就是為什麼這類操作需要「最乾淨的廚房」（Grade A）——因為食材本身非常脆弱且珍貴，而且操作過程不可避免地要暴露在外。

重點提示 Key Note — 監管視角

EU GMP Annex 1（2022 年版）明確要求，細胞庫製備等級需要適當的環境控制。FDA 和 EMA 在審查生物製劑 BLA/MAA 申請時，會特別審視細胞庫製備和接種物製備的環境等級選擇是否有充分的科學依據。

文件要點：你的 Site Master File（SMF）或設施設計依據（URS/FDS）應清楚說明這些操作的暴露風險評估，作為選擇 Grade A 的文件依據。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 業務情境：一家 CDMO 正在為客戶的 mAb（單株抗體）產品建立細胞庫。若採用傳統的 BSC（生物安全操作台）方式，需要 Grade B 背景 + Grade A 操作台，設施建置與維護成本較高。

替代方案：評估採用預先無菌化的一次性接種物製備系統（如 Cytiva ReadyToProcess 或 Sartorius Biostat 系列），搭配驗證的無菌接頭，可能使背景環境從 Grade B 降為 Grade D，大幅降低 HVAC 成本與環境監測頻率。

4.5.2 Examples of Closed Aseptic Operations — 典型密閉無菌操作範例

原文內容 Original Text

Set up and preparation of closed systems should be managed, validated, and monitored to confirm that system integrity is established and maintained throughout a bioprocess.

Examples of aseptic operations in biologics manufacturing that are typically closed include:

  • Cell culture and fermentation operations
  • Bulk fill
  • Harvest operations
  • Filtration steps
  • Sterile hold operations for media and buffer

Preferably bulk fill is closed, but may be open based on the final container closure needs (such as recapping).

Cell Culture and Fermentation Operations

Single use systems used in aseptic operations are received sterile (typically polyethylene based systems sterilized by gamma irradiation) at the manufacturing site. A sterilization certificate should accompany each system certifying the conditions used for sterilization. Setup and preparation of the system for use in cell culture operations should ensure that system integrity and continued isolation from the environment is maintained.

The closing of a traditional stainless steel bioreactor includes cleaning and thermal sterilization and maintenance of a positive pressure on the system post-SIP to mitigate the risk of contamination from the environment. CIP and SIP operations should be validated. Following pre-manufacturing validation, CIP and SIP operations should be monitored to ensure that the system is maintained in a validated state.

The connections of all transfer systems also should be demonstrated to be aseptic or closed. The introduction of particulates into an open bioreactor in any environment whether Grade 7, 8, or CNC is a probability; however, the risk to the manufacturing process is considered to be small following a properly executed SIP of the system.

The initial phase in an SIP sequence during heat up of the vessel includes the condensation of clean steam (equivalent to purified water) along the cool surfaces of the vessel, resulting in a rinsing of those walls. However, if this initial "rinse" of the vessel is insufficient, a WFI (or other purified water) burst prior to SIP could be performed to ensure removal of any particulates that could have settled on the product contact surfaces during the opening of the vessel. The SIP would subsequently sterilize the vessel rendering it functionally closed.

Bulk Fill

Fully integrated bulk fill – filtration systems are available. With the exception of materials that cannot be filter sterilized, it is recommended that all bulk fill operations are prepared using an integrated filter – container system. The product at this phase of the bulk drug substance manufacturing sequence normally has high value. Performing a bulk fill operation open in a Biosafety Cabinet (BSC) should be considered bad practice.

If sterile filtration is not an option for the bulk fill operation, the use of an isolator to protect the required zero bioburden (Grade A; Grade 5) processing environment is recommended.

Harvest Operations

In some processes, such as continuously harvested perfusion systems, the harvest process should be aseptic. Filtration and sedimentation technology is typically used as the cell barrier in a perfusion system. Filtration systems, centrifuges and cell settlers should be steamed in place (or single use) to functionally close the fermentation/cell culture – harvest integrated system. The integrated system should maintain its aseptic state throughout the perfusion process until final harvest at end of batch.

Sterile Buffer Hold Operations

Solutions that are not used within a short time period after formulation should be stored sterile, even if used in low bioburden non sterile operations. Sterile solutions (media and/or buffers) should be stored in sterile single use systems or in traditional stainless steel vessels that have been sterilized prior to use. Exposing solutions that are stored long term to the environment should be considered moderate to high risk, unless these solutions are bacteriostatic. Buffer hold systems should be closed and either single use or sterilizable to allow for long term storage of buffers. These systems should be closed to prevent contamination from the environment.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：密閉操作的三種實現方式

Section 4.5.2 列舉的密閉操作可以透過以下三種方式實現：

  • 完全密閉（Fully Closed）：一次性使用袋（Single-Use Bag），系統在出廠前已經 Gamma 滅菌，現場只需確認完整性後即可使用
  • 功能性密閉（Functionally Closed）：傳統不銹鋼生物反應器，透過 SIP（就地滅菌）+ 正壓維持，使系統在使用過程中「功能上等同密閉」
  • 驗證無菌連接（Validated Aseptic Connections）：使用已驗證的無菌連接器（如 ReadyMate、Lynx）在系統間傳遞物料，保持密閉狀態

比喻說明 Analogy — 功能性密閉

功能性密閉就像「每次都有滅菌保護的接口」：

想像一個高規格的水族箱系統——雖然偶爾需要打開維護（換水、清潔），但每次「打開」之後都要經過嚴格的消毒程序（SIP），讓系統重新回到無菌狀態。這種「雖有接口、但接口有保護」的設計，就是功能性密閉的精髓。

不銹鋼生物反應器的 SIP 就是這個「每次連接都有滅菌保護」的機制——SIP 完成後系統渲染為密閉，因此可以容納在非管制環境中。

重點提示：SIP 前 WFI 衝洗的重要性

原文提到一個常被忽略的細節：SIP 升溫階段，蒸汽冷凝水確實有「沖洗器壁」的作用，但不一定足夠。若生物反應器開口期間（如接種、取樣）已累積顆粒物，應考慮在 SIP 前先進行 WFI 衝洗。

這個細節在設施 SOP 中常被省略，但在 FDA 工廠視察中可能成為觀察項目，特別是對於 Grade 8 或 CNC 環境中的反應器。

重點提示：Bulk Fill 在 BSC 中操作 = Bad Practice

這是書中少見的強烈措辭。背景是：批量原液（Bulk Drug Substance, BDS）在此階段通常已是產品最終精製狀態，具有極高的商業價值（每批可能價值數百萬美元）。

在 BSC 中開放操作意味著：操作員的微生物污染風險直接暴露給最珍貴的產品，且 BSC 的保護程度遠不及密閉過濾填充系統。ISPE 的明確立場：使用整合的過濾-容器系統是業界最佳實踐，不可取巧。

灌流系統（Perfusion System）的特殊考量

灌流（Perfusion）是一種連續培養技術，特點是不斷補充培養基、同時持續收穫產品（通常是 mAb）。與批次（Batch）或饋批（Fed-Batch）不同，灌流系統的收穫過程是持續的，因此：

  • 收穫設備（離心機、過濾器）必須與培養系統完全密閉整合
  • 任何收穫步驟的密閉失效，都可能危及整個長時間運行的批次（有時長達數月）
  • Cell settler 和 ATF 過濾器的 SIP 驗證是灌流系統的關鍵要素

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 建廠決策情境：一家 CDMO 正在設計一個新的上游生物製程（Upstream Bioprocessing）廠房，包含 2000L 不銹鋼生物反應器。

如果能充分驗證 SIP 程序並維持正壓，這台生物反應器可以放在 Grade 8（ISO Class 8）甚至 CNC 環境，而不必建置在 Grade D（ISO Class 8）的潔淨室中，兩者的差異主要在 HVAC 系統的規格與維護要求。

這一個決定可以節省的成本：HVAC 系統成本差距可達 30-50%，加上後續的環境監測（EM）人力成本大幅降低。對於 5-10 台反應器的設施，累計節省可達數百萬美元。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一個 2000L 不銹鋼生物反應器，其 SIP 程序已驗證、正壓維持系統已安裝，但環境監測紀錄顯示偶爾出現細菌計數偏高。這個觀察如何影響你對其環境等級需求的判斷？
  2. Bulk fill 若因為最終容器設計（需要二次加蓋）而無法採用密閉系統，你應該選擇什麼替代方案？依據 ISPE 的建議是什麼？
4.5.2 Filtration Steps — 過濾步驟的密閉性分析

原文內容 Original Text

The assembly and setup of a filtration skid is normally an open operation. The system may be rendered closed by effective conditioning, such as flush and/or SIP as appropriate for the filtration step. The use of a 0.2 µm (absolute) or better filter may not in all instances result in the effective closing of a process.

The assembly, preparation, conditioning, and configuration of the filtration system can determine whether a filtration system is effectively isolated from the environment housing it. The aseptic integrity of a gamma irradiated single use filter can be compromised with improper setup. All process contact surfaces of a sterilizing grade filtration system should be sterile on the post filtration side of a filter element for effective closure. This also applies to steamable filtration systems. Upstream configuration of an absolute 0.2 µm filter can have little effect on the integrity of a sterile barrier (or system closure).

Example evaluation of a typical configuration of a solution sterile filtration system is shown in Figure 4.11.

Figure 4.11: Typical Configuration of a Solution Sterile Filtration System
Upstream
(Non-sterile)
⚠️ Open Zone
→
0.2 µm
Absolute Filter
(Sterile Barrier)
→
Downstream
(Sterile)
✓ Closed Zone

Yellow zone (upstream of 0.2 µm): non-sterile — HEPA environment adds little benefit
Blue zone (downstream): must remain sterile — any breach = system is open

Figure 4.11 (reconstructed): Typical Configuration of a Solution Sterile Filtration System — p44

The components of this sterile filtration system that are to the left (prior to, depicted in yellow) of the 0.2 µm absolute sterile filter are non-sterile. The activities within the yellow area are open or briefly exposed activities. Adding HEPA filtration to the yellow space to reduce the environmental bioburden and particulate levels (to Grade 7 or 8) will have little if any effect on the product quality or the ability to provide sterile media (depicted in blue).

The integrity of the closed system depicted in blue depends on the integrity of the 0.2 µm filter and all attached components to the right (downstream) of the filter element. Breach of integrity of any of these components will result in an open system that can be compromised by the environment. Validation of the integrity of the system is integral to successful closure.

The value of redundant absolute 0.2 µm filters in series in a sterile solution filtration process as depicted below should be evaluated from a risk mitigation standpoint. Manufacturers will use redundant filters in the event of failure or breach of integrity of a system. Possible reasons for failure in sterile filtration systems include:

  • Temperature or pressure excursions during SIP
  • Fouling of the filter element during the product filtration process
  • Improper installation of the filter

Post integrity testing should confirm that failure of the filter element has occurred. Re-filtration of the media or buffer or product solution may be possible. The solution may need to be discarded. Where fouling occurred in the upstream filter, removal or replacement of upstream filter may be allowable, dependent upon an organization's protocols. Where the error occurred during SIP, both absolute filter elements in the filtration system could be compromised; therefore, redundancy provides little benefit in terms of mitigation of risk.

If the filtration system fouls during operation, it is probable that the lead (upstream) filter fouled. Typically, protocol calls for replacement or removal of the lead filter. If these are positioned in series as depicted in Figure 4.12, the lead filter no longer represents the sterile barrier and is no more than a very expensive pre-filter. In addition, the SIP of the lead filter actually increases the risk of the overall operation. A more cost effective and lower risk option is to use a non-absolute 0.2 µm filter that is not steamed in place during the setup of the system.

Figure 4.12: Redundant (Series) Filter Configuration
0.2 µm
Filter 1
(Lead / SIP)
→
0.2 µm
Filter 2
(True Sterile Barrier)
→
Sterile
Product

⚠️ If SIP fails both filters → redundancy provides no benefit. Lead filter after fouling = expensive pre-filter only.

Figure 4.12 (reconstructed): Redundant Filter Configuration — Series (In-Line) — p45

An alternative is to position the filter in parallel in a lead lag configuration for true redundancy of the system as depicted in Figure 4.13.

Figure 4.13: Parallel Filters Configuration (True Redundancy)
Upstream Feed
↙        ↘
Filter A
(Active)
Filter B
(Standby)
↘        ↙
Sterile Product

True redundancy: if Filter A fails, switch to Filter B — SIP failure does not affect both simultaneously.

Figure 4.13 (reconstructed): Parallel Filters Configuration — True Lead-Lag Redundancy — p46

The different options should be evaluated for each specific operation to determine the best configuration for the application.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：無菌屏障的「方向性」

Figure 4.11 揭示了一個關鍵的思維框架：0.2 µm 過濾器是一道「單向屏障」——它只保護下游（Downstream），對上游（Upstream）的無菌狀態毫無幫助。

這個概念可以直接轉化為設施設計決策：

  • 過濾器上游的連接管路、閥門、感測器 → 不需要在無菌環境中安裝
  • 過濾器下游的所有組件 → 必須維持無菌完整性，任何一個接口的洩漏都等於打開了系統
  • 因此，提升上游區域的環境等級（如從 CNC 到 Grade 8）幾乎不帶來任何無菌保證的提升

重點提示：冗餘過濾器的邏輯陷阱

許多工廠在串聯（Series）配置中安裝兩個 0.2 µm 過濾器，認為這樣更安全。ISPE 明確指出這種邏輯的缺陷：

  • SIP 失效情境：如果 SIP 溫度/壓力超標，兩個過濾器同時受到影響 → 冗餘無效
  • 前置過濾器堵塞情境：堵塞的 Filter 1 已失去無菌屏障功能，成為「昂貴的預過濾器」，而 Filter 2 才是真正的無菌屏障 → 問題是你不知道 Filter 2 是否也有損傷
  • 安裝失誤情境：兩個過濾器都可能在同一次安裝中發生錯誤 → 冗餘同樣無效

結論：真正的冗餘需要並聯（Parallel）配置，讓兩個過濾器在不同的操作條件下承受壓力，才能提供獨立的保護。

比喻說明 Analogy

串聯 vs. 並聯冗餘過濾器 = 消防系統設計：

如果你有兩個「連在一起」（串聯）的煙霧偵測器，但它們共用同一條電源線——斷電時兩個同時失效，冗餘是假的。

真正的冗餘系統需要兩個偵測器使用獨立的電源（並聯），讓一個失效時另一個仍能正常運作。過濾器的並聯配置正是這個道理——兩條獨立的過濾路徑，分別進行 SIP，互不干擾。

過濾系統風險評估矩陣 Risk Evaluation Matrix

過濾器失效原因           串聯冗餘有效？   並聯冗餘有效？
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SIP 溫度/壓力超標         ✗ 無效          ✓ 有效
（兩個同時受影響）         （共享 SIP）     （獨立 SIP）

前置過濾器堵塞            △ 部分有效      ✓ 有效
（下游過濾器仍為屏障）      （需更換前置）   （切換備用路徑）

安裝失誤                 ✗ 可能無效      ✓ 較有效
（同次安裝）              （同時失誤）     （獨立安裝）

過濾器本身缺陷            △ 有效          ✓ 有效
（製造瑕疵）              （不太可能兩個同壞）（切換備用）
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
結論：串聯冗餘對最常見的 SIP 失效情境無效
      並聯（Lead-Lag）才是真正的冗餘設計

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一個新建廠房的工程師提議在主過濾器上游的管線區域升級為 Grade 7（ISO Class 7），認為這樣可以增加無菌保證。你如何用 Figure 4.11 的邏輯反駁這個提議？成本上的影響是什麼？
  2. 若你的工廠正在評估是否為緩衝液無菌過濾系統添加第二個 0.2 µm 串聯過濾器，你會提出哪些問題來評估這個決策的實際風險緩解效益？
4.5.3 Low Bioburden Operations/Systems — 低生物負荷操作系統

原文內容 Original Text

The risk of contamination from the environment of a bioprocess should be mitigated for systems qualified as low bioburden. Low bioburden systems that are closed do not need to be sterilized prior to use and it may not be feasible to sterilize some systems. For example, WFI distribution systems are not sterile, but are effectively closed. There is little concern of contamination from the environment of the WFI systems except at the Points Of Use (POUs) where WFI is collected or sampled. The risk of contamination from the environment at the POU can be mitigated by maintaining a constant flow and pressure on the distribution loop.

Examples of bioprocess unit operations that are usually open and typically are not (or cannot be) sterilized include:

  • Chromatography operations
  • Ultrafiltration TFF Operations
  • Virus nanofiltration operations
  • Buffer preparation
  • Media preparation
  • Centrifugation operations

Open Briefly Exposed Operations

Some open operations represent very low risk as these are transitional operations that are subsequently closed, e.g.:

  • Media preparation operations
  • Buffer preparation operations
  • Centrifugation operations

The exposure of a process solution to the environment should be brief and validated for each process. The concept of briefly exposed is depicted in Figure 4.14.

Figure 4.14: Briefly Exposed Process — 短暫暴露製程示意圖
Closed
System A
→
⚡ Brief
Open
Exposure
→
Closed
System B
(+ 0.2µm filter)

Brief exposure → closed again → downstream 0.2 µm filtration removes any acquired bioburden

Equipment in transition zone (e.g., centrifuge) can be housed in CNC environment

Figure 4.14 (reconstructed): Briefly Exposed Process — p47

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：低生物負荷 vs. 無菌的區別

低生物負荷（Low Bioburden）和無菌（Sterile）是截然不同的概念：

  • 無菌（Sterile）：理論上無任何活微生物（SAL ≤ 10⁻⁶），需要通過滅菌程序達成
  • 低生物負荷（Low Bioburden）：微生物數量受到控制（如 <10 CFU/mL），但不要求完全無菌，透過密閉+控制來維持

WFI 分配系統是最典型的例子：WFI 在藥典規格下最多允許 <10 CFU/100 mL，系統透過維持高溫循環（70°C+）或持續流動來維持低生物負荷，而非滅菌狀態。

「短暫暴露操作」（Briefly Exposed Operations）的判定標準

Figure 4.14 揭示了一個非常實用的概念框架：如果一個操作是「短暫開放，隨後重新密閉，且下游有 0.2 µm 過濾步驟」，這個操作就可以被定義為「短暫暴露操作」，其設備可以放在 CNC（非管制區）環境中。

判定三要素：

  • 暴露時間「短暫且有界定」（Brief and bounded）
  • 操作後系統重新密閉
  • 下游有滅菌級過濾步驟（0.2 µm 絕對值）作為最終屏障

比喻說明 Analogy

短暫暴露 = 隧道中的短暫開放路段：

想像一條水管，大部分是密閉的（隧道），只有一小段是開放的（橋上）——但橋的盡頭有一個「超級過濾閘門」（0.2 µm 過濾器）。任何在開放路段進入的「乘客」（微生物）都會在閘門被攔截。

因此，開放的橋段雖然有風險，但因為有後段的過濾保護，這段橋不需要建在最嚴格的環境中——用 CNC 就夠了。

重點提示：下游的哪些操作不能用這個框架？

「短暫暴露」邏輯的適用限制：

  • 如果製程串流（Process Stream）在暴露後不接受 0.2 µm 過濾（例如含有不能過濾的大分子或細胞），這個邏輯就不適用
  • 病毒奈米過濾（Virus Nanofiltration）雖然是過濾步驟，但其目的是病毒去除，而非降低生物負荷——需要分開評估
  • 色層分離（Chromatography）操作本身不是無菌的，其樹脂通常以低生物負荷狀態維護，不需要滅菌條件

實務應用 Practical Application — 下游製程廠房設計

典型下游製程操作的環境等級建議（依據 ISPE Vol.6 邏輯）：

4.5.3 Centrifugation — Briefly Exposed Operation in Practice

原文內容 Original Text

Buffer Preparation — Risk Analysis

Most buffer salts used in bioprocessing are not sterile when processed during buffer preparation. The sources of bioburden and contaminants in a buffer preparation include contamination from the environment, including contamination from operators and the contaminants present in the buffer salt package.

Risk of contamination from personnel can be mitigated by protecting the buffer salts in protected containers, such as gamma irradiated sterile bag containers. An in-line 0.2 µm process filter for the removal of bioburden and suspended contaminants from the process stream is likely to be more effective than addition of terminal HEPA filtration and over gowning of personnel in the buffer preparation suite. Upgrading the buffer preparation suite to a Grade 7 or 8 may reduce a small portion of the bioburden load in a briefly exposed buffer solution; however, the overall impact may be insignificant when compared to that of adding an in line 0.2 µm filter.

Exposure time also should be considered in a buffer preparation risk mitigation strategy. If buffers are not processed and/or stored at temperatures below 10°C (50°F) or above 50°C (122°F), or processed under other bacteriostatic conditions, exposure time can be significant. Microbial contamination can double as quickly as every 20 minutes under ideal conditions; therefore, buffers that are not consumed soon after formulation should be 0.2 µm filtered. It may be necessary to 0.2 µm filter any buffer not fully consumed within 24 hours and store the buffer in sterile containers.

Centrifugation as Briefly Exposed

Centrifugation for cell culture harvest clarification represents another example of an open operation that can be closed or briefly exposed operation. It is possible to configure a centrifuge, whether disk stack or tubular bowl for full CIP and SIP; however, centrifuges are not regularly steamed in place. A preferred approach is to combine the best of available technologies to make centrifugation a briefly exposed operation.

In the briefly exposed option, an aseptic cell culture is clarified rapidly by centrifugation. The goal of the centrifugation is to remove 95% to 98% of the turbidity (i.e., cells, cell debris, and other suspended solids) in the harvested culture. The remaining turbidity is removed by depth filtration followed by 0.2 µm filtration. If properly executed, the filtration steps render the process cell-free (thereby closed) thereby effectively isolating the process stream from the environment and from any potential bioburden that may have been present in the transition equipment.

In this scenario, the product or process stream is very briefly exposed to the transition equipment. From a process risk standpoint, the centrifuge and depth filter are analogous to a transfer pump and representing extremely low risk of contamination from the environment to the process; therefore, this equipment can be housed in a non-classified environment.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：緩衝液配製的風險緩解優先順序

ISPE 提供了一個反直覺但極其重要的結論：

加裝在線 0.2 µm 過濾器 > 升級房間等級至 Grade 7/8

為什麼？因為緩衝液中的生物負荷主要來源有兩個：

  1. 緩衝鹽本身帶入的污染（佔主要部分）
  2. 操作環境的空氣污染（暴露時間短，影響相對小）

升級房間等級只能緩解第 2 項，對第 1 項幾乎無效。但一個 0.2 µm 在線過濾器可以同時消除兩個來源的污染。

Cost-benefit 結論：把房間從 CNC 升級到 Grade 8 的成本，遠不如安裝一個 0.2 µm 過濾器。這是資源配置的最優決策。

重點提示：微生物倍增時間的實際意義

原文提到「在理想條件下，微生物每 20 分鐘可以翻倍」——這個數字有重要的實務意義：

  • 若緩衝液在配製後 2 小時才過濾，初始 1 CFU/mL 可能增長至 64 CFU/mL（2⁶）
  • 若在 4 小時後過濾，可能已達 4096 CFU/mL（2¹²）
  • 儲存在 2-8°C 可以顯著延緩倍增，但不能完全阻止生長

SOP 設計建議：緩衝液配製後應設定「最長未使用時限」（如 24 小時），超過時限必須重新過濾或廢棄。這個限制應該有微生物挑戰研究作為依據。

比喻說明 Analogy — 離心機的「短暫暴露」地位

離心機就像水管中的「彎頭」：

水從一個密閉管道（密閉培養系統）→ 流過一個彎頭（離心機）→ 進入另一個密閉管道（過濾系統）。彎頭雖然不是密閉的，但流過的時間極短，而且後段有「終端過濾閘門」（0.2 µm）。

因此，彎頭（離心機）放在哪個環境中（CNC vs. Grade D），對最終產品的無菌性幾乎沒有影響——這就是為什麼 ISPE 說這些設備可以放在非管制區。

離心機「短暫暴露」邏輯的成本影響估算

情境：一個包含 4 台碟片堆疊離心機（Disk Stack Centrifuge）
     的收穫（Harvest）廠房設計

選項 A：Grade D 潔淨室（ISO Class 8）
  建置成本：+30-50% 相較 CNC（主要是 HVAC）
  年度環境監測成本：~$50,000-100,000 USD
  年度驗證維護：~$20,000-50,000 USD

選項 B：CNC（非管制區）+ 驗證的過濾步驟
  建置成本：基準
  年度 EM 成本：~$5,000-10,000 USD（僅基本監測）
  年度驗證維護：~$5,000-10,000 USD

前提條件（選項 B 的必要依據）：
  ✓ 離心後接深層過濾（Depth Filtration）
  ✓ 深層過濾後接 0.2 µm 絕對過濾
  ✓ 暴露時間已驗證且短暫
  ✓ 離心機洗滌程序已驗證

結論：可節省設施建置成本 + 每年節省 $60,000-130,000 USD
     這是「製程密閉性」帶來的直接商業價值

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若一個 CDMO 正在評估是否將收穫（Harvest）廠房的碟片堆疊離心機從 Grade D 降為 CNC 環境，他們需要準備什麼科學依據來支持這個決定？（提示：考慮驗證要求、監管文件、過濾步驟的完整性測試）
  2. 緩衝液配製後未在 24 小時內使用（且沒有 0.2 µm 過濾），你如何處理這個偏差？這個偏差的根本原因可能是什麼？
4.5.3 Weigh Dispense Operations — 稱量分裝操作

原文內容 Original Text

Weigh Dispense

When materials arrive from suppliers, the material outer packaging and transportation materials (e.g., pallets, cardboard boxes) should be removed prior to introduction of the material into the manufacturing area to mitigate risk of contamination of the process area environment. Materials received are usually not sterile, having been manufactured in controlled or uncontrolled and unclassified environments. Powders and other non-liquid ingredients should be kept out of the manufacturing areas. These materials should be introduced into the manufacturing process via closed transfer systems. Where closed transfers are not possible, minimizing open operations is preferred.

Weigh dispensing operations should be performed in clean and controlled environments. The use of a well-designed weigh booth will both protect the ingredient during open manipulations and can protect the environment from dust or other particulates that can spread into the facility. The weigh booth should provide a Unidirectional Airflow (UDAF) HEPA filtered air supply over the weighing area and can collect stray particulates in a dust collection system. These particulates could include viable organisms and could serve as carriers for viral contaminants. The risk of these manipulations increases with increased volume and number of manipulations.

The kitting of pre-weighed materials into closed transfer systems can further mitigate the risk of particulate contamination by removing the open manipulations from the primary process areas and by providing a vehicle for the closed transfer of materials into a process system.

Centralizing the weigh dispense area is typically more cost effective and can minimize the number of areas where dust formation can occur. Locating this function in a cGMP area near the warehouse area may provide better control of the raw material inventory as partially open containers can now be stored and controlled by the warehouse specialists. The centralized weigh dispense area can serve as the warehouse – manufacturing transfer point enhancing control of incoming materials.

Additional Considerations for Solids Handling Operations

Handling large volumes in a central location can be beneficial, as risks spills and dust generation are higher. Kitting of material in closed containers for delivery to the manufacturing area is usually preferred.

A central weigh dispense next to a warehouse can provide a better method for controlling partial lots. When a raw material container is opened, it typically requires special handling and storage to prevent adulteration of product.

If raw material additions are batch dependent, there is likely a minimum threshold volume that will be required for each batch. A secondary staging area may be used to address the smaller remaining volumes that may be required in the specific batch. Options include a two stage weigh dispense function or standardization of batch sizes (possibly with discard of product) to streamline all additions.

The classification of weigh dispense areas should be consistent with the quality of the materials weighed and the quality requirements of materials prepared. Buffer salts are typically manufactured in CNC or uncontrolled unclassified environments. Quality of the buffer can be dependent on the:

  • Quality of the water (e.g., WFI ≤10 cfu/100 mL)
  • Quality of the salt
  • Time of incubation, prior to sterile filtration or prior to use

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：稱量分裝設計的三個目的

設計稱量分裝（Weigh Dispense）區域需要同時達到三個目的，這三個目的有時相互矛盾：

  1. 保護原料：防止稱量過程中環境對原料的污染
  2. 保護環境：防止粉塵（包括具有生物活性或病毒載體的微粒）擴散到生產區域
  3. 保護操作員：防止原料粉塵（特別是高效能 API）對員工健康的影響

因此，稱量台（Weigh Booth）的設計不僅是一個 GMP 問題，也是職業安全（OEL）問題。HEPA 過濾+單向氣流（UDAF）+ 粉塵收集系統是應對三個目的的核心設計。

「Kitting（套件化）」的策略價值

Kitting 是指將一批製程所需的所有原料預先稱量、分裝到密閉袋/容器中，再以密閉方式轉入生產區域。其好處包括：

  • 將所有開放稱量操作集中在一個有控制的「稱量間」，而非在多個生產區域各自稱量
  • 一次稱量、密閉包裝，在生產區域只需開袋加入系統 → 最小化生產區的開放操作
  • 批次記錄（Batch Record）更清晰，每個批次的 Kit 對應到一個批號，可追溯性更強

比喻說明 Analogy

集中稱量站 = 超市的預先包裝區：

超市不會讓顧客自己去倉庫切牛肉——而是在有控制的後台預先包裝好，顧客只需取走密封包裝。

集中稱量站對 CDMO 的意義也一樣：原料在有 HEPA 防護的稱量間完成「預先包裝」，生產操作員只需取走密封的 Kit，最大限度減少生產區的粉塵暴露與開放操作。

重點提示：稱量區分級依據材料的最終用途

原文強調：稱量區的環境等級應與被稱量材料的品質需求一致，而不是統一最高標準。

實務上的分級原則：

  • 緩衝鹽（Buffer Salts）：通常在 CNC 或非管制環境稱量即可，因為後段有 0.2 µm 過濾
  • 培養基（Media）成分：需要考慮後段是否有滅菌步驟，若有則 CNC 可以接受
  • 直接添加到無菌系統的原料：需要更高等級的保護（Grade D 或以上）

關鍵因素：水的品質 + 鹽的品質 + 配製後存放時間共同決定最終緩衝液的品質，環境等級只是其中一個（且通常不是最重要的）因素。

集中稱量站的成本-效益框架

分散式稱量（每個生產區域各有稱量台）：
  - 多個區域都有粉塵風險 → 多處環境監測需求
  - 部分用量的原料需要多點存放 → 庫存管理複雜
  - 每個稱量台需要各自維護和驗證
  - 生產員工需要接受稱量操作訓練

集中式稱量站（Centralized Weigh Dispense）：
  - 僅一個高規格稱量間需要建置和維護
  - 庫存集中在倉庫旁 → 部分用量管理更容易
  - 只需培訓少數專職稱量員工
  - 生產區域只接收密封 Kit → 降低生產區複雜性

位置建議：緊鄰倉庫（Warehouse）
理由：
  1. 原料不必穿越生產區才能到稱量站
  2. 未用完的開封容器可以立即回到倉庫控制
  3. 作為「倉庫-生產」的物料轉移控制點

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一家 CDMO 正在設計新的 DSP（下游製程）廠房。他們需要為緩衝液配製建立稱量區。根據 ISPE Vol.6 的邏輯，稱量區的環境等級應該是什麼？你需要哪些文件來支持這個決定？
  2. 若緩衝鹽的 Kitting 操作後，Kit 需要在生產區域存放 3 天才被使用。這對稱量台設計（密封要求）和生產區域管理有什麼影響？
綜合風險矩陣 Comprehensive Risk-Based Environment Matrix (Section 4.5 Summary)

以下矩陣彙整 Section 4.5 中所有操作類別的環境等級建議，可作為設施設計和監管申請的快速參考。This matrix consolidates the environment grade recommendations from Section 4.5 for all operation categories.

* 所有等級選擇均需有書面的風險評估（Risk Assessment）作為依據，並記錄在設施設計文件（如 FDS, URS）中，以備 FDA/EMA 審查。

本節重點回顧 Section 4.5 Summary

  • 人員是最高風險：開放無菌操作中，人員（Personnel）是主要的生物負荷和微粒污染來源；製程密閉性是緩解「人員風險因子」的核心策略
  • 開放 vs. 密閉的典型例子：MCB/WCB 製備、接種物製備屬於必要的開放操作，需要 Grade A/B 環境；細胞培養、收穫、過濾、緩衝液儲存屬於可密閉操作，可放置在較低等級甚至 CNC 環境
  • 0.2 µm 過濾器是「方向性屏障」：它只保護下游（Downstream），升級上游環境等級對無菌保證幾乎沒有貢獻——這是設施設計中常見的資源浪費點
  • 冗餘過濾器需要並聯（不是串聯）：串聯冗餘在 SIP 失效情境下提供的保護很有限；並聯（Lead-Lag）配置才能提供真正的冗餘保護
  • 「短暫暴露操作」（Briefly Exposed）可放在 CNC：離心機、緩衝液配製等操作，只要暴露時間短且下游有 0.2 µm 過濾，可以放置在非管制區，顯著節省設施成本
  • 緩衝液配製：在線過濾 > 升級房間等級：安裝 0.2 µm 在線過濾器的效益遠大於將緩衝液配製間升級為 Grade 7/8——這是資源配置的最優決策
  • 集中稱量站設計：將稱量操作集中、靠近倉庫，提供 UDAF+HEPA+粉塵收集，配合 Kitting 策略，可以最小化生產區的開放操作和環境管制需求
  • 文件化是關鍵：所有環境等級的降低決策，都需要有書面的風險評估和科學依據，以備 FDA/EMA 審查——這是將技術邏輯轉化為監管認可的必要步驟
5

Chapter 5: Operations

操作 | p49-p61

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol.6 (2nd Ed.): Biopharmaceutical Manufacturing Facilities | p49 – p61

本章學習目標

  • 理解多產品 (Multi-product) 廠房的分時與分空間策略，說明分批次連續生產 (Campaign manufacturing) 與並行生產 (Concurrent production) 的差異及清潔驗證要求。
  • 掌握一次性使用系統 (Single-Use Systems, SUS) 的設計優勢（免 CIP/SIP、較小廠房足跡）與風險（供應鏈依賴、可萃取物與可滲出物 E&L）。
  • 分析密閉系統 (Closed systems) 與開放系統 (Open systems) 對環境分類、著裝要求、清潔計畫及人員編制的影響。
  • 了解自動化 (Automation)、製造執行系統 (MES)、程序標準化與操作員訓練如何提升生物製藥廠的一致性與合規性。
  • 評估產能 (Capacity)、排程 (Scheduling)、可維護性及供應鏈策略對生物製藥設施整體績效的影響。
5.1 Introduction｜導言

原文內容 Original Text

This chapter addresses the operational aspects of a biopharmaceutical facility and the impact of facility and equipment design decisions on manufacturing operations. Conversely, this chapter also describes how operability and maintainability considerations should influence the design of the facility.

Newer or updated facilities may enable more closed processing and less physical segregation. In conjunction with higher titers and smaller markets, allowing for increased use of single use systems with less cleaning and SIP. This can result in lower production labor requirements.

For information on segregation and flows, see Chapters 5 and 6 of this Guide.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Operability（可操作性）：設備與廠房是否能讓操作員安全、有效率地執行日常製造工作。

Maintainability（可維護性）：設備是否容易進行預防性保養、校正與零件更換，而不需要長時間停機。

本章的核心命題是「雙向影響」：設計影響操作，操作需求也應在設計階段反映。這是 ISPE 強調「早期介入 (Early Involvement)」的具體體現。

比喻說明 Analogy

廠房設計就像蓋廚房——如果設計時沒考慮廚師的動線和設備維修需求，廚師每天工作都會卡關。本章就是要確保「蓋廚房時，廚師有參與設計討論」。

重點提示 Key Notes

更高效價 (Higher titers) 意味著同樣的藥量可以用更小的生物反應器生產，這是一次性使用系統 (SUS) 擴大應用的關鍵驅動力。小批量製程更適合 SUS，大批量製程仍以傳統不鏽鋼設備為主。

5.2 Multiple Product Operations｜多產品操作

原文內容 Original Text

Multiple product operations require product separation either on a time (campaigned operations) or space (concurrent operations) basis through engineering design and procedures. Facilities may be required to run several campaigned or concurrent products.

Campaigned Product Operation

A campaigned product operation separation is based on time (producing one product at a time in a single space). For campaigned products, prevention of cross-contamination through cleaning validation, changeover procedures, and clearance between product runs should be demonstrated.

Clearance should be demonstrated by removal of product, components, and waste residues from process equipment. Clearance procedures should be appropriately tested to ensure compliance with regulatory expectations. Cleaning endpoints should be established using scientific reasoning. Dedicated equipment may be used.

Concurrent Product Operations

Concurrent product operations can be performed using spatial segregation to prevent product cross-contamination. A single product (dedicated facility) is an example of spatial segregation. These operations are usually used in non-product specific activities, such as media preparation or buffer preparation. They also can be used for product specific steps when closed systems are demonstrated. Concurrent production focuses on physical segregation (i.e., using closed systems) and procedural control to ensure the quality and safety of the products produced.

Campaigned production requires the ability to perform quick changeovers. Concurrent production of different products requires the ability to demonstrate an acceptable risk of crossover of one product to another.

The use of closed systems can minimize the risk of release of product fluids into the room environment during operation. Closed systems also reduce the risk of contamination via exposure of product to the external environment. This concept allows for side by side concurrent production of multiple products, e.g., for cell culture bioreactor spaces.

Where open operations are necessary, such as in seed preparation, BSCs within seed preparation suites can be used. In general, these operations are limited to a single product in a single room at one time. A risk assessment may be performed to determine when multi-product operations within separate BSCs can occur in the same room at the same time.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Campaign Manufacturing（分批次連續生產）：在同一空間，不同時間生產不同產品。換產前須完成清潔驗證 (Cleaning Validation) 並確認殘留物符合可接受限度。

Concurrent Production（並行生產）：在同一時間，不同空間（或密閉系統內）同時生產不同產品。依賴物理隔離 (Physical Segregation) 或程序管控 (Procedural Control)。

BSC（Biological Safety Cabinet，生物安全櫃）：開放製程中保護產品與操作員的局部隔離設備，常用於種源培養 (Seed Preparation) 等開放步驟。

比喻說明 Analogy

Campaign 製造 = 餐廳預訂制（一次只做一批）：早上做法式料理，下午打掃廚房、換餐具，晚上做日式料理——每次切換都需要徹底清潔，否則前一批的殘留（交叉污染）會影響下一批。

Concurrent 生產 = 用不同鍋子同時煮多道菜：不同產品在物理隔離的密閉容器裡同時運行，互不干擾——前提是密封性要足夠好。

重點提示 Key Notes

清潔驗證 (Cleaning Validation) 是 Campaign 製造的核心合規要求：需科學建立清潔終點 (Cleaning Endpoint)，並驗證殘留物（前產品、清潔劑、微生物）均低於可接受限度。彈性體（橡膠墊圈 Gaskets、軟管 Hoses、隔膜 Diaphragms）需特別關注，因為它們可能吸附並釋放殘留物。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您的 CDMO 廠房同時承接三個客戶的生物製藥產品，您會建議採用 Campaign 模式還是 Concurrent 模式？請說明理由和所需的技術條件。
  2. Campaign 製造中，「Clearance（殘留清除）」的法規要求具體包含哪些面向？只檢測不鏽鋼表面殘留是否足夠？

原文內容 Original Text (continued)

Multiple product operations require a facility to be flexible to allow for easy and quick changeover to new product processes or changes in product demand. Strategic approaches or levels of decisions to deliver flexibility include:

  1. Expandability: allows for future growth to incorporate changes, e.g., saving space to allow for building expansion. In the short term, this may be the least expensive option, while allowing for plans to deliver changes in demand or process changes.
  2. Adaptability: provides some pre-investment for future needs, e.g., shell space, local building services in the general area possibly with a valved service tie-in point. This allows for future modifications while reducing the effect on current operations.
  3. Flexibility: can provide utility connections to the planned location of new or modified equipment. This is the most costly and requires clarification of future needs.

Organizations may use platform processes for similar types of products to minimize changes required for new product changeover. Downtime consumed during changeovers reduces the operational time available to generate product. When running many short campaigns the changeover downtime can significantly reduce total throughput of a facility.

Automation changes required to bring a new product into a facility can be time consuming. Changeover to new product processes can be aided by the use of batch programming standards and recipe management strategies. Hard coded changes should be documented and re-qualified. Simple recipe changes can be verified.

Product changeover requires documented confirmation that residual product inside process equipment is removed and does not contaminate the subsequent product beyond acceptable limits. Cleaning validation strategies should include a rationale for the change-out of elastomers (gaskets, diaphragms, hoses) as part of product changeover.

Single use systems can eliminate the issue of lot to lot carryover. There is still a potential for crossover contamination; however, the components should be handled properly during system breakdown to avoid spillage post operation.

5.2.1 Clinical Trial Manufacturing

Clinical trial manufacture may require an early facility design and investment decision before having complete knowledge of a product or process. A step-wise incremental approach to GMP compliance, based on the stage of product development, may be used.

The level of process validation at each processing stage should be considered, particularly for the steps that have the greatest impact on product quality and consistency.

Clinical trial manufacturing can be more flexible and manual with more extensive process instrumentation and data collection to allow for the increasing knowledge of the product process during product development. Extensive in-process testing should be used to collect additional information and to help to ensure acceptable product quality.

During product development, change management systems should be used to manage changes that affect the facility.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：三層彈性策略

ISPE 將廠房彈性由低到高分為三層：

  • Expandability（擴充性）：現在省錢，預留未來擴建空間。最便宜。
  • Adaptability（調適性）：預留 shell space（空殼空間）與公用設施接口，改建時影響較小。
  • Flexibility（靈活性）：已佈設好公用管線到每個預計位置，可即插即用。最貴，但換產最快。

CDMO 因需頻繁換產，通常傾向採用 Flexibility 設計；新創 Biotech 早期臨床廠則可先採 Expandability，節省資本支出。

Platform Process（平台製程）的商業價值

生物製藥企業（尤其 mAb 廠商）建立標準化 Platform Process，讓新產品能快速套用既有的上游培養條件、下游純化步驟和清潔驗證方法。這大幅縮短換產時間與驗證成本，是 CDMO 接案效率的關鍵競爭優勢。

比喻說明 Analogy

Recipe Management = 餐廳的菜單系統：自動化系統只需「換一份食譜」就能切換產品，不需要重新寫整套程式——大幅降低換產的軟體確效 (Qualification) 工作量。

臨床試驗製造的特殊考量

臨床階段廠房設計面臨「先有雞還是先有蛋」的困境：製程知識尚不完整，但 FDA/EMA 要求必須在 GMP 條件下生產臨床用樣品。解法是採用「分階段 GMP 合規 (Step-wise GMP compliance)」——早期臨床允許較多人工操作和彈性，隨製程知識累積逐步強化管控。

實務應用 Practical Application

一家 CDMO 正在評估是否接受一個新的 mAb 臨床一期案子。客戶的製程資料尚未完整確立，但希望 6 個月後就開始生產。ISPE 的建議是：在廠房設計上採用 Adaptability 策略，在 GMP 合規上採用 Step-wise 方法，同時建立嚴格的 Change Management 系統以追蹤製程變更對產品品質的影響。

5.3 Single Use Systems｜一次性使用系統

原文內容 Original Text

New products produced at higher titers can be run at smaller scale to satisfy market demands. This has allowed for increased use of single use systems. This impacts on facility design by reducing or eliminating the need for CIP and SIP operations. It also can substantially reduce the demand for water and the volume of liquid waste.

Considerations for single use systems include:

  • Cost (purchase, transport, storage, setup, disposal)
  • Dependence on single sourced approved suppliers
  • Leachables and extractables

Facility design factors for single use systems include:

  • Compliant inventory management
  • Receipt, inspection, and release storage space
  • Availability of pre-use release testing

A bar coding system can be used to manage inventory.

When single use system components are contaminated with product solutions, they can be considered bio-hazardous waste. Proper post-use disposal should be considered and these systems may be incinerated to:

  • Address the biohazard concerns
  • Minimize risk of liability
  • Benefit from the fuel value of the plastic

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Single-Use System, SUS（一次性使用系統）：由一次性塑膠材料（袋子、管路、接頭、生物反應器內膽等）組成的製程系統。每批次使用後即拋棄，不需要清洗 (CIP) 或滅菌 (SIP)。

Extractables & Leachables, E&L（可萃取物與可滲出物）：塑膠材料中的化學物質可能在特定條件下（高溫、有機溶劑）遷移（Extractables）或在正常製程條件下逐漸滲出（Leachables）到藥品中，影響安全性。需根據 USP <661>、ISO 10993 等標準進行測試。

比喻說明 Analogy

SUS = 免洗餐具 vs. 瓷器：傳統不鏽鋼設備像高檔瓷器——每次用完要徹底清洗消毒，耗時費力；一次性使用系統像免洗餐具——用完即丟，省去清洗步驟，但有塑膠材料安全性（E&L）和廢棄物處理的顧慮。

重點提示 Key Notes

SUS 的供應鏈風險是最被低估的風險之一：許多關鍵 SUS 組件（尤其是特定尺寸的生物反應器袋）僅有 1-2 家供應商，一旦供應中斷（如 COVID-19 期間發生的情況）可能導致整個生產線停頓。ISPE 和 FDA 均建議製造商建立供應鏈風險評估 (Supply Chain Risk Assessment) 和備用供應商認證計畫。

廢棄物處理的法規面：接觸過生物製品（尤其是含活性病毒的疫苗製程）的 SUS 廢棄物屬生物危害廢棄物 (Biohazardous Waste)，必須經過高壓滅菌或焚化處理，不能直接進入一般廢棄物流。

SUS vs. 傳統設備 TCO 比較框架

傳統不鏽鋼設備成本 =
  資本支出 (CapEx)
  + CIP/SIP 系統建置與驗證
  + 純化水 / WFI 用量
  + 清潔驗證（跨批次）
  + 定期更換密封件

一次性使用系統成本 =
  每批 SUS 耗材採購價
  + 儲存空間與庫存管理
  + 生物危害廢棄物處理費
  + E&L 測試費用
  + 供應鏈風險備用金

關鍵：批次規模越小，SUS TCO 優勢越明顯
      批次規模越大（>2000L），傳統設備 TCO 反而較低

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. E&L（可萃取物與可滲出物）測試的重點是什麼？製造商應在哪個開發階段開始評估 SUS 的 E&L 風險？
  2. 如果您的 SUS 袋唯一供應商突然宣布停產，您的 CDMO 應如何應對？有哪些預防措施可以在設計階段就納入？
5.4 Impact of Closed and Open Systems on Operations｜密閉與開放系統對操作的影響

原文內容 Original Text

According to Good Engineering Practice (GEP), process systems should be kept closed, where possible, to avoid exposing products to the room environment. For some biopharmaceutical products (e.g., viral vaccines or live viruses), closed systems also protect operators from exposure to these products.

Where it is not possible to demonstrate that a process system is closed, environmental controls such as room classifications, local ventilation, and higher gowning practices should be used.

It is usually easier to design a well-understood, robust process system into a closed system:

  • Early stage development or clinical trial supply processes are usually less developed, less characterized and are more often open.
  • Early upstream processes (pre-bioreactor) are usually open and run under BSCs. Using single use systems and plastic weldable connections may allow these processes to be closed.
  • Upstream processes run in bioreactors usually require containment to avoid contamination and are usually closed.
  • Downstream processes have made progress toward closed designs (e.g., by using on-line analytical devices which allow for real time mainstream collection).

When closed systems are used, the arrangement and access to processing systems and areas can be simplified. Closed upstream systems may be located in the same room as closed downstream systems. Airlocks may not be required and can reduce the footprint needed to accommodate operations. Using single use systems can reduce the clean space footprint that requires stringent housekeeping procedures:

  • Closed processing systems allow use of less stringent area environments (CNC) which can reduce capital costs and operating costs associated with cleaning, environmental monitoring, and gowning. There is also a reduction in time required to gown in and out.
  • Where upstream and downstream systems are located in the same room, operators can manage both systems. Staffing levels may be reduced significantly (as high as 50% with proper cross training) when closed systems are combined with suitable automation.
  • Closed processing systems can reduce downtime required for product changeover, as room clearance is not required before the next product is introduced.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Closed System（密閉系統）：製程液體與外部環境完全隔絕，不需要依賴房間分類 (Room Classification) 提供保護。密閉系統是自身的一級圍堵 (Primary Containment)。

CNC（Controlled but Not Classified，受控非分類區）：相較於 ISO 5/7/8 潔淨室，CNC 只需基本環境管控（如 HEPA 過濾、正壓），無嚴格微粒和微生物限度要求，建設和運行成本顯著較低。

Plastic Weldable Connections（塑膠焊接接口）：透過熱焊接方式連接 SUS 管路，避免開放性連接操作，是將原本開放的製程步驟轉為密閉的關鍵技術。

重點提示 Key Notes

密閉系統帶來的「50% 人員節省」是驚人的商業影響：密閉系統 + 自動化允許上下游操作員在同一空間作業，搭配適當的交叉培訓 (Cross-training)，人員需求可降低高達 50%。這對 CDMO 而言直接影響報價競爭力和運營成本。

下游 (Downstream) 密閉化是當前的技術趨勢：傳統層析 (Chromatography) 操作有許多開放連接點，但在線分析儀器 (On-line analytical devices) 和自動收集閥 (Automated fraction collection) 的進步正在使下游製程逐步走向密閉化。

比喻說明 Analogy

密閉系統 = 完全密封的食品加工線：牛奶從牧場到利樂包，全程密封管路輸送——不需要「潔淨廠房」，因為產品本身就被密封保護著。但如果某個環節需要打開（如取樣），就必須立刻在嚴格環境下操作。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 廠房設計評估：一個新的 mAb 製造設施，若採用全密閉系統設計，可以將潔淨室面積從 2000 m² 降至 800 m²（其餘使用 CNC），同時減少環境監測點位約 60%，人員配置降低 40%。這些節省在 20 年 TCO 中可達數千萬美元，是 ISPE 密閉化設計的核心商業論據。

5.4.1 Closure｜密閉性

原文內容 Original Text

Open processing requires physical segregation and appropriate control of the processing environment. For further information on classified spaces and physical segregation, see Chapter 6 of this Guide.

For closed systems, closure is provided by process equipment. Each closed system acts as the primary containment for its contents. Other closed systems then act as a second level of protection against contamination; two closed systems need to fail for the contamination to occur. Definition of what constitutes a breech, consequences of the breech, and the required actions to re-establish closure should be considered. Procedures to address breech of closure should be established.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：雙重失效保護

密閉系統的安全邏輯：要發生污染，需要兩個密閉系統同時失效。這與 EU GMP Annex 1 的「污染控制策略 (CCS)」哲學一致——多重屏障 (Multiple Barriers) 提供冗餘保護。

Breach of Closure（密閉失效）：任何導致密閉系統完整性被破壞的事件（如管路脫落、接頭漏液）。必須有書面 SOP 規範：如何識別、如何上報、如何評估影響、如何重新建立密閉性。

重點提示 Key Notes

「Breach of Closure SOP」是 FDA 和 EMA 查廠時的常見查核項目。若廠房宣稱使用密閉系統來降低房間分類要求（如採用 CNC），則必須能夠證明密閉失效的應對程序是充分的且已被演練過。

5.4.2 Cleaning and Housekeeping｜清潔與環境整潔

原文內容 Original Text

Housekeeping is considered an indicator of the quality of an operation. Processing spaces should be well organized. Specific housekeeping practices should match the risk to the product and the classification of the space. Classified spaces require frequent cleaning with potent cleaning agents to ensure compliance to classified space definitions. An environmental monitoring program should be established to assess the effectiveness of the area cleaning practices.

CNC can use reduced cleaning regimens. For further information, see the ISPE Baseline Guide on Risk-MaPP.

Suitable cleaning and housekeeping amenities should be considered, e.g.:

  • Refuse disposal points
  • Handling and storage space for cleaning supplies and equipment
  • Access to appropriate water for facility cleaning

In multi-product facilities, cleaning practices should help to prevent cross-contamination. Facility materials should be compatible with common cleaning agents.

Access to production areas should be suitably controlled.

Biopharmaceutical facilities generally do not need fumigation when processes can be demonstrated as contained. Decisions on fumigation should be based on an appropriate risk assessment.

Pest control programs are normally required by regulations. Raw materials used in biopharmaceutical processing, such as media components or sugars, can be subject to contamination by pests. Tight-sealing, self-closing doors, sticky mats, and UV lights at key facility entry points should be considered. SOPs should be established for the use of suitable rodenticides, insecticides, and fungicides.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Risk-MaPP（Risk-based Manufacture of Pharmaceutical Products）：ISPE 指南，提供基於風險評估的多產品設施設計和操作框架，特別針對高活性藥物 (Highly Potent APIs) 的清潔驗證和人員保護。

清潔計畫的強度應與產品風險和空間分類相稱。CNC 空間的清潔要求顯著低於 ISO 7/8 潔淨室，這是密閉系統設計節省成本的重要來源之一。

重點提示 Key Notes

生物製藥廠的病蟲害管制 (Pest Control) 常被忽視，但實際上是法規要求。培養基成分（糖類、胺基酸）本身就是害蟲吸引物。FDA 483 觀察報告中，廠房曾因在生產區發現昆蟲而被發出 483 不合格項。

材料兼容性 (Material Compatibility)：廠房表面材料（牆面、地板、設備外殼）必須與常用清潔劑（如次氯酸鈉、過氧化氫）相容，不得在清潔過程中腐蝕或產生顆粒。

比喻說明 Analogy

整潔度 = 廠房品質文化的鏡子：FDA 查廠員在正式檢查前，往往先觀察廠房的整體整潔程度。一個雜亂的走廊或標識不清的廢棄物桶，可能比任何文件問題更早引起查廠員的注意。「Housekeeping is considered an indicator of the quality of an operation」——這句話是法規查廠的潛台詞。

5.4.3 Gowning｜著裝要求

原文內容 Original Text

Gowning practices should match the room classification and HVAC design capabilities. HVAC design criteria should match product and process requirements, and could be affected by the number of operators required in selected spaces.

For example, gowning practices generally have a greater impact on CNC spaces with monitoring or microbial limits than CNC spaces with no monitoring. The higher the room classification, the greater the impact gowning has on meeting environmental acceptance criteria.

In classified spaces, jumpsuits are typically used with hair nets, shoe covers or facility dedicated shoes, gloves, and face masks at the highest area classifications. Where engineering controls cannot be employed to reduce personal risk adequately, organizations should ensure that appropriate personal protective equipment (PPE) is used, e.g.:

  • Safety glasses
  • Safety shoes
  • Goggles and/or face shields
  • Protective gloves
  • Respirators

Closed systems allow for relaxed gowning practices, e.g., use of laboratory coats or scrubs as a worker uniform to enhance operator comfort. Gloves, shoe covers, or dedicated facility shoes and hair nets may be worn.

Organizations may require disrobing before gowning. This may contribute to improved comfort while gowned (less layers of clothing) and adds another level of disconnection between open production environments and the environment outside.

Costs associated with high levels of gowning include:

  • Investment in airlocks, changing spaces, and the gowning materials
  • Time spent performing the gown in and out procedures
  • Higher cooling demand for operator comfort
  • Performance issues working while gowned

Working in traditional production environments (heavily gowned in a white box) can result in fatigue and stress. Facilities should be designed to allow operators to spend the minimum time in processing areas, e.g.:

  • Processing terminals (HMIs) can be located in adjacent production administrative spaces, allowing operators to enter the processing areas only when needed for set up or sampling.
  • Full glass views can be provided into processing areas from adjacent production administrative spaces.
  • The proper use of controls can assist in minimizing the amount of time operators need to supervise production equipment.
  • Daylight and/or an outside view into the processing areas or adjacent non-classified support space can be provided.
"Figure 5.1: Non-Classified Production Support Space Adjacent to Production Operations — Used with permission from Novo Nordisk and NNE Pharmaplan."
"Figure 5.2: Maximum Use of Viewing Windows to Reduce Need to Enter Production Areas — Used with permission from Novo Nordisk and NNE Pharmaplan."

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：著裝等級與空間分類的關聯

比喻說明 Analogy

著裝 = 手術衣 vs. 廚師服：在全密閉製程中，操作員穿著廚師服（實驗室外套）即可安全工作；但在開放製程中（如無菌充填），必須穿戴全套「手術衣」——舒適度差，疲勞感高，長期下來對工作品質和人員健康均有影響。

HMI 移至隔壁行政區 = 有倒車雷達的車：司機不必下車就能了解後方狀況——操作員不必進入潔淨室就能監控製程狀態，大幅減少著裝/卸裝的時間成本。

重點提示 Key Notes

著裝要求的隱性成本常被低估：一個操作員每天著裝/卸裝可能消耗 30-60 分鐘，在多班制運作的生物製藥廠，每年累積的人時成本相當可觀。此外，高溫潔淨室環境下的疲勞效應也是 FDA 觀察到的人為錯誤 (Human Error) 重要來源之一。

亞太地區的特殊著裝文化：中國和日本部分地區要求設置獨立的脫鞋室 (Shoe removal room) 和風淋室 (Air shower)，這些設施需要在廠房設計時提前規劃，否則事後改裝成本極高。

圖表解讀 Figure Analysis

Figure 5.1 & 5.2（Novo Nordisk / NNE Pharmaplan 案例）：這兩張圖展示了現代生物製藥廠的最佳實踐設計——在生產區外側配置非分類的行政支持空間（配備 HMI 終端機），操作員可透過大型觀察窗監視製程，只在需要時才進入生產區。這種設計將潔淨室暴露時間降至最低，同時透過充足採光和視野改善操作員的工作環境品質。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果廠房設計選擇將 HMI 終端機移至非分類行政區，需要對哪些 GMP 系統進行額外的設計考量（如 21 CFR Part 11 電子記錄、網路安全等）？
  2. 著裝等級對環境監測 (Environmental Monitoring) 計畫有何影響？CNC 空間和 ISO 7 空間的採樣頻率和限度設定有何不同？
5.5 Automation, Procedures, and Training｜自動化、程序與訓練

原文內容 Original Text

Traditional facilities which needed to fully integrate and coordinate CIP and SIP operations used supervisory controls. The plug and play nature of recent facility designs focuses control on unit operations. These systems allow for process engineers and automation engineers to work with users to develop and implement appropriate process automation controls.

5.5.1 Impact of Automation

An increased use of automation should be driven by quality and safety improvements, e.g.:

  • Automation drives consistency of processing actions — things are done at the same pace and in the same order.
  • Automation allows for data input verification checks to ensure the entry is within expected ranges. Actions can be prevented when interlocks are not satisfied.
  • Control systems can collect and organize data into records to improve the ability to monitor processes and to evaluate performance with a goal to achieve incremental improvements.

Cost saving opportunities are provided through: faster operations, more predictable actions, less failed lots due to non-conformance to required procedures, lower production staffing levels.

Increased data collection and analysis provides an opportunity for demonstrating product quality through process controls. Statistical tools can help to monitor process performance and can aid in process decisions. Alert and action levels should be justified and established for key process indicators and critical process parameters.

Automation can be used to support the claim of closure and to maintain system closure. System specific interlocks may be used to ensure the isolation of closed systems and that a closed environment is effective until (and unless) it is intended to breach closure.

Integration controls can be used to ensure that two closed systems are not inappropriately connected to each other or to the same service. For example, two systems connected simultaneously to a CIP system; therefore, facilitating a cross connection between the systems.

Automation usually increases the need for detailed knowledge of process operations at an earlier stage in the design of a facility. Increased use of batch programming standards and recipe management tools can expand the flexibility of automation controls, and decrease the costs and time to execute changes to automation software.

Cleanability

Cleanability should be considered when locating computer screens and stations in classified spaces. Units should be sealed to allow for appropriate space cleaning practices. Sealed units may prevent the proper removal of heat generated by the enclosed electronics.

Wireless Connectivity

Wireless connectivity may help in the collection of processing data and in facilitating the addition of plug and play portable equipment into facilities. Tablet type hand-held devices may improve efficiencies and timeliness of operations, such as data entry or confirmation of actions, e.g., material additions or status of equipment using barcode labels.

Manufacturing Execution Systems

A Manufacturing Execution System (MES) can be used to oversee the local manufacturing operation. Supervisory Control and Data Acquisition (SCADA) / Process Analytical Technology (PAT) can be used to control and monitor the process at the skid level. The documentation of the process sequence via time date stamps can reduce the need for quality checks, allowing for faster release of completed batch records and lots of material by focusing on review by exception. MES can serve as the verification function, allowing quicker operations and reducing staffing requirements.

Scanning a material label before completing an addition operation can ensure that material is through its release process and is not expired. Scanning an operator badge could confirm that an operator's training to perform a task is current. Scanning an equipment label can confirm the equipment is within its cleaning window and any required maintenance has been performed. These functions can reduce the probability of a rejected lot.

Process Analytical Technology

Process analytical technology, used to provide live operational data, is becoming more available and useful, e.g., improved understanding of bioreactor operations and tools to collect monitoring data. This information can be used to speed decisions and to increase the consistency of process streams. PAT provides continuous monitoring and control of processes which demonstrates the quality of the product produced. When PAT is used during product development stages, it can aid in earlier and greater process knowledge, improved regulatory submissions, and simplify technology transfer to clinical and commercial operations.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

DCS/SCADA（分散式控制系統／監控與數據採集系統）：負責設備層級的即時製程控制（溫度、壓力、流量）。

MES（Manufacturing Execution System，製造執行系統）：負責批次層級的操作管理，包含電子批次記錄 (EBR)、物料追蹤、人員培訓核查、設備狀態確認。

PAT（Process Analytical Technology，製程分析技術）：即時監測關鍵製程屬性（如細胞濃度、溶氧、pH），使製程決策從「事後檢驗」轉為「即時調整」，符合 FDA PAT Guidance (2004) 和 ICH Q8 的 QbD 精神。

21 CFR Part 11：美國 FDA 法規，規範電子記錄與電子簽名的合規要求。MES 和 EBR 系統必須符合 Part 11 要求，包括稽核軌跡 (Audit Trail)、版本控制和存取權限管理。

比喻說明 Analogy

MES = 餐廳的 POS 系統（訂單管理系統）：服務員掃描食材條碼確認庫存，廚房按標準流程出餐，系統自動記錄每道菜的製作時間和用料——電子批次記錄 (EBR) 就是生物製藥廠的「數位出菜單」，取代傳統的紙本記錄，讓品保 (QA) 審核從逐行核對變成「例外審查 (Review by Exception)」。

Interlocks（連鎖機制）= 汽車的安全帶感知器：沒繫安全帶車就不能發動——製程中若某個前置條件未滿足（如清潔窗口過期），系統自動阻止下一步操作，防止人為疏失。

重點提示 Key Notes

「Review by Exception（例外審查）」是 MES/EBR 帶來的最重要 QA 效率提升：傳統紙本批次記錄需要 QA 人員逐行核對每一筆數據；EBR 系統在製程中即時驗證，只有超出範圍的數據才需要人工審查。這可將批次記錄審核時間縮短 50-70%，對 CDMO 的批次放行週期 (Lot Release Cycle Time) 有顯著影響。

密閉系統的 Interlock 設計是合規關鍵：宣稱密閉系統的廠房，必須通過自動化連鎖確保密閉性——例如，清潔系統同時連接兩個生產系統的情境必須被物理或邏輯性阻止，否則可能造成批次間交叉污染。

自動化系統層次結構

Level 4: ERP（企業資源規劃）
         ↕ 物料/訂單整合
Level 3: MES（製造執行系統）
         批次管理、EBR、人員/物料/設備確認
         ↕ 配方下發/批次記錄上傳
Level 2: SCADA/DCS（監控與控制）
         製程數據採集、報警管理、趨勢記錄
         ↕ 設定點/控制命令
Level 1: PLC/現場設備（現場控制器）
         閥門、泵浦、感測器的直接控制

PAT 工具通常整合於 Level 1-2，
數據流向 Level 2-3 進行決策支持

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 21 CFR Part 11 對電子批次記錄 (EBR) 有哪些具體要求？如果稽核軌跡 (Audit Trail) 功能未被啟用，會有什麼合規風險？
  2. PAT 工具（如在線 pH 探針、近紅外光譜儀）的數據若顯示製程超出正常範圍，MES 系統應如何自動回應？操作員的職責又是什麼？
5.5.2 Procedures｜程序標準化

原文內容 Original Text

Standardized procedures across multiple products and facilities should help to drive consistency and cross training of operators. Where feasible, the facility design should use error-proofing features, using, e.g.:

  • Color coding
  • Physically matched connections
  • RFID
  • MES and an automation system — to replace human verifications such as proper setup of transfer panel connections

When claiming the benefits of closed systems, the definition and practices required to achieve closure should be documented, in addition to actions required to return an area to closed when a breech is encountered.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：防呆設計 (Error-Proofing / Poka-Yoke)

來自日本製造業的品質工具 (Poka-Yoke)，目標是讓錯誤在發生之前就被阻止。在生物製藥廠中：

  • 色碼 (Color Coding)：不同產品或流體路徑使用不同顏色管路，減少混淆
  • 物理配對接頭：只有正確的管路才能連接到正確的接口（防止管路接錯）
  • RFID：設備、物料、人員均有唯一識別，系統自動確認組合是否合法

重點提示 Key Notes

轉接板 (Transfer Panel) 是生物製藥廠最常見的人為錯誤來源之一：操作員在複雜的管路面板前連接錯誤的閥門是實際發生過的偏差事件。MES 結合 RFID 的系統可以在操作員連接前就驗證每個接頭的合法性，大幅降低此類風險。

5.5.3 Training｜操作員訓練

原文內容 Original Text

Operators should be appropriately skilled with a broad knowledge base. Quality and technical support personnel can observe operations and be present in processing areas during operations. This allows for immediate consultation of these personnel when questions or deviations occur. Multi-tiered training can help to ensure safe operations.

Training methods used should include:

  • Review of written procedures
  • Classroom
  • Simulations of facility operations
  • On-the-job mentored/supervised training
