模組化設計（Modular Design）對新興市場的價值：模組化廠房設計是近年來生物製藥廠建造的重要趨勢。主要優勢包括：

  • 可在工廠（factory）預建、預測試，減少現場施工時間（縮短 30-50%）
  • 設計已被驗證（proven design），新廠不需要從頭設計——直接採用已通過 FDA 查廠的模板
  • 複雜潔淨設施的建造技術可以從已有經驗的國家（美、歐）輸出到新興市場（印度、東南亞、非洲）
  • 對 CDMO 而言，模組化設計可以快速複製到不同地點，實現全球產能擴張

精實製造整合思考 Lean Manufacturing Integration

精實製造對廠房設計的指導原則：

1. 價值流（Value Stream）分析：
   原料入庫 → 放行 → 生產 → 製程 QC →
   成品 → 放行 → 出貨

   每個步驟的等待時間 = 廠房設計的優化機會

2. 支援區域的距離最小化：
   QC 樣品路線: 生產室 → QC 實驗室 <5分鐘
   物料補給路線: 倉庫 → 生產室 <同一建築物

3. 消除浪費（Muda）：
   - 不必要的搬運 (Transport)
   - 等待物料放行 (Waiting)
   - 過度加工 (Over-processing)

實務應用 Practical Application

現代生物製藥 CDMO 廠房的設計越來越採用精實製造原則。例如，將品質管制實驗室（QC lab）設計為「快速分析中心」，位於生產廠房旁邊，可在 2-4 小時內完成製程中測試並放行中間產品，而傳統設計中 QC 實驗室設置在獨立建築，樣品傳遞和等待結果可能需要 8-12 小時。這種精實設計直接縮短了批次整體週期時間（Cycle Time），提高生產效率。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在廠房設計階段，如何決定 QC 實驗室的最佳位置？應考慮哪些因素？
  2. 一個在印度建設中的新興生物製藥廠考慮採用模組化設計。請列舉模組化設計的三個主要優點和一個潛在挑戰（相較於傳統現場施工）。
  3. 如果倉庫的「物料放行時間」是一個持續的生產瓶頸，精實製造原則建議用哪些廠房設計策略來改善？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary — Chapter 6B (Sections 6.4–6.9)

  • 6.4 物流隔離（Logistical Segregation）：核心目的是防止混淆（mix-ups）。有四種主要隔離類型：批次、產品、病毒削減操作、含細胞 vs. 無細胞操作。封閉製程（CIP/SIP、一次性系統）可以安全整合傳統需要隔離的操作，但共用元件（CIP 管線）是最大風險點。
  • 6.5 廠房與製程流向：三層目的（邏輯展示、避免混淆、環境保護）。雙走廊（clean supply + dirty return）適合開放製程；封閉製程可採用單走廊——節省廠房面積並簡化驗證。封閉製程消除了 Level 3 流向需求。
  • 6.6 清潔與表面完工：設備清洗室採用穿透式設備實現髒-乾淨單向流（二房 vs. 三房設計取決於通量）。CNC/Grade 8/Grade 7 各有對應的表面完工標準和清潔要求，與產品保護關係直接相關。封閉製程中的溢漏通常只是家務問題；開放製程中的溢漏是嚴重的 cGMP 事件。
  • 6.7 臨床試驗 vs. 商業生產：Phase I 豁免許多 cGMP 要求；Phase II 及以上必須完全符合 cGMP。Phase II 與商業生產的 cGMP 要求相同，差異只在規模，不在法規。
  • 6.8 疫苗與 BSL 圍堵：最關鍵的設計衝突——BSL（負壓）vs. GMP（正壓）。疫苗廠必須透過精確的壓力分區解決此矛盾。活病毒區域維持負壓（BSL），病毒滅活後恢復正壓（GLSP）。這是疫苗廠設計與標準生物製藥廠最根本的差異。
  • 6.9 生產支援區域：支援功能（倉庫、QC、設施工程、公用設施）的位置應最小化與生產的互動距離。精實製造原則（拉取系統、消除浪費）指導廠房設計。模組化設計對新興市場尤其有價值——可快速轉移已驗證設計、縮短建廠時間。

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol.6 (2nd Ed.): Biopharmaceutical Manufacturing Facilities

Chapter 7: Architectural

建築設計 | p85-p97

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol.6 (2nd Ed.): Biopharmaceutical Manufacturing Facilities | p85 - p97

本章學習目標

  • 理解生物製藥廠房「由內而外」的建築設計原則，以及三個設計階段（概念、基本、詳細）的意涵
  • 掌握廠房功能概念：垂直/水平流程、模組化建設（Off-Site Construction）、廠區流動管理（人員、物料、廢棄物）
  • 學習廠址選擇（Masterplanning）的關鍵考量：氣候、生物安全、現有設施改建限制（Brownfield vs Greenfield）
  • 了解建築外殼（Building Envelope）設計、模組化設計（Modular Design）對廠房長期投資回報的影響
  • 掌握結構設計要點：樓板荷重、跨距、抗震設計、以及對未來廠房彈性的影響
  • 認識建築資訊模型 BIM（Building Information Modeling）在生物製藥廠房設計管理中的應用
7.1 Introduction — 導論

原文內容 Original Text

This chapter aims to provide a client, design manager, or project manager a set of guidance information to aid the initial design implementation process.

The focus of the chapter is on features of concern to biopharmaceutical and vaccines facilities. Information applicable to other pharmaceutical facilities is included for completeness of facility design.

Design Principles

Pharmaceutical facilities are usually designed from the inside out. The design should be based on user needs and requirements.

The life cycle and potential for future change of use of the overall facility site and buildings also should be considered in order to comply with sustainable construction expectations, particularly where an organization's product range includes more than biopharmaceuticals. In this case, the potential for sharing or re-use of facilities for oral solid dose or over-the-counter products should be considered, subject to compliance with GMP regulatory expectations and the definition of a "facility" from a single use perspective.

The knowledge learnt from initial design discovery and technical transfer should be combined. Project front end definition methodologies can help with rapid transfer of key project information.

Facility design has three phases:

  1. Conceptual
  2. Basic
  3. Detailed

Risk and safety assessment processes should be applied during each phase of the design to support the construction design and implementation process.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

由內而外設計（Inside-Out Design）：生物製藥廠房的設計順序是先確定製程需求（設備、流程、清潔分級），再由此向外推演建築結構。這與一般商業建築「先蓋好外殼再想怎麼用」完全相反。

三個設計階段：

  • 概念設計（Conceptual）：確定廠房類型、規模、整體布局方向。此階段是最重要的，因為此後的決策成本代價最高。
  • 基本設計（Basic）：確定具體尺寸、結構系統、主要設備位置。
  • 詳細設計（Detailed）：完成所有施工圖紙和規格說明。

比喻說明 Analogy

「由內而外設計」就像裁縫做衣服：先量身材（製程需求），再剪布料（建築設計）。反過來「先有建築再硬塞製程」就像買了一件現成西裝，卻發現袖子太短——改起來非常麻煩且昂貴。

重點提示 Key Notes

每個設計階段都應執行風險與安全評估。生物製藥廠房在概念設計階段就必須考慮生物安全（Biosafety）分級需求，因為這直接影響通風系統、廢水處理、以及建築外殼設計。越晚發現問題，修改代價越高。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為何生物製藥廠房的設計必須「由內而外」？若反過來「由外而內」，會造成哪些具體問題？
  2. 技術轉移（Technical Transfer）時，哪些製程資訊對建築設計影響最大？請舉例說明。
7.2 Facility Design — 廠房設計

原文內容 Original Text

Facility design deals with both the visual and functional aspects of biopharmaceutical facility operation.

In addition to process area, elements to be integrated within a facility design can include:

  • Administration and amenity facilities
  • Security facilities
  • Quality Assurance (QA)
  • Quality Control (QC) laboratories; including line In-Process Control (IPC) and microbiology laboratories for product and environmental testing
  • Warehousing, including cold chain operations
  • Downstream fill finish operations
  • Process and building services, including utilities feed housings

The appropriate integration of these elements together with an appreciation of any future needs in regard of adaptability, flexibility, and expandability should help to ensure the viability of a sustainable operation.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

廠房設計的全面整合：一座完整的生物製藥廠房不僅有生產區，還必須整合行政、品保、品管實驗室、倉儲（含冷鏈）、下游充填完成、以及公用設施。這些區域的相對位置和動線規劃，直接影響日常運作效率和GMP合規性。

三個關鍵設計屬性：

  • 適應性（Adaptability）：廠房能否調整以應對製程變化
  • 彈性（Flexibility）：廠房能否支援多品項或多製程
  • 可擴展性（Expandability）：廠房能否在未來增加產能

重點提示 Key Notes

對於CDMO而言，「彈性」特別重要——因為CDMO需要同時服務多個客戶、多種產品。廠房設計必須在初期就規劃好如何實現多品項切換，而不是事後亡羊補牢。品管實驗室（QC）的位置應靠近生產區，以縮短IPC樣品傳遞時間，提升生產效率。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在CDMO廠房設計中，「彈性」和「效率」有時會產生矛盾。您會如何在設計層面取得平衡？
  2. 冷鏈倉儲（Cold Chain）在建築設計上需要哪些特殊考量？
7.2.1 Key Drivers for a Fully Functional Production Facility and Campus — 功能性生產廠房的關鍵驅動因素

原文內容 Original Text

Operational and functional design drivers toward ensuring best flows and correct layout design include:

  • Functionally focused risk assessment and response:
    • Design risk assessment should be performed from the start of a project, starting with concept stage. The assessments should be reviewed and updated throughout the design and construction process.
  • Economy and efficiency of operation:
    • Simple work flow from site receipt to point of use:
      • Avoiding crossing transport/workflows
      • Where unavoidable, a provision of an SOP for ease of operation
    • Ease of access to location for facility and equipment maintenance
  • Flexibility, adaptability, and expandability:
    • Review of potential future operations. Acceptance of new methods or processes that may impact future operations:
      • Clear zones for storage, process, support, process services, building services, utilities, administration, amenity
      • Administration and amenity functions integrated with workflow and location
      • Visual integration and involvement of the administration function with the work process can be beneficial
    • Nice place to work: Bright, light, and visually sustaining; Safe; Open operation without barriers, where possible; Maintenance of visual links through use of clear materials allows capacity for visual checks by staff; Secure; Product risk awareness; Maintain staff and visitor parking outside the security perimeter

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

三大設計驅動因素：

1. 功能導向風險評估：從概念階段就開始做設計風險評估，並在整個設計和施工過程中持續更新。這是ISPE對「Quality by Design（QbD）」理念在建築設計層面的體現。

2. 運作經濟性與效率：物料從收貨到使用點的流程應儘量簡單直接，避免交叉流動（Cross-Flow），這對GMP合規和日常操作效率都至關重要。

3. 工作環境品質：明亮、安全、視野開闊的工作環境可以提高員工士氣和警覺性，也有助於管理層進行目視管理（Visual Management）。

比喻說明 Analogy

「避免交叉工作流程」就像超市的單向動線設計——購物車只走一個方向，收銀台在出口附近，不會讓顧客在走道中對撞。生物製藥廠房的物料流、人員流、廢棄物流也需要類似的「單向化」規劃，減少GMP風險。

重點提示 Key Notes

「保持行政和訪客停車在安全邊界外」這個看似簡單的要求，其實涉及廠房安全設計的核心：未授權人員不應接觸生產區。CDMO廠房還需要特別考慮客戶訪問（Client Visit）路線的設計，既要讓客戶能夠看到生產情況，又不能違反GMP動線規定。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在廠房設計中，「透明度（視覺連結）」與「清潔區域隔離」之間如何取得平衡？
  2. CDMO接待客戶參觀時，訪客動線應如何規劃才能同時滿足GMP要求和客戶體驗？
7.2.2 Facility Concepts — 廠房概念設計

原文內容 Original Text

The process design may demonstrate lean values that can be lost if they are not reflected in the design of the remainder of the facility. In this respect, both design consistency and a strong overall design concept are considered important.

Vertical, Stepped, Horizontal

Vertical or semi-vertical (stepped) flow is often necessary from a process concept viewpoint, rather than a horizontal flow. This may have a significant effect on facility design and integration with other facility activities, e.g., warehousing, integration of amenities and administration. This also may affect future facility flexibility.

Off-Site Construction

This may be referred to as modular, flat-pack, container, or skid based construction. The introduction of off-site construction techniques can provide an alternative to the traditional construction process (which may be referred to as a "stick-build").

Using these techniques, construction takes place in a controlled environment and is not dependent on variability weather at a construction site. Typical benefits of these techniques include:

  • Improved quality
  • Overall program (schedule) reduction, including reduced site time
  • Ease of future expansion
  • Less reliance on site/local resources with attendance weather conditions
  • Potential for cost reduction through repetition

Modular systems linked with off-site builds can provide better cost effectiveness through increased cleanliness, better fit, and a reduced program (schedule). The design team (particularly the architectural and structural disciplines) should focus on a modular approach from the beginning of the design.

Larger facilities can gain from a mixture of construction processes with, e.g.:

  • Modular process sets linked to flat pack building construction, and skid mounted and container based building services
  • Utilities linked to stick built or flat pack administration and amenities building construction

Geographical location should be considered when determining an appropriate construction technique.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

垂直 vs 水平流程（Vertical vs Horizontal Flow）：

生物製藥製程有時需要利用重力進行物料傳遞（例如：培養基從高樓層配製後重力流入下層生物反應槽），這就形成「垂直流程」。設計師必須在廠房高度和樓層規劃上提前預留空間。水平流程則較常見於小分子藥廠，物料在同一樓層平移。

模組化建設（Off-Site Construction / Modular Construction）：在工廠預製模組，再運到現場組裝。相對於傳統現場施工（Stick-Build），具有品質更穩定、工期更短、可重複利用等優點。

比喻說明 Analogy

模組化廠房（Modular Facility）就像積木式玩具（LEGO）——每塊積木在工廠精確製造，到現場只需組合。傳統現場施工則像用水泥砌牆，需要等待硬化、受天氣影響，且建好後很難改變。CDMO擴廠時，模組化設計可以直接「加裝積木」，省去大量時間和成本。

重點提示 Key Notes

生物製藥廠房有一個獨特挑戰：大型生物反應槽（Bioreactor）可能高達數層樓，廠房需要為此設計高天花板（可能需要4-6公尺淨高）。這是與一般小分子藥廠截然不同的建築需求。設計團隊必須在早期就確認最大設備尺寸，否則後期改動代價極高。

實務應用 Practical Application

台灣某CDMO正計劃建設新的生物製藥廠房，預算有限且工期緊迫。採用模組化建設（Off-Site Construction）有以下優勢：在台灣天氣多變的環境下，工廠預製可確保品質穩定；模組可預先通過驗證；未來若獲得新客戶，可快速增加模組擴大產能。缺點是前期設計決策必須非常明確，因為模組尺寸一旦固定就難以更改。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 模組化建設相比傳統現場施工（Stick-Build），在GMP驗證方面有哪些優劣勢？
  2. 如果您是CDMO的工程負責人，您會在哪些情況下選擇垂直流程設計？哪些情況下選擇水平流程？
7.2.3 Flows and their Impact — 流動管理及其影響

原文內容 Original Text

In-facility flows are of cGMP and regulatory concern. When in-facility flows are integrated with site flows, they contribute to the interdisciplinary understanding of a design layout, particularly at the masterplanning stage. The flow characteristics of a site and the impact of material, personnel, waste, and sample flows should be considered to help to ensure efficiency and economy of operation.

Space constrictions should be considered for smaller biopharmaceutical facilities and retrofits, particularly with closed or continuous processing. Internal site workflows should ensure safe and secure operation within the needs of GMP compliance and cleanliness requirements. For example, the master seed/cell bank should be positioned close to its use location, to avoid significant commercial, operational, or biosafety risks through unnecessary transport, security, and safety issues.

For closed processing, individual flows should be analyzed to ensure that each element of an operation follows an efficient and safe route without compromising the product. For example:

  • Personnel flows:
    • Street clothes
    • Facility gowning
    • Individual grade gowning paths
    • Warehouse clothing
    • Maintenance gowning
    • Location of specialist Personal Protection Equipment (PPE)
  • Material flows:
    • Master cell
    • Product flows: Upstream, In-process staging areas, Downstream, Fill/finish to store
    • Buffer and media flows including materials from store to location
    • Equipment maintenance flows
    • Clean-In-Place (CIP) considerations
    • Clean-out-of-place considerations

The impact of changes in flow formats should be understood in an architectural and structural site context and responded to accordingly.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

廠內流動管理（In-Facility Flow Management）：GMP法規要求對廠內的人員、物料、廢棄物、樣品流動進行嚴格管控，防止交叉污染（Cross-Contamination）。這不只是操作程序問題，更是建築設計問題——廠房的通道、門的位置、換衣室的配置都必須支持正確的流動模式。

主要流動類型（六大流）：

  • 人員流（Personnel Flow）：不同更衣級別需要不同的更衣通道
  • 物料流（Material Flow）：從上游到下游的單向流動
  • 緩衝液/培養基流（Buffer/Media Flow）
  • 設備維護流（Equipment Maintenance Flow）
  • 廢棄物流（Waste Flow）
  • 樣品流（Sample Flow）

重點提示 Key Notes

「主菌種/細胞庫（Master Seed/Cell Bank）應放置在靠近使用位置」這個看似小事的要求，實際上涉及重大的商業和生物安全風險。細胞庫是整個生產的核心資產，不必要的搬運會增加污染和遺失風險。在設計階段就將細胞庫位置靠近接種工作站，是降低操作風險的重要設計決策。

比喻說明 Analogy

廠內流動管理就像醫院的「清潔區、污染區、半污染區」分區管理——手術室護士不會從污染走廊走進手術室，同樣地，生物製藥廠的操作人員在不同清潔等級區域之間也需要有明確的更衣換裝流程，而這些流程必須在建築設計階段就用空間布局來「強制執行」。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在生物製藥廠房中，人員流動（Personnel Flow）需要考慮哪些不同的換裝路徑？為何不同等級的更衣不能共用同一條通道？
  2. CIP（就地清洗）管路的走向如何影響廠房的整體物料流規劃？
7.3 Placing the Facility on the Site — 廠址選擇與廠區規劃

原文內容 Original Text

A biopharmaceutical manufacturing facility may be constructed within an existing or new site. The facility should be able to operate efficiently within the type and location of the site.

7.3.1 Masterplanning

Masterplanning is the overall consideration of a site's or facility's current and future needs. It should be flexible in its response to varying product supply requirements. Masterplanning should reflect an operation's business planning aspirations and should oversee site and operational planning.

The need for defining a masterplan is dependent on the size of site operation (on-going or planned). A manufacturing facility dealing with all stages of pharmaceutical production should link the elements of the facility to each other in a logical sequence. For existing facilities, where a site has developed due to need and availability, the overall site operation should be reviewed to help maintain or improve cost effective production and management.

Bio Security and Safety Considerations

Local issues should be considered in the placement of a biopharmaceutical facility. Facilities may need significant security and safety protection due to local political situations. Risks around these concerns should be reviewed early in the design process to ensure that the issues are fully understood and appropriate protection, access, or facility placement and physical design/specification measures are implemented.

Facility Size and its Impact on Design and Concept

Existing sites and facilities may experience a size reduction through the use of continuous processes, particularly with large volume throughput. Significantly increased titers can result in reduced equipment sizing for the same throughput. Small high volume process modules may have a disproportionate effect on upstream and downstream operations with a consequent effect on site planning.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

總體規劃（Masterplanning）：Masterplanning是對整個廠區現在和未來需求的全面考量。它不只是今天的廠房配置，更是一份「廠區發展藍圖」——預留未來擴建空間、規劃公用設施管廊、考慮不同建築物之間的邏輯連結。

連續製程對廠房規模的影響：現代生物製藥趨勢是從批次製程（Batch Process）轉向連續製程（Continuous Process）。連續製程可大幅縮小設備尺寸，意味著同樣產能的廠房可以更小。但這也可能造成上下游設備規模不匹配，需要在Masterplanning階段就考慮到。

重點提示 Key Notes

生物安全（Bio Security）的廠址考量：生物製藥廠房處理的是活的生物材料（微生物、病毒等），廠址選擇必須考慮：
1. 周邊環境污染源（工業廢氣、農業粉塵）
2. 生物材料意外洩漏對當地環境的影響
3. 政治穩定性（涉及高價值生物材料的安全）
這些考量在一般建築設計中幾乎不存在，是生物製藥廠房的特殊挑戰。

比喻說明 Analogy

Masterplanning就像城市規劃——一個好的城市不只考慮今天的建設，還要預留未來道路、捷運、公園的空間。生物製藥廠區也一樣：初期建廠時就要規劃好未來10-20年可能的擴建位置，否則等到需要擴廠時才發現沒有空地，代價將非常高昂。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 連續製程（Continuous Process）的導入，如何影響生物製藥廠房的空間規劃？請從上游和下游兩個角度分析。
  2. 為什麼生物製藥廠房在廠址選擇時需要特別考慮「生物安全」因素？請舉出兩個具體的風險場景。
7.3.2 Facility Concepts: Large / Small / Greenfield / Brownfield — 大型/小型廠房；全新/改建廠址

原文內容 Original Text

Large Facility Concepts

The impact of climate on larger facility design means, e.g.:

  • An open campus format being more acceptable in mild temperate/mesothermal climate zones
  • An integrated or spine format being more suited to equatorial and cold climates where protection from the elements is necessary

A key consideration is the protection and ease of passage of goods or equipment in transit from one part of a facility to another. The selection of which format suits the operation is dependent on several factors, e.g., geographical location. Each format has advantages and disadvantages. For some locations or operations, a mixture of format may provide most flexibility in use, by providing expansion capacity, acceptance, and placement also will be a matter of compliance with local permitting criteria.

Small Facility Concepts

Smaller integrated biopharmaceutical facilities with multi-product or single product capability use less site area and are usually less affected by utilities issues that affect the large facilities.

Process Pods and Field Located Processes

The possibility of reduction in size of biopharmaceutical and vaccines facilities processes allows the capacity to contain processes in process pods. These process pods may be used both as 'plug and play' units within a facility or they could be positioned close to the drug need, e.g., as support to medical emergencies the needs of developing countries.

Greenfield

Layout opportunities depend on site size, access, and orientation. For further information, see Chapter 8 of this Guide.

Brownfield

For brownfield sites, pre-existing utilities, administration, warehousing, and engineering functions should be considered in association with the User Requirement Brief (URB) of a new project, e.g., to ensure the benefits of brownfield site integration. A brownfield site may be considered as a "retrofit" facility and introducing new ways of working may have a significant effect on other site operations. This can lead to further capital works with an overall operational life cycle gain.

Pre-existing Site Issues

Pre-existing site issues can significantly affect operation. Examples include:

  • Placing the primary HVAC intake of a biopharmaceutical facility close to the extract ventilation outlets of neighboring facilities and introducing significant environmental contamination risk
  • Locating a biopharmaceutical facility next to a conserved pond where clouds of small flying insects live and breed each season providing a continuing filtration issue
  • Locating a biopharmaceutical facility near cottonwood trees whose seeds cause significant filtration issues

Flood risk may be issue in some countries. This is a particular issue for biopharmaceutical facilities with potential risks to the local environment and public drainage system, as well as the potential risk of contamination of both process and product.

Retrofits

There may be unforeseen issues with a location. Pre-existing permitting, structural, or architectural issues should be considered prior to proceeding with a project. Local permitting should be checked as carrying out retrofit or conversion work may lead to the need to upgrade the entire facility to meet current environmental, accessibility, or other governmental requirements.

Pre-existing facilities: upgrade considerations:

  • Structural design: close columns indicates a high floor loading above or a facility that may not provide the required flexibility
  • Insulation costs to meet current regulations may be prohibitive as this may involve recladding the structure
  • Floor loadings may not relate to the use required: point or superimposed loads, such as individual leg loads of a large column or loadings of full bags of buffer, may prohibit use of a floor
  • Utilities and building services should be evaluated, as they may be oversized and not able to be "de-tuned" or undersized and unable to respond to the projected facility needs

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Greenfield vs Brownfield：

  • Greenfield（全新廠址）：在空地上全新建設，設計自由度最高，但初始投資最大，且無現有基礎設施可用。
  • Brownfield（改建廠址）：在已有建築或廠區基礎上改建，可利用現有設施降低成本，但受現有結構限制，可能有隱藏問題（如地基不足、配管老舊）。

Process Pods（製程艙）：可獨立運作的小型自包含製程模組，可在廠內作為「插拔式」單元使用，也可部署到偏遠地區（如發展中國家的醫療緊急需求）。這是生物製藥去中心化製造（Decentralized Manufacturing）的雛形。

比喻說明 Analogy

Brownfield改建就像在老房子裡重新裝潢：你省去了打地基的費用，但可能發現牆壁裡有老舊水管、地板承重不足、或是不符合現行法規的電路。有時候「改建成本」反而比「全新建設」更高，這就是為什麼必須在改建前做詳細的盡職調查（Due Diligence）。

重點提示 Key Notes

HVAC進氣口的位置是生物製藥廠址選擇的關鍵！若主進氣口（HVAC Intake）靠近鄰近廠房的廢氣排放口，或靠近昆蟲繁殖地（水塘）、樹木（楊樹飛絮），將造成持續性的過濾堵塞問題，嚴重影響潔淨室等級和維運成本。這些「現場問題（Pre-existing Site Issues）」在廠址評估階段必須逐一排查，絕不能等到施工後才發現。

改建廠房評估清單 Brownfield Assessment Checklist

改建前必須評估的項目：
1. 結構柱距（Column Spacing）
   → 柱距過密 = 樓板設計荷重過高 = 可能不敷使用
   → 或：缺乏設備重新配置的彈性

2. 樓板荷重（Floor Loading）
   → 大型色層管柱（Chromatography Column）的腳支撐點荷重
   → 大型緩衝液袋（Buffer Bag）的面荷重

3. 現有公用設施（Utilities）評估
   → 過大（Oversized）→ 無法「降噸」以符合節能需求
   → 過小（Undersized）→ 無法滿足新製程需求

4. 隔熱材料（Insulation）
   → 升級至現行法規可能需要整個外牆重新包覆
   → 成本可能高於全新建設

5. 現有許可（Pre-existing Permits）
   → 改建可能觸發全面升級至最新建築法規的要求

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您的公司考慮收購一座舊製藥廠進行生物製藥改建。您會優先評估哪五個方面的「隱藏風險」？
  2. Process Pods（製程艙）在CDMO的商業模式中有何潛在應用？請從客戶服務和產能彈性兩個角度思考。
7.4 Envelope/Building Shell Design and Visual Design Influences — 建築外殼設計與視覺設計影響

原文內容 Original Text

The design of the building shell is significant in setting the tone of perception for a facility. The enclosure should perform a primary task of providing environmental shelter.

Local conditions should guide the approach to envelope design. This in turn affects the visual response. There can be an expectation of high visual quality for biopharmaceutical manufacturing facilities.

A facility is likely to be there for at least 30 years, and this should be considered when designing its shell. Issues to be addressed include:

  • Does the shell respond to the environmental conditions correctly?
    • Is it sensible to use flat roofs and parapets in high volume rain or snow areas?
    • Should items be integrated into the facade that provide short term value?
    • Will it wear well?
    • What is the location of intakes, extracts and extraneous pipework?
    • Is access for facility changeover correctly considered?
    • How easy and safe is it to maintain?
    • Is the opportunity for expansion considered through the provision of fallow or swing space or additional land?

Facilities that look good and operate successfully over long time periods normally provide significant return on investment.

7.4.1 Modular Design

Consideration should be given to the integration of modules into a building shell or to the construction of fully modular facilities. Examples of limitations and opportunities provided by available construction technology, include:

  • Need to retain controlling dimensions: to obtain the advantages of repetition, a standard dimension set may apply that provides less dimensional flexibility than stick build
  • Different systems have different modular dimensions: where a modular system is to be used, the choice of system should be made early in the design process to ensure that the building is designed in accordance with the correct dimensions and any limitations are respected
  • How the module will be transported from the module fabrication shop to the final installation site. The method of transport should be considered, including:
    • Road limitations with overhead clearances, width and weight limits
    • Shipping sizes, including specialist hoist requirements
    • Airfreight limitations on size and weight
  • Allowance for module to module interconnection:
    • Space needed for process pipework connection
    • Lateral linking electrical and data trays, conduit, or ladders
    • Access space needed for maintenance of valves
  • Checking that future flexibility and adaptability are not compromised
  • Ensuring the risk of increased costs through initial factory tooling are balanced by site schedule/program and value gains

The decision to proceed with a modular design should be made at the front end of the design process, preferably at concept stage. Decisions on which process equipment is to be purchased, its design, the utility requirements of the equipment, and the process areas and method of installation, should be made early, as the facility design is significantly affected. The choice of modular contractors also should be made early to ensure their involvement from the commencement of the detail design process.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

建築外殼（Building Envelope / Building Shell）：指廠房的外牆、屋頂、基礎——即將室內與室外環境分隔的整個外部結構。對於生物製藥廠房，建築外殼除了提供基本的遮風擋雨功能外，還需要：

  • 支持潔淨室的氣壓和溫濕度控制
  • 最小化熱橋（Thermal Bridges）以減少結露
  • 正確配置HVAC進排氣口位置
  • 考慮30年以上的耐久性和維護性

Fallow/Swing Space（預留空間）：在廠房初建時刻意留出的未開發空間，供未來擴建使用。預留空間雖然短期看起來「浪費」，但長期來看是非常划算的投資。

重點提示 Key Notes

模組化設計決策必須在最前期做出！一旦開始詳細設計，模組尺寸就基本固定了。如果到了施工階段才決定改用模組化，不但無法享受成本優勢，反而可能因為設計改動付出更大代價。此外，模組從製造工廠到安裝現場的運輸方式（公路/海運/空運）也必須提前規劃——因為台灣的部分山路或港口可能對超大模組有限制。

比喻說明 Analogy

建築外殼設計就像選擇車的外殼：不只看好不好看，還要考慮當地氣候（台灣多雨→防水性能）、長期維護成本（容不容易修）、30年後是否仍功能完好。一個漂亮但難以維護的建築外殼，長期TCO（總擁有成本）反而更高。

實務應用 Practical Application

在台灣建設生物製藥廠房時，建築外殼設計需特別注意：颱風和梅雨季帶來的大量降雨（考慮平屋頂vs坡屋頂的選擇）、高溫高濕對外牆隔熱的需求、以及地震（抗震設計）。這些因素都會影響建築外殼的設計規格，並在初期增加成本，但長期運作中可大幅降低維護費用。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 模組化設計在運輸階段可能遇到哪些限制？這些限制如何影響模組的最大尺寸規格？
  2. 「模組對模組的連接（Module-to-Module Interconnection）」在生物製藥廠房中有哪些特殊要求？為什麼管道連接空間特別重要？
7.5 Construction Issues — 施工相關議題

原文內容 Original Text

Construction based decisions can be significant in both the implementation of a facility design, safety, and its subsequent use. Attributes that should be available to facilities include:

  • Flexibility, adaptability, and extendibility
  • Equipment access for replacement or maintenance

A biomanufacturing process may be installed only for five years of the building use. A facility represents significant investment and should be adaptable to another use without significant spend in order to meet its longer term objectives.

Examples of basic decisions that can be made that make a facility a better investment from the outset include:

  • The construction of the floor slab to take a variety of loadings should be considered. This will allow the potential for relocation of vessels without the need for consideration of specialist foundations for each location. This would provide only a small additional cost or even be cost equal to the specially provided condition if considered at commencement.
  • A transfer deck or suspended through floor vessel should be considered, as these affect loadings and provide vibration issues on an upper floor slab. This can cause the need for local or a special built-in support structures. Alternative options such that initial decisions do not affect future flexibility should be considered.
  • Provision of fallow space for utility expansion. Future utility needs for different products should be considered.
  • Provision for entry and exit paths for different equipment types. Installation of removable walls and floor sections for equipment movement should be considered.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

「生物製造製程的壽命往往短於廠房壽命」：一個生物製藥製程可能只使用廠房5年，但廠房本身設計壽命是30年以上。這意味著廠房必須在設計時就考慮未來的多種用途，不能只為當前製程量身訂做。

樓板（Floor Slab）設計的前瞻性：在初期就將樓板設計為能承受多種荷載，雖然增加了少許初始成本，但可以省去日後每次重新配置設備時的專項基礎工程費用。

可移動牆板和地板段（Removable Walls / Floor Sections）：大型設備（如生物反應器）在未來維護或更換時，可能需要從廠房外搬入。預先設計好「設備進出路徑」（包括可拆卸的牆段），可大幅降低未來翻修成本。

重點提示 Key Notes

本節最重要的洞察：施工時多花一點點，未來省很多。例如：樓板加厚以支持更大荷重，初期多花5%，但可能在未來10年內省下數百萬元的專項基礎工程費用。這種前瞻性的設計思維，是優秀的生物製藥廠房工程師必備的素養。

比喻說明 Analogy

「預留公用設施擴充空間（Fallow Space for Utility Expansion）」就像蓋房子時預先配置額外的電管和水管接頭——不用立即使用，但當未來要新增冷氣或洗碗機時，不需要重新破壁重拉管線。在生物製藥廠房中，「多預留一根管道槽（Pipe Chase）」的成本遠低於日後打通牆壁增加的費用。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼「Transfer Deck（轉移層）」或「穿樓板懸掛槽（Suspended Through-Floor Vessel）」需要特別的結構設計？振動問題如何影響生產？
  2. 如果您是工程負責人，您會如何說服財務團隊批准「多花初期成本以換取未來彈性」的預算申請？
7.5.1 Impact of Structure on Design — 結構設計對廠房設計的影響

原文內容 Original Text

Additional Footings/Foundations

Inclusion of additional footings, foundation, and/or piling to support potential future expansion should be considered. This is a relatively small cost to allow flexibility.

Long Span/Short Span

Assuming a facility with more than one level, the risk to flexibility and adaptability of layout rests on structural loading and column location. Structural spans for commercial buildings have slowly been creeping up from a given 6 m × 6 m (20 ft × 20 ft) span 30 years ago to a normal 7.5 m × 7.5 m (25 ft × 25 ft) or even 9 m to 10 m (30 to 35 ft) spans in 2012. New secondary and biopharmaceutical facilities have been constructed with 30 m to 40 m (100 ft to 130 ft) spans to allow for flexibility in equipment layout and maximum future use flexibility. Safety codes should be met.

Dancefloor or Ballroom Concepts

The availability of smaller modular horizontal format biopharmaceutical equipment and more flexible set-ups allows the design of low building structures based on long spanning roofs. The structures are designed for reasonable service loads and capable of support of walk-on ceilings and/or high level service modules. This allows the opportunity for significant flexibility and adaptability with greater opportunity for expansion through extension or provision of swing space.

Construction Materials

These are generally dependent on geographical location and local availability and capability. Normally steel or concrete (either pre-cast or in situ) primary structures are used, although composite materials are becoming more available. Higher insulation requirements to meet energy targets have ensured the growth of modular insulated panel systems for both wall cladding (siding) and roofing. Workplace expectations and regulations are necessitating greater areas of glass wall both internally and externally.

Slab Thickening and Piling

Early decisions that affect future options become limiting factors for facility re-use or onward design. Careful consideration should be given to the laying of a piling mat and slab for very specific purposes. It may be preferable to design the slab for a general high loading initially and consider the area overall for a higher floor loading.

Example: A late design decision on volumes meant a late inclusion into a basement of an 18,000 L kill tank for a vaccines based facility. The new basement structure was designed for a general floor loading for mechanical plant, as there was a poor geotechnical condition and the kill tank was not highlighted to be an issue. Given a two week window, the design team was fortunate to design a special load spreading frame to fit the location, select a vessel that could fit the one sufficiently large access stairwell, pass between the column structure, and those items of plant that were in place. This provided a significant on-cost and will affect future flexibility.

Movement Issues

The inclusion of structural or constructional movement joints into clean buildings should be avoided.

Joint systems that provide a simple seal may be difficult to obtain; therefore, location of both primary structural joints, and screed or slab day joints, becomes critical for ease of maintenance of a cleanliness regime. Floor slabs at ground level should be designed to ensure either no joints or joints in discrete locations agreed with the design team and with a clear understanding of risk.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

結構跨距（Structural Span）對廠房彈性的影響：結構柱之間的距離越大，樓板中間越少有柱子阻礙，設備配置就越靈活。30年前商業建築的跨距是6m×6m，現在生物製藥廠房可達30-40m的超大跨距。雖然大跨距的鋼結構初始成本較高，但換來的是無限的設備重新配置彈性。

舞廳概念（Dancefloor / Ballroom Concept）：大空間、長跨距的廠房設計，就像一個大舞廳——中間沒有柱子，可以隨時重新排列設備，且天花板夠高可走維修路徑。這特別適合單層或低層的生物製藥製造廠房。

重點提示 Key Notes

18,000 L Kill Tank 的案例教訓：這個真實案例說明了「晚期設計決策的代價」——一個18,000公升的殺菌槽（Kill Tank），因為在設計後期才決定加入，導致結構工程師必須在2週內設計特殊承重框架，同時還需要選一個恰好能通過樓梯口和柱位的槽體。這種情況完全可以通過早期確認製程需求來避免。生物製藥廠房的「隱藏大型設備」（如Kill Tank、大型緩衝液槽）必須在概念設計階段就列出清單。

潔淨室中的結構伸縮縫（Movement Joints）：普通建築需要伸縮縫來應對熱脹冷縮，但潔淨室的伸縮縫會破壞密封性，造成微粒和微生物的潛在污染點。因此潔淨室應盡量避免結構伸縮縫，或將其設置在可以有效密封的位置。

結構跨距的演進 Structural Span Evolution

一般建築結構跨距的演進：
30年前（1990年代）：  6m × 6m  （20ft × 20ft）
現在（2010年代）：    7.5m × 7.5m  （25ft × 25ft）
                    9m-10m  （30-35ft）
先進生物製藥廠：      30m-40m  （100-130ft）

結構跨距越大 → 設備配置越靈活 → 初始鋼材成本越高
但：未來重新配置的成本 → 大幅降低

大型生物反應器高度需求：
10,000L 生物反應器 → 約需 4-6m 淨高
20,000L 生物反應器 → 可能需要 6-8m 淨高（含設備頂部操作空間）
→ 樓高設計必須提前確認最大設備尺寸！

比喻說明 Analogy

「舞廳概念（Ballroom Concept）」廠房就像一個大型倉庫式量販店（如家樂福）：沒有中間柱子、挑高天花板、任何區域都可以重新配置。相比之下，傳統小跨距廠房就像老式住宅：到處是承重柱，要改格局非常困難。生物製藥製程的設備不斷更新換代，「舞廳概念」讓廠房能夠跟上製程演進的腳步。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼生物製藥廠房需要比一般商業建築更大的結構跨距？請從設備尺寸和未來彈性兩個角度分析。
  2. 潔淨室地板的接縫（Floor Joints）設計為何如此重要？如果接縫位置設計不當，可能造成哪些GMP問題？
7.5.2 Seismic Considerations — 抗震設計

原文內容 Original Text

The design of biopharmaceutical facilities for seismic risk locations (e.g., west coast USA, Romania, North East India, south east China) should be carefully considered. For the US guidance, see the National Institute of Building Sciences Whole Building Design Guide [53].

The European Eurocode 8 [54] is likely to be adopted by Russia, Ukraine, and Belarus, along with the other nine structural Eurocodes. Kazakhstan is adopting the codes from 2015 in place of the previous reliance on Russian codes. For biopharmaceutical facilities, seismic design needs special consideration in terms of slab sizes and equipment connections. For example, design for earthquake code does not usually cover utilities considerations. Inclusion of additional bracing for the utility systems, as well as for the primary structure and securing of equipment may allow the opportunity for rapid restart for a biopharmaceutical facility after a seismic event.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

生物製藥廠房抗震設計的特殊性：一般建築的抗震設計只關注建築結構本身（不倒塌即可），但生物製藥廠房還需要考慮：

  • 大型液態槽（Buffer Tank、Bioreactor）在地震中的液態晃動荷重（Sloshing Loads）
  • 精密設備（天秤、質量流量計）的抗震固定
  • 公用設施管路（純水、WFI、蒸汽）的抗震支撐——標準建築法規通常不涵蓋此項目
  • 地震後快速重啟的能力（Rapid Restart）

重點提示 Key Notes

台灣位於地震高風險區域，是亞太地區地震最頻繁的地區之一。台灣的生物製藥廠房在設計時必須特別重視：公用設施管路（WFI、蒸汽、氮氣管路）的抗震支撐設計；大型槽體的錨定設計；以及建立地震後的快速復工標準作業程序（SOP）。一旦地震造成停產，其商業損失遠超結構修復費用。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼標準建築抗震法規「不足以」保護生物製藥廠房？需要額外考慮哪些因素？
  2. 地震後「快速重啟（Rapid Restart）」能力對CDMO的商業價值是什麼？如何在設計階段實現這一目標？
7.5.3–7.5.4 Modular Build & Structural Spans — 模組化建設與結構跨距

原文內容 Original Text

7.5.3 Modular Build

Process modules, whether as enclosed containers or skids, within a facility can be set on a deck or integrated into a frame. They are not usually self-supporting. Structural loading considerations and access to process modules, e.g., for replacement, should be considered.

7.5.4 Structural Spans

Longer spans and less floor interruption can provide greater flexibility.

Items of equipment which need special consideration for support on an upper level should be identified in order to maintain flexibility and adaptability. Items that require special consideration in terms of location and effect on current or future facility include:

  • Static loads (through floor buffer and/or media vessels)
  • Active loads (e.g., 2 tonne IBCs)

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

靜態荷重 vs 動態荷重（Static vs Active Loads）：

  • 靜態荷重（Static Loads）：固定不動的大型槽體（如穿樓板的緩衝液槽、培養基槽）的重量，需要在結構上設計專門的支撐點，且可能需要特殊地基處理。
  • 動態/活動荷重（Active Loads）：可移動的大型中間散裝容器（IBC, Intermediate Bulk Container），例如2噸重的IBC桶，在廠內以叉車或起重機移動時，會在不同位置產生動態荷重，樓板設計必須考慮這些荷重可能出現的所有區域。

重點提示 Key Notes

製程模組（Process Modules）通常不能自支撐（not self-supporting），必須設置在支撐甲板（Deck）或整合式框架中。這意味著在設計模組化廠房時，主體建築結構和模組結構必須協同設計，不能分開進行，否則可能出現結構不匹配的問題。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 2噸重的IBC容器在廠內移動時，為何對樓板設計的挑戰大於一個固定放置的2噸槽體？
  2. 製程模組（Process Module）「不能自支撐」的特性，對廠房主體建築設計有何影響？
7.6 Permitting, Code, and Insurance Issues — 許可、法規與保險議題

原文內容 Original Text

Permitting varies between geographical locations. Planning and building codes should be understood early on in the construction process. Basic guidance includes:

  • International Building Code (IBC) is a US originated code that does not apply to all countries. A number of countries have stricter compliance requirements. This could affect building compartmentalization and escape compliancy for larger biopharmaceutical facilities, including the break-out requirements with highly contained deep plan facilities.
  • Insurers may have significantly higher and tighter expectations than many country codes. Depending on product value or facility throughput, insurers may apply Maximum Foreseeable Loss (MFL) requirements that could impact adversely on initial intended flexibility.
  • Fire and spillage risk issues: along with flood risk, the risk of fire, even in local facility areas, provides specific issues for biopharmaceutical facilities. Both code and insurer requirements may expect bunding to a facility either in specific areas, area by area, and/or at floor perimeters for sprinkler and/or fire water retention and analytical testing prior to safe release or disposal to ensure that there is no biological risk to public health via sewage, surface water, or ground water systems. This may introduce an undercroft or suitably sized basement to ensure the necessary volume is retained.

It is advisable to speak with the insurers and the permitting authorities from the outset of a project to ensure that code interpretations are in line with design expectations.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

三個關鍵監管/保險概念：

1. IBC（International Building Code）：美國建築法規，不適用所有國家，各地有自己的建築法規。重要的是：許多國家的法規比IBC更嚴格。

2. 最大可預見損失（Maximum Foreseeable Loss, MFL）：保險公司評估的最壞情況損失金額。MFL要求可能迫使設計增加額外的防火/防爆隔間，這可能與設計師希望的「開放彈性空間」相衝突。

3. 圍堰（Bunding）：在設備或區域周圍設置的低矮隔堰，用於收集消防水、洩漏液體，防止生物性或化學性污染物進入污水系統。對於生物製藥廠房，消防水必須在排放前經過生物安全評估。

重點提示 Key Notes

保險要求往往比法規更嚴格！這是ISPE文件的重要提醒。建築師通常只確保符合建築法規，但保險公司（特別是針對高價值生物製藥產品的專業保險）可能提出更嚴格的MFL要求，包括防火隔間、自動滅火系統規格、以及消防水收集系統。這些要求應在設計初期就與保險公司討論，否則後期改動代價極高。

生物性廢水的特殊處理：與普通化學品不同，生物製藥廠房的消防水可能含有生物活性物質（如活病毒、重組蛋白），在排放前必須進行分析測試，確認無生物安全風險。這是建築設計中必須為此預留的物理空間（地下室/儲槽）。

比喻說明 Analogy

保險公司的MFL要求就像嚴格的房東——即使你的設計符合建築法規，房東可能要求額外的消防設備才願意出租。在生物製藥廠房中，「保險公司的要求」這個「房東」的標準可能遠比政府建築法規更嚴，必須在規劃初期就納入考量，否則中途被要求大幅修改，損失極大。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO在建設新廠時，應在概念設計階段就邀請保險公司和政府審批單位參與設計審查。這樣可以提早發現「法規要求」與「保險要求」之間的差異，並在設計中取得平衡。例如：保險公司可能要求廠房每300平方公尺就要有防火隔間，但製程設計需要開放式大空間——這個矛盾必須在初期通過協商解決，而不是在施工完成後。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為何生物製藥廠房的消防水排放需要特別的生物安全評估？這與一般化工廠有何不同？
  2. 圍堰（Bunding）設計在建築空間規劃上有何影響？為什麼需要提前考慮地下儲槽（Undercroft）空間？
7.7 Facility Design and Design Management Methodologies and Tools — 設計管理方法與工具

原文內容 Original Text

Software developments provide design tools for the development and cross discipline integration of design from an early stage with a consequent capacity to design, record, and integrate projects from commencement. Visual development from instigation through 3D modeling of all aspects allows the consideration and review process to happen at significant speed allowing rapid option development and value judgment.

Subsequent construction and operation interfacing and sequencing review using real-time scheduling to post construction facility management using the fully integrated design model developed through construction for facilities management is possible. This is known as Building Information Modeling (BIM) and its attributes, referred as onward developments of 3D from 4D to 8D.

Biopharmaceutical and vaccines facilities can be extremely complex buildings, and may use up to 15 disciplines or more for design. This team needs to be integrated. BIM integrated with facility design management systems has evolved to make such programs significantly simpler to understand and implement.

Examples of integrated design tools include:

  • Integrated Project Delivery (IPD) [55]
  • ADePT design management tool [56]

7.7.1 BIM and Design Management

IPD was developed in the US as an integrated project management method. ADePT was developed initially in the UK by Loughborough University working with major contractors and design practices to provide an integrated design management system. Engineering companies may use similar integration methodologies for early project definition and front end design development.

BIM supports these systems through the integration of attributed 3D design software parametrics.

"Building information modeling may involve the introduction of new contracting methodologies as it allows for the adoption of a 'build before you build' opportunity with earlier review of design concepts and methodologies integrated with multi-discipline detail design interfaces."

For further information on the use and integration of the methodology, see the American Institute of Architects (AIA) [57].

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

建築資訊模型（BIM, Building Information Modeling）：BIM是一種以3D模型為核心、整合所有設計、施工、運維資訊的數位化工作方式。「從3D到8D」的維度擴展：

  • 3D：三維空間模型（長×寬×高）
  • 4D：加入時間維度（施工進度模擬）
  • 5D：加入成本維度（造價管理）
  • 6D：加入永續設計（能源效率）
  • 7D：加入設施管理（建成後的運維資訊）
  • 8D：加入安全管理（施工安全模擬）

「先建後建（Build Before You Build）」：BIM允許在實際施工前，先在電腦中「虛擬建造」整棟廠房，提前發現管道碰撞（Clash Detection）、施工順序問題等，大幅減少施工現場的變更。

比喻說明 Analogy

BIM就像電動遊戲中的「城市建設模擬器」——在電腦中先建一座虛擬城市，觀察道路是否順暢、水電是否夠用、人流是否合理，確認沒問題後再真正動工。生物製藥廠房有15個以上的設計專業（建築、結構、電氣、暖通、管道、儀表……），沒有BIM整合，各專業之間的衝突幾乎不可避免，發現越晚代價越高。

重點提示 Key Notes

生物製藥廠房的設計複雜度遠超一般建築——可能涉及15個以上的設計專業。BIM的核心價值在於：所有專業在同一個模型中工作，當一個專業修改設計時，其他相關專業可以即時看到影響。例如：HVAC工程師修改風管路徑時，結構工程師可以立即看到是否與結構梁衝突，而不是等到施工時才發現需要改管。

BIM維度說明 BIM Dimensions Reference

BIM維度層級（From 3D to 8D）：

3D → 三維空間模型（幾何形狀與位置）
4D → + 時間（施工進度規劃與模擬）
5D → + 成本（預算管理與變更估算）
6D → + 永續性（能耗分析、綠建築評估）
7D → + 設施管理（設備資產管理、維護記錄）
8D → + 安全管理（施工安全分析）

生物製藥廠房最關鍵的BIM應用：
- 管線碰撞檢測（Clash Detection）：3D
- 施工序列驗證（Construction Sequence）：4D
- 驗證計畫整合（Commissioning Schedule）：4D
- 設備維護資訊（Equipment Maintenance Data）：7D

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO在建設或擴建廠房時採用BIM，可以帶來以下具體效益：施工前消除管線碰撞（Clash Detection）可節省大量施工返工費用；4D施工模擬可確保在不影響現有生產的情況下規劃擴建序列（特別重要：在已運作廠房旁邊擴建時，施工粉塵和噪音必須嚴格控制）；7D設施管理模型可在廠房交付後直接用於設備維護管理，提高設施管理效率。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. BIM的「Clash Detection（碰撞檢測）」功能在生物製藥廠房設計中為何特別重要？請舉出兩個生物製藥廠房特有的管線衝突場景。
  2. 生物製藥廠房可能需要15個以上的設計專業，這些專業之間的協調挑戰是什麼？BIM如何幫助解決這些挑戰？

本章重點回顧 Chapter Summary

  • 由內而外設計（Inside-Out Design）：生物製藥廠房設計從製程需求出發，先確定設備、流程、清潔分級，再推演建築結構——這是與一般建築設計最根本的差異。
  • 三大設計驅動因素：功能導向風險評估、運作經濟效率、彈性/適應性/可擴展性，三者需在整個設計週期中持續平衡。
  • 廠內流動管理（Flow Management）：人員、物料（上游→下游）、廢棄物、樣品六大流的設計，不只是操作程序問題，更必須通過建築空間布局來「強制執行」。
  • Greenfield vs Brownfield：改建廠址（Brownfield）看似省錢，但隱藏的結構、公用設施、法規升級問題可能使總成本超過新建，必須在前期進行徹底的盡職調查。
  • 模組化設計的關鍵決策時機：模組化建設的決策必須在設計最前期（概念階段）做出，且需選定承包商參與詳細設計，才能真正享受其成本和工期優勢。
  • 生物製藥廠房獨特的結構挑戰：大型生物反應器的高空間需求（4-8m淨高）、大型槽體的集中荷重、超大結構跨距（30-40m）、以及潔淨室中不得有結構伸縮縫——這些是小分子藥廠不存在的特殊設計考量。
  • 施工期間的前瞻性設計：樓板加強、預留公用設施空間、設置可拆卸牆板——這些初期多花的小錢，是廠房30年壽命中最划算的投資。
  • 法規、保險雙重要求：保險公司的MFL要求往往比政府建築法規更嚴格；生物性廢水需要特殊的收集和評估設施——兩者都應在設計初期就與相關方確認。
  • BIM是現代複雜廠房設計的必備工具：15個以上設計專業的協調、「先建後建」的虛擬建造驗證、以及從施工到運維的全生命週期資訊整合，BIM讓這一切變得可能。
8

Chapter 8: Mechanical

機械系統 | p97-p111

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 6 (2nd Ed.): Biopharmaceutical Manufacturing Facilities | p97 - p111

本章學習目標

  • 理解機械、電氣、管線與防火（MEP）系統在生物製藥廠房設計中的核心角色，以及風險評估框架的應用方式
  • 掌握 HVAC（暖通空調系統）設計中生物安全等級（BSL）、動能、生物圍堵與生物安全等各風險因子的評估方法，並能分辨各因子對氣流策略的影響
  • 熟悉 ISO 14644-1 潔淨室分級標準，以及 ISPE / EU GMP / FDA / PIC/S 監管等級對照關係與換氣次數（ACH）設計範圍
  • 認識生物製藥廠特有的防火與電氣考量，包含可燃溶劑處理、潔淨滅火劑系統，以及細胞培養製程對不斷電電源（UPS）和緊急備用電力的迫切需求
8.1 Introduction — 導論

原文內容 Original Text

Mechanical, Electrical, Plumbing, and Fire Protection (MEP) systems should be designed to meet local codes and regulations and to satisfy both good engineering practice and business needs.

The utilities needed for biopharmaceutical facilities are common to many manufacturing facilities, and include:

  • Lighting
  • Power
  • Cooling water
  • Process water
  • Fire protection
  • Compressed air
  • Other gases

The design of HVAC and other supporting systems specific to biopharmaceutical facilities relies on the evaluation of factors pertaining to the risk of product contamination or adulteration by the system or the ambient environment. In addition, the design should consider the sometimes conflicting risks to worker or public health from the product or process.

The factors to be evaluated may be divided into two groups:

  1. Those risk factors that add to the risk of product contamination
  2. Those protection factors that provide layers of protection against contamination

The combination of risk and protection factors determines the design of the facility. Example risk and protection factors include:

  • Product Risk Factors:
    • Kinetic energy of the process (ability to produce aerosols)
    • Biocontainment (related to pathogenic or hazardous nature of organisms or genetic material)
    • Biosafety (related to biocontainment with regard to operator exposure)
    • Hazardous and flammable material handling
    • Product potency
    • Material sensitivity to molecular contaminants
    • Material ability to support microbial growth
  • Business Risk Factors:
    • Resource conservation and sustainability
    • Product value
    • Product medical criticality
  • Protection Factors:
    • Process closure
    • Process containment (use of micro environments)
    • Downstream processing (virus reduction and removal of other impurities and contaminants)
    • Pre and post-viral separation
    • Gowning
    • Classification
    • General arrangement and physical construction

A risk management approach is usually applied to these factors and may be formal, informal (or both). Risk mitigation approaches should be concomitant with the level of identified risk and the acceptable level of operator exposure. The risk to product quality should be assessed, appropriate mitigations designed, and the risks tracked. These tasks may be performed by the MEP engineering team.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

MEP (Mechanical, Electrical, Plumbing and Fire Protection) 機械電氣管線防火系統：這四個子系統合稱 MEP，是廠房建築工程的骨幹。在生物製藥廠中，MEP 不只是「讓建築能用」的基礎設施，更直接影響產品品質、操作員安全，以及生物圍堵的完整性。

HVAC (Heating, Ventilation, Air Conditioning) 暖通空調系統：在所有 MEP 系統中，HVAC 對生物製藥最為關鍵，因為它同時影響：產品微生物污染風險、操作員生物安全暴露、以及對外部環境的生物圍堵。

風險因子 vs 保護因子的雙向框架：ISPE Vol.6 的設計哲學是先識別每個製程步驟的風險來源，再疊加對應的保護層，最終決定空間等級與 HVAC 需求。這與 ICH Q9 品質風險管理的架構完全一致。

比喻說明 Analogy

設計生物製藥廠的 HVAC，就像設計一棟醫院的感染控制系統——既要防止外部病原體進入手術室（保護產品），也要防止醫院裡的病菌擴散到走廊（生物圍堵），還得避免醫護人員被患者的傳染病感染（生物安全）。三個目標有時相互衝突，需要整合式風險評估。

重點提示 Key Notes

生物製藥 vs 傳統製藥的關鍵差異：傳統製藥 HVAC 設計的主要目標是「保護產品不受環境污染」；生物製藥多了兩個獨特挑戰——生物圍堵（biocontainment）防止活生物體外洩危害公眾，以及生物安全（biosafety）防止操作員被製程中的病原體感染。這使得 HVAC 設計必須同時滿足三個有時相互矛盾的目標。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼同一個製程空間，可能既需要「正壓」（保護產品）又需要「負壓」（生物圍堵）？在什麼情況下這兩個需求會同時存在，應如何解決？
  2. 列舉三個屬於「保護因子」的設計策略，並說明每個策略如何降低污染風險。
8.2 Mechanical Systems and Environmental Controls — 機械系統與環境控制

原文內容 Original Text

Each step in the manufacture of a biopharmaceutical drug substance should be evaluated for risk and protection factors to determine the type of mechanical systems and environmental controls required to assure both a safe product and a safe work environment.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

本節的關鍵邏輯是：逐步驟評估（step-by-step assessment）。不同製程步驟的風險輪廓差異極大——細胞培養（上游）的主要風險是外部污染進入，而病毒去活化步驟（下游）的主要風險是活病毒外洩。因此，同一棟廠房的不同區域，可能需要截然不同的 HVAC 策略。

8.2.1 Applying Risk Tools to Classification and HVAC Design

原文內容 Original Text

HVAC design can impact basic parameters of the work environment and emissions to the outside, including:

  • Temperature
  • Pressure
  • Moisture content
  • Particulate content
  • Molecular (contaminant) content

The capabilities of an HVAC system can impact product contamination risk factors. Risk factors also can impact the need for the HVAC system to enhance or provide environmental parameters to support product quality.

An assessment of the impact of the environment on the process is required in order to understand the environmental control requirements of each space within a facility appropriately. During this risk assessment, product risk factors specific to each stage of a process should be considered and the effect on HVAC design should be identified.

8.2.1.1 Kinetic Energy

Process steps which add significant energy to a culture or product present an increased risk of generating aerosols and cross-contaminating other products or increasing operator exposure. Examples of processes and equipment that, if breached, may allow product to become airborne include positive pressure and pumped transfers (for chromatography, filtration, or movement of material), centrifugation, and pressurized reactor vessels. Typical mitigations in areas of high aerosol risk include increasing air exchange rate to dilute aerosols in the space and enhanced filtration to remove aerosols from the airstream.

8.2.1.2 Biocontainment (Related to Hazardous or Pathogenic Nature of Organisms or Genetic Material)

Biocontainment requires the prevention of the escape of airborne organisms from a space to protect public health. When assessing the biocontainment risk, the probability of the material becoming airborne should be considered. Liquids or solids will need added energy (e.g., by pumping) to allow the material to become airborne.

The need for biocontainment can drive risk mitigation approaches such as:

  • Primary process containment or closure
  • Secondary containment isolation or facilities
  • Treatment of the exhaust air from a space (e.g., scrubbing, chemical or thermal deactivation, or filtration)
  • Negative pressurization of spaces to prevent accidental emissions
  • Terminal filtration of supply air to prevent emission through the supply ductwork in the case of fan failure
  • Dedicated air handling equipment

Filtration is a frequently used treatment for exhaust air with single and double HEPA filters used to help provide assurance of containment. A single properly installed HEPA filter can provide a greater than 4 log reduction in airborne pathogens. The need for biocontainment also may drive redundancy in HVAC systems to assure that pressure reversals and flow stoppages do not occur.

Biocontainment should not drive decisions relating to the use of recirculation or once-through ventilation.

8.2.1.3 Biosafety (Similar to Biocontainment — With Regard to Operator Exposure)

Biosafety requires the containment of airborne organisms within a space. The need for biosafety can drive risk mitigation approaches such as:

  • Secondary containment isolation or facilities
  • Treatment of the recirculated air from a space (e.g., filtration)
  • Negative pressurization of spaces to prevent accidental emissions
  • Terminal filtration of supply air to prevent emission through supply ductwork in the case of fan failure
  • Dedicated air handling equipment
  • Once-through ventilation

Filtration is a frequently used treatment for recirculated air with single and double HEPA filters used to help provide assurance of reduction of airborne pathogens. A single properly installed HEPA filter can provide a greater than 4 log reduction in airborne pathogens. Where isolators are used, the need for biocontainment also may drive redundancy in HVAC system, to assure that primary containment is preserved.

When assessing this risk of potential airborne contaminants, the probability of the material becoming airborne should be considered. Liquids or solids will need energy added (e.g., by pumping) to allow the material to become airborne.

The quantitative reduction in potential airborne contaminants provided by filtration should be evaluated as part of the risk assessment. At high levels of biosafety (e.g., BSL-3 and 4) once-through ventilation is frequently used. Although HEPA filters are effective against microorganisms, increasing levels of biosafety discourages the use of recirculation, favoring once-through ventilation.

8.2.1.4 Hazardous and Flammable Material Handling

Hazardous or flammable material handling requires dilution of the hazard within a space and containment of airborne hazards to prevent fugitive emissions from escaping a space. Hazardous or flammable material handling can drive risk mitigation approaches such as:

  • Primary process containment closure
  • Treatment of the exhaust air from a space (e.g., scrubbing, adsorption, thermal oxidation, or filtration)
  • Negative pressurization of spaces to prevent accidental emissions
  • Redundancy to assure pressurization in all conditions
  • Lower Explosive Limit (LEL) detection
  • Deflagration containment and venting

Fume scrubbing or carbon adsorption may be used to treat exhaust air. Hazardous or flammable material handling also may drive redundancy in HVAC systems to assure that dilution of contaminants and pressurization are not lost.

The use of hazardous or flammable materials usually discourages the use of recirculation, favoring once-through ventilation. When assessing this risk, the actual probability of the material becoming airborne should be considered. Flammable liquids and some other hazardous materials may have a high vapor pressure, emitting vapors without added energy; some liquids or solids will need to have energy added (e.g., by pumping) to allow the material to become airborne.

8.2.1.5 Product Potency

The handling of potent products has the same impact as hazardous material handling; however, the actual concentration of the potent product at the particular stage of the process should be considered. The potency of biological products usually increases as they move downstream through purification. The potency of an API is usually reduced during formulation, as it is mixed with excipients.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

動能（Kinetic Energy）與氣溶膠（Aerosol）風險：任何對培養液或產品施加機械能的操作（離心、加壓傳輸、攪拌等），都可能將液滴霧化為氣溶膠。氣溶膠比液滴更危險，因為它能懸浮在空氣中長時間漂移，穿越房間甚至進入其他空間。高動能區域的 HVAC 設計核心是：加大換氣次數（ACH）稀釋濃度 + 強化排氣過濾。

生物圍堵（Biocontainment）vs 生物安全（Biosafety）的細微差異：

  • Biocontainment（生物圍堵）：防止活性生物體/基因物質從設施內逃逸到外部環境，保護公眾安全。重點是「向外圍堵」，通常需要負壓。
  • Biosafety（生物安全）：防止活性生物體在設施內暴露給操作員，保護員工安全。重點是「向內圍堵」，同樣需要負壓。
  • 兩者都指向負壓設計，但控制的邊界和目標不同。

比喻說明 Analogy

雙層 HEPA 排氣過濾 = 核電廠排氣過濾的製藥版本：核電廠為防止輻射微粒外洩，排氣管道裝設多道過濾器；BSL-2+ 以上的生物製藥廠排氣系統，也裝設單層或雙層 HEPA 過濾器，確保含有活性微生物的空氣在排出前已被充分清潔。一道 HEPA 即可提供 >4 log（99.99%）的病原體去除率，是非常強的保護屏障。

一次通過氣流（Single-pass / once-through air）：就像醫院手術室——空氣進來用一次就排掉，不循環回去。這是高等級生物安全區域（BSL-3, 4）的標準做法，代價是能耗極高，因為每一立方米空氣都需要重新加熱或冷卻。

重點提示 Key Notes

LEL（爆炸下限）偵測的重要性：生物製藥下游純化普遍使用大量乙醇（Ethanol）和異丙醇（IPA）作為層析管柱的沖提液（eluent）。這些有機溶劑的蒸氣在特定濃度範圍內即會形成爆炸混合物。LEL 偵測器是強制性的安全設備，一旦偵測到超過 10~20% LEL 就需啟動警報和排氣應急程序。

產品效能（Potency）沿製程遞增：生物製藥的有效成分在下游純化過程中被濃縮，效能遞增。這意味著下游製程空間對空氣的潛在暴露危害更高——即使少量氣溶膠也可能造成操作員嚴重暴露，需要更嚴格的圍堵措施。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 離心機（centrifuge）在生物製藥廠被視為「高動能設備」。如果一台離心機在使用中發生密封洩漏，列出三個可能的 HVAC 減緩措施。
  2. 為什麼「生物圍堵不應驅動循環或一次通過通風的決策」，但「生物安全可以驅動一次通過通風」？兩者的根本差異是什麼？
8.2.1.6 — 8.2.1.12 Pre/Post-Viral Separation, Process Closure & Classification

原文內容 Original Text

8.2.1.6 Pre- and Post-Viral Separation

Processes normally use several process steps to reduce the concentration of organisms or DNA/RNA and "virus-like particles" from a culture. In the case of vaccines, the pathogens may not be completely removed, but an acceptable level of inactivation may be achieved by a similar series of steps. The continuous nature of these processes may make "pre-viral" and "post-viral" steps difficult to determine precisely; however, a point in the process where virus reduction is adequate to justify separation should be identified.

Air systems that serve upstream open processing areas (e.g., bioreactor and harvest) are usually separated from downstream processes (e.g., purification) at the point at which an acceptable reduction is achieved. Air systems are usually separated with the intent of reducing the chance of contamination of the final product; however, this may not be scientifically supportable.

Using closed processing during pre- and post-viral separation can minimize the need to use HVAC systems for separation of these process stages.

The ability of the product or organisms to become airborne and the ability of treatment steps to remove viruses or virus-like particles should be considered.

8.2.1.7 Product Sensitivity to Molecular Contaminants

Open processes may be susceptible to ambient contamination by particulate or molecular contaminants, such as copper or zinc, which can denature products. This may impact HVAC material and filtration selections.

8.2.1.8 Product Ability to Support Microbial Growth

The greater the ability of the product or culture to sustain microbial growth, the greater the risk and associated drive toward classified space or process closure. A frequently used mitigation, required to protect product, is supply filtration with single HEPA filtration providing a very high level of protection.

8.2.1.9 Process Closure

The more layers of closure (separation from the room environment) a process has, the less impact the room environment normally has on product quality. This can drive a reduction in the:

  • Classification of spaces
  • Required contamination and cross contamination control
  • Need for exhaust of any hazardous gases, vapors, or dusts
  • Once-thru air supply

Process closure also can provide primary containment to address issues of biocontainment and biosafety.

8.2.1.10 Downstream Processing

Bioprocesses typically move from a clean or sterile media to an aseptic culture to a harvested solution that is contaminated with cellular material and other effluvia. These processes isolate desirable proteins and discard undesirable proteins and organisms from a culture. Downstream stages of processing, which are closer to the final API state are typically more sensitive to contamination than are early stages, see Figure 8.1.

[Figure 8.1: Sensitivity of Contamination to Processing Stage — referenced in source, image not available]

8.2.1.11 Gowning

The level of gowning can have a significant impact on room contamination and particulate/microbial performance. Personnel can be significant contributors to space contamination, due to the shedding of both particulate and viable organisms.

The higher the level of gowning, the lower the demand for diluting airflow to offset the particulate and bioburden from operators. This becomes increasingly important as the space classification increases. For further information on gowning and its relationship to space classification, see the ISPE Good Practice Guide: HVAC [58].

8.2.1.12 Classification

Manufacturing environments should be controlled in a manner appropriate to the process and product being handled. Where the risk of product quality being impacted by the ambient environment is unacceptable; the environment is typically identified as "high risk" or "critical" and an enhanced level of environmental control is usually required.

Classification of critical environments in biotech and vaccine facilities according to airborne particulate concentration, as outlined in ISO 14644-1 and ISO 14644-2, is intended to reduce this risk to product quality. While there is no direct correlation between total particulate count and microbiological purity, it is generally accepted that reductions in airborne particulate should result in reductions in airborne colony forming units.

Regulations further enhance these particulate requirements by setting limits for the expected and tested airborne particle count and airborne microbial counts in sterile product facilities. Although there is no specific requirement for formal classification of spaces for non-sterile product according to ISO 14644-1, the latest draft of the EudraLex Annex 2 suggests that the principles of space classification outlined in Annex 1 (for sterile product) should be applied to biological product production as appropriate. This is also consistent with historical and risk-based practices which have typically employed classified spaces for both sterile and non-sterile therapeutic protein and vaccine manufacture.

Process closure (see Chapter 3 of this Guide) also can be a significant driver of environmental classification. Generally speaking, the fewer layers of closure a process has, the greater the need to perform it in a classified space. The relationship between process risk of contamination and layers of protection (e.g., from process closure) requires a flexible, multi-dimensional, approach to classification of spaces. For further information, see Appendix 1.

Historical approaches to area classification were usually more prescriptive.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

病毒分離點（Pre/Post-Viral Separation Point）：生物製藥製程中，有一個關鍵的「病毒分離點」——在這個點之前，製程液含有活性病毒或病毒樣粒子（來自細胞培養）；之後，通過病毒去活化/去除步驟，病毒濃度降至可接受水平。HVAC 系統設計需要識別這個分離點，並在該點前後使用不同的空調系統，防止含病毒的上游空氣污染已「清潔」的下游產品。

製程密閉性（Process Closure）的槓桿效應：這是本章最重要的設計原則之一。製程密閉程度每提升一個層次（例如從開放製程升級到密閉管路），就可以相應降低環境分級要求——這意味著可以降低 HVAC 複雜度、減少潔淨室面積、大幅節省能源和建設成本。生物製藥廠廣泛採用單次使用（SU）生物反應器和密閉傳輸系統，部分原因正是為了利用這個槓桿。

ISO 14644-1 分級系統：以每立方公尺空氣中的微粒濃度定義 ISO Class 1 至 9，數字越小越潔淨。監管層面，EU GMP 使用 Grade A/B/C/D，PIC/S 系統近似，FDA 使用 ISO 5/6/7/8，而 ISPE 提出了 Grade 5-8 + CNC+ / CNC / UC 的統一橋接系統。

比喻說明 Analogy

病毒分離點 = 污水處理廠的特殊版本：城市污水處理廠在排放前必須殺滅病菌；生物製藥廠的病毒去活化步驟就是製程中的「殺菌站」。在「殺菌站」上游的空調系統，必須與下游的完全隔離——這就像污水管道絕對不能與飲用水管道相連。

換衣程度 vs 換氣量的取捨：就像廚師戴帽戴手套能大幅減少食物落菌風險一樣，操作員穿著更嚴密的無塵衣，對環境排放的微粒和微生物會顯著減少，從而讓 HVAC 系統不需要那麼高的換氣次數（ACH）來稀釋污染。高級別分級空間的換衣規程嚴格，正是「用換衣換取低 ACH」的工程取捨。

重點提示 Key Notes

EudraLex Annex 2 對非無菌生物製品的分級要求：傳統上，ISO 14644-1 的分級系統主要針對無菌產品。但 Annex 2 的最新草案指出，即使是非無菌生物製品的生產，也應參照 Annex 1（無菌產品）的分級原則執行。這對疫苗和重組蛋白製造商影響深遠，意味著更高的合規投入。

下游製程對污染更敏感：直覺上可能認為「越到最後越乾淨」，但 Figure 8.1 顯示的邏輯是：越接近最終 API 狀態，產品的純化程度越高，但也越沒有緩衝能力——一旦污染，沒有後續的去除步驟可以補救。因此下游區域（純化、配製）雖然不再含有活性病毒，但對環境污染的敏感度反而更高。

實務應用 Practical Application

一家 CDMO 正在設計一棟新的生物製藥廠（生產治療用 mAb），評估是否採用全密閉單次使用（SU）生物反應器系統（相比傳統開放式不鏽鋼生物反應器）：

  • 製程密閉性提升的好處：SU 系統幾乎消除了人工操作與環境空氣的接觸點，可將培養區（上游）從 ISO 7（Grade B）降至 ISO 8（Grade C），大幅節省 HVAC 設計複雜度與能耗
  • HVAC 成本節省：ISO 7 要求 30-60 ACH，ISO 8 僅需 15-20 ACH——換氣量減半即代表 AHU 機組容量、管道尺寸、能耗均可顯著縮減
  • 建議：採用 SU 系統並結合密閉傳輸，可實現分級降等（classification downgrade），是現代生物製藥廠設計的主流策略

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一個 mAb 生產廠的細胞培養（bioreactor）區域，如果使用完全密閉的 SU 生物反應器，其環境分級可以從 ISO 7 降至哪個等級？根據本節的哪個原則？
  2. 為什麼「下游純化區域對污染的敏感性高於上游培養區域」？請從製程邏輯和監管角度各說明一個理由。
8.2.2 Classification Standards, Tables & Typical HVAC Parameters

原文內容 Original Text

The ISO standard 14644-1 and 14644-2 is designed to support a number of industries classifying spaces according to the concentration of airborne particulate in a number of size categories. Only some of these size categories are of interest in the biopharmaceutical and vaccine facilities.

The ISO standard only describes a system for categorizing or classifying cleanrooms by particle size and concentration (count per cubic meter). It addresses multiple particle size ranges and operational states, but it does not specify which particle sizes are of importance or in which state they should be measured.

Table 8.1: ISO 14644-1 Air Quality Classes (particles per cubic meter by size)

Notes: Values in parenthesis are US Customary Class per USP and defunct FS 209. Yellow highlighted values are recognized by all regulatory authorities. Green highlighted values are applied for products sold outside the US.

Regulations and regulatory guidance documents normally outline the particle sizes of concern and the operational state in which they are to be measured. In addition, these regulations establish action limits for airborne viable organisms.

Table 8.2 outlines the relationship between ISO classifications and several regulatory systems of classification, including an ISPE system which is intended to bridge other regulatory systems and designations.

Table 8.2: Environmental Control Requirements

Notes: Values may be averages. EU and PIC/S require measurement of particles at 0.5 µm and 5 µm; the US requires 0.5 µm. Samples from Grade 5 areas should normally show no viable organisms. Recovery from the "In Operation" to the "At Rest" state should be verified to occur within 15 to 20 minutes for ISPE grades 6, 7, and 8. "At Rest" figures support Recovery and Static Room Classification testing — maintenance of these levels during idle periods is not intended.

The level of space classification drives both airflows and filtration directly. All other factors being equal, cleaner spaces (lower number classification) require greater airflow and higher grades of filtration.

Classifications of CNC, CNC+ (and/or ISO 9) can usually be achieved with high efficiency non-HEPA filtration (e.g., MERV 14/15) filters. These filters can be mounted in the Air Handling Unit (AHU) in lieu of a terminal location.

Grade 8 (ISO 8 in operation) classification also can be achieved using high efficiency non-HEPA filters; however, both regulation and industry practice suggest that HEPAs should be employed for all sterile operations, starting at ISO 8.

The greater airflow in cleaner spaces may be expressed in terms of the ventilation rate (or Air Change (AC) rate). While this measure has been dropped by IEST and others, the USP cites air change rates from 20 AC/hr for ISO-8 to 100 AC/hr for ISO-5. This approach is also embodied in the FDA 2004 Sterile Guide, which contains a suggestion that 20 AC/hr should be adequate for ISO-8 and suggests that cleaner spaces should have higher ventilation rates.

However, considering only the ventilation rate neglects the correction for the mixing factor (K). The mixing factor is a measure of room design performance. In addition, considering only the air change rate in the design of cleanrooms fails to account for the following fundamental factors:

  • Contaminant Sources:
    • Occupants (people): Population, Gowning, Activity level
    • Process: Equipment, Materials
    • Contamination Ingress: Through facility fabric (cracks in walls, ceilings, etc.), Through doorways
  • Configuration:
    • Architecture
    • HVAC system layout
    • Room distribution
  • Engineering Controls and Mitigations:
    • Local exhaust ventilation at generation points
    • Containment of generated particles
    • Room performance (ventilation effectiveness)
    • Pressurization/direction of airflow
    • Supply filtration
    • Airlocking

When using the ventilation rate principal to set air volumes (flowrates) in classified spaces, airflow should be increased as the classification becomes more stringent. However, the air volume required should be adjusted to accommodate the factors above. Sophisticated cleanroom airflow calculators and Computational Fluid Dynamic (CFD) modeling can help designers to achieve effective and efficient designs that relate directly to the process design and architectural configuration.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

分級系統對照一覽（記憶捷徑）：

  • Grade 5 / ISO 5 / EU Grade A：最高等級，無菌充填區，<1 cfu/m³，靜層流
  • Grade 7 / ISO 7 / EU Grade B：高等級背景，支援 Grade A 操作
  • Grade 8 / ISO 8 / EU Grade C：一般無菌支援區
  • CNC+ / EU Grade D：受控非分級（Controlled Not Classified Plus）
  • CNC / UC：一般製造或倉儲區

換氣次數（ACH = Air Changes per Hour）參考值：這些數字是設計起點，不是固定規範，必須依污染源分析調整：

  • ISO 5（Grade A）：通常為單向層流（UDAF），以流速定義（0.45 m/s），非 ACH
  • ISO 7（Grade B background）：30–60 ACH
  • ISO 8（Grade C）：15–20 ACH（非無菌），HEPA 空間建議更高
  • CNC+：6–15 ACH
  • CNC：6–10 ACH

公式與計算 Formula

換氣次數計算（ACH）：
ACH = Q_supply (m³/hr) / V_room (m³)

混合因子（K factor）修正：
有效 ACH = 實際 ACH / K
其中 K 值通常在 1.0（完美混合）至 10（極差混合）之間
設計目標通常假設 K = 2~4

CFD（計算流體力學）可幫助確認實際 K 值

舉例：一個 100 m³ 的 ISO 7 空間
目標 ACH = 45（中間值）
Q_supply = 45 × 100 = 4,500 m³/hr = 1.25 m³/s
若 K = 2，實際需求 ACH = 90，
Q_supply = 9,000 m³/hr
→ 使用 CFD 優化氣流分佈是節省能源的關鍵

重點提示 Key Notes

「僅依賴 ACH」的局限性：ACH 是個粗略的設計工具，忽略了三大關鍵因素：(1) 污染源的強度和分佈；(2) 氣流分佈效率（K 因子）；(3) 補氣方向與壓力梯度。一個 ACH 較低但氣流設計優良的房間，實際性能可能優於高 ACH 但氣流死角多的房間。現代設計越來越依賴 CFD 模擬來驗證。

「At Rest」vs「In Operation」的雙態測試：EU GMP 要求潔淨室在兩種狀態下達到不同的粒子限度。「At Rest」限度更嚴（較低粒子數），因為沒有操作人員和設備產生污染；「In Operation」允許較高限度，但監管更關注這個狀態。Recovery 測試（15-20 分鐘內從「In Operation」狀態恢復到「At Rest」限度）是 HVAC 性能的重要驗證指標。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一個 ISO 7（Grade 7）潔淨室在「In Operation」狀態測得 0.5 µm 粒子數為 400,000 particles/m³。根據 Table 8.2，此數值是否超出限度？超出多少倍？
  2. 為什麼 CFD 模擬對現代生物製藥廠 HVAC 設計越來越重要？列舉兩個使用 CFD 可以優化的設計參數。
8.2.1.13–8.2.1.16 Sustainability, Product Value & Physical Construction | 8.2.2 Typical HVAC Parameters

原文內容 Original Text

8.2.1.13 Resource Conservation and Sustainability Targets

As much as 60% of the energy consumed by an average pharmaceutical facility is dedicated to the HVAC systems. Optimizing the selected critical parameters and acceptance criteria for HVAC can provide a significant reduction in both cost and greenhouse gas emissions.

The design of highly efficient systems, employing a few core principles, can lead to further reductions and achievement of sustainability goals. The core principles for energy reduction include:

  • Classification of a space should be based on real risk. Over-classifying spaces should be avoided.
  • Over-filtering should be avoided. A single HEPA filter can provide a greater than 4 log reduction in airborne contaminants.
  • Where operations are not continuous, an idle mode should be considered to reduce airflow (and possibly relax temperature requirements) whenever an area is idle or when no open operations are present.
  • Consideration of advanced control techniques such as discharge air dewpoint control and adaptive static pressure reset.
  • Consideration of use of recirculated air wherever practical.
  • Consideration of heat recovery from exhaust streams.
  • Consideration of use of once-through air systems for heat rejection during winter months.
  • Consideration of utilizing local recirculation systems separate from primary pressurization air to allow recirculation to be shut down during idle periods.

8.2.1.14 Product Value

As product value increases, business drivers may push design toward a higher level of space classification to minimize the risk of a lost batch due to environmental contamination or due to an inconclusive investigation into potential contamination.

8.2.1.15 Product Medical Criticality

An increased medical need for a product may push design toward a higher level of space classification to minimize the risk of a lost batch due to environmental contamination or due to an inconclusive investigation into potential contamination.

8.2.1.16 General Arrangement and Physical Construction

The physical arrangement of spaces and details of construction can have a significant impact on HVAC system design. The adjacency of spaces with different classifications and biosafety needs can drive pressurization schemes and outside air usage. Similarly, the use of tight space construction can minimize the use of outside air for pressurization while maintaining good environmental control. Typical elements of concern include:

  • Doors and door seals
  • Walls
  • Ceilings

8.2.2 Other Typical HVAC Design Parameters

Tables 8.3 and 8.4 offer typical practice for selected design parameters; they are not intended to be definitive nor to provide minimum acceptable practice:

8.2.2.1 Room Conditions

Table 8.3: Typical Room Condition Ranges

Note: Conceptual air change rates are for the purpose of estimating only and are derived from previously published documents. Actual airflows should be calculated during the design process.

8.2.2.2 Biosafety

Table 8.4: Recommended Design Conditions for Biosafety Levels

Gaseous decontamination can be applied to most biopharmaceutical and all vaccine processes. For gaseous decontamination, exposed HVAC ductwork should be compatible with the decontamination means. The HVAC system also should be arranged to allow isolation of gaseous decontamination spaces or recirculation of the decontaminating gas in order to assure good distribution.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

能源消耗中 HVAC 佔 60% 的含義：製藥廠是能源密集型設施，而其中 HVAC 是最大的單一能源消耗者。這直接轉化為巨大的運營成本（OpEx）和碳排放。在廠房設計生命週期內，過度分類（over-classification）造成的累積能源浪費可能遠超建設成本節省。

「待機模式（Idle Mode）」的概念：當潔淨室沒有開放操作進行時（如換班、假日），可以臨時降低換氣次數（通常降至全速的 20-50%），待恢復生產前再升回至全速，並以 Recovery 測試確認達到規格。這一技術稱為「setback mode」或「idle mode」，是現代 HVAC 節能設計的核心策略之一。

生物安全等級（BSL）與 HVAC 要求的遞進關係：從 BSL-1 到 BSL-4，壓力、排氣過濾、循環方式、氣鎖要求全面遞增：

  • BSL-1/GLSP：正壓，允許循環，無特殊過濾
  • BSL-2：負壓，允許循環，氣鎖「建議」
  • BSL-2+：負壓，HEPA 過濾（選配），局部循環，氣鎖「建議」
  • BSL-3：強負壓，強制 HEPA，100% 新鮮風（不循環），多道氣鎖
  • BSL-4：全封閉負壓，雙層 HEPA，100% 新鮮風，多道強制氣鎖

比喻說明 Analogy

「不要過度分類」= 開飯館不需要手術室等級的無菌廚房：如果廚師的食材不需要在滅菌條件下處理，強制使用 ISO 5 潔淨廚房只是浪費電費。同理，如果一個生物製藥製程步驟使用完全密閉的設備，將其所在空間分級為 ISO 7 而非 ISO 8，只是白白多花換氣費用——這就是 ISPE 強調「基於真實風險分級」的本意。

HVAC 的 Idle Mode = 辦公室的空調下班自動降溫：現代智慧大樓在下班後自動降低空調設定點，節省夜間能耗；潔淨室的 Idle Mode 邏輯相同——無人作業時降低換氣量，節省大量電費，只需確保「開工前恢復到規格狀態」即可。

重點提示 Key Notes

大多數生物製藥廠的 BSL 等級是 GLSP 或 BSL-1/2：雖然 BSL-3 和 BSL-4 在學術文獻和監管指南中常被討論，但商業生物製藥（mAb、疫苗）製造廠絕大多數在 GLSP（適宜大規模生產的生物體）或 BSL-1/BSL-2 條件下操作。BSL-2+ 適用於含有條件致病性元素的製程，BSL-3/4 在商業規模製藥中非常罕見。理解 Table 8.4 有助於在設計新廠時與監管機構討論設施適當性。

溫度控制對細胞培養的重要性：Table 8.3 中 Grade 7/8 的溫度控制範圍（±3–5°C）看似寬鬆，但要注意：這是房間的溫度控制；生物反應器內的細胞培養溫度（通常是 37°C ± 0.5°C）是由設備本身的夾套控制，而非環境控制。HVAC 環境溫度主要影響操作員舒適度和設備散熱。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 設施節能設計案例：一家台灣 CDMO 新建生物製藥廠，年生產 200 個批次的 mAb，每批製程週期 14 天。廠房 HVAC 設計可以採用以下節能措施組合：

  • Idle Mode：週末停工期間（每週 2 天）將 ISO 7 區域換氣量降至 30%，每年節省約 20-25% 的 HVAC 能耗
  • 熱回收（Heat Recovery）：排氣熱交換器回收排氣能量，預熱送風，在台灣氣候條件下可減少 15-20% 冷熱負荷
  • 精準分級（Avoid Over-classification）：全密閉 SU 生物反應器區域設計為 ISO 8 而非 ISO 7，每年節省換氣能耗約 35%

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 根據 Table 8.4，BSL-2 和 BSL-2+ 在排氣過濾和氣鎖要求上有何差異？在實際設計中，這些差異如何反映在廠房建設成本上？
  2. 一家新廠計畫生產 HPV 疫苗（使用 E. coli 表達系統，非致病性菌株）。根據本節，應設計為哪個生物安全等級（BSL），理由為何？
8.3 Fire Protection — 防火系統

原文內容 Original Text

Attributes of fire protection systems specific to biopharmaceutical and vaccine facilities include:

  • Use of cleanable sprinkler heads that are compatible with cleaning agents. Sealing of concealed heads should be considered for reducing risk of accidental release and increasing the capacity for cleaning. These heads can also minimize air leakage.
  • Use of pre-action systems to minimize the risk of accidental release in cleanrooms and biosafety areas.
  • Collection of sprinkler discharge may be required in manufacturing and biosafety areas. The collected discharge may require abatement prior to discharge.
  • Dry chemical extinguishing systems are typically only needed where volatile organic solvents are used.
  • Clean agent extinguishing systems (gaseous suppression) may also be used in high risk/high value areas, to assure prevention of contamination of product by the fire extinguishing agent:
    • Clean agent extinguishing systems normally require HVAC isolation, room seal testing. Any means of egress and notifications should be considered. Appropriately qualified personnel should be consulted when employing these systems.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Pre-action 消防系統（預作動系統）：傳統濕式灑水系統在灑水頭熔解時立即噴水。Pre-action 系統需要兩個觸發條件才噴水（通常是煙霧偵測 + 高溫熔斷），大幅降低「誤噴」的機率。在潔淨室或生物安全區域，誤噴水會造成：(1) 批次損失（水污染）；(2) 廠房停機清潔（Recovery 驗證需時數天）；(3) 生物安全事件（若含活性生物體的液體被噴灑散布）。因此 pre-action 是生物製藥廠的標準選擇。

Clean agent（潔淨滅火劑）系統：使用氣態化學物質（如 FM-200、Novec 1230）滅火，不留殘留物，不污染產品。適用於高價值設備間（電腦機房、精密分析儀器區、高價值 API 存儲區）。

灑水排放的生物安全隱患：如果消防灑水系統在 BSL-2 以上的區域激活，噴出的水會混入含活性微生物的液體，產生的廢水必須當作生物危害廢液（biological waste）處理，需要滅活後才能排放——這就是「abatement prior to discharge」的含義。

比喻說明 Analogy

Pre-action 消防系統 = 雙重認證的保險箱：普通灑水頭像一把鎖，溫度到了就開；Pre-action 系統像一個需要密碼 + 鑰匙的保險箱——必須兩個條件同時滿足才啟動，大幅降低誤觸發機率。在動輒數百萬美元一批的生物製藥生產中，避免誤噴的代價絕對合理。

乾粉滅火系統的侷限性：乾粉是最便宜的滅火方式，但粉末殘留會污染 ISO 7/8 以上的潔淨室，需要極長時間清潔復原，因此只用於有大量有機溶劑（如乙醇槽）的倉儲或處理區域，而非生產潔淨室內。

重點提示 Key Notes

乙醇（Ethanol）和 IPA 在生物製藥下游的廣泛應用：蛋白質 A 管柱（Protein A chromatography）用水性緩衝液；但反相色譜（RP-HPLC）、病毒滅活（低 pH 加溶劑）、以及設備 70% IPA 消毒等步驟，都大量使用可燃有機溶劑。下游純化車間（DSP area）必須進行防爆設計評估（ATEX / hazardous area classification），包含 LEL 偵測器、防爆電氣設備、以及必要時的乾粉或 clean agent 滅火系統。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一個 BSL-2 的生物反應器間（約 200 m²）發生消防灑水系統激活（誤觸發），大量水噴入房間。請列出必須立即採取的三個應急措施，並說明理由。
  2. Clean agent（潔淨滅火劑）系統在使用時需要「HVAC 隔離」（HVAC isolation），為什麼？如果不隔離會發生什麼？
8.4 Electrical — 電氣系統

原文內容 Original Text

Attributes of electrical systems specific to biopharmaceutical and vaccine facilities include:

  • Cleanroom lighting that is fully sealed from the room side may be required for manufacturing areas. Top access should be considered to minimize the risk of contamination of these rooms.
  • Cleanroom phones and intercoms that are fully sealed from the room side are recommended for manufacturing areas.
  • It may be beneficial to seal all conduits and penetrations from the room side in manufacturing areas.
  • Within biosafety level 2+, 3, and 4 areas conduits and penetrations from the room side in manufacturing areas should be sealed.
  • Biopharmaceutical processes are typically wet and the use of NEMA 3R, 4, and 4X closures may be beneficial within manufacturing areas.
  • Within biosafety areas, NEMA 4X wiring devices and liquid tight conduit are recommended.
  • Backup power should be considered for all biological product facilities. Loss of power to bioreactors and processing equipment for more than a brief period can be catastrophic and result in the loss of batches. This is generally a business issue, rather than a GMP issue, but in cases of medical necessity the loss can be more than financial.
  • When evaluating the need for backup power, the need for HVAC during periods of power loss to assure environmental control should be considered. Qualification of the period that the facility is capable of maintaining conditions without active HVAC systems and a study of the sequencing of the restart of all systems upon the application of emergency power are recommended.
  • The transition back from emergency power to normal power also should be evaluated. Standard transfer switches make an "open" transition from normal power to emergency power and back, requiring equipment to restart in both cases. It may be advisable to make the transition back to normal power a manual transition (rather than automatic) in order to minimize impact. Similarly, "closed" transition equipment, which is capable of transferring back to normal power without a loss of current for more than a few milliseconds, can be considered to minimize this impact. Paralleling equipment can be considered, which would allow a facility to transition to backup power and back to normal power without loss of current, in a planned outage, offers the greatest flexibility, but at the greatest cost.
  • Uninterruptable power supplies (UPS) should be provided for critical control systems and equipment. The loss of data from process equipment can result in lost batches. While it is advisable to put environmental monitoring systems on uninterruptable power; it is not usual to put environmental equipment on these systems as the inrush current needed to start motors presents a challenge to these systems. In addition, environmental control (HVAC) systems can usually withstand a short shut-down period.
  • Wiring means and methods within biopharmaceutical facilities vary, but the electrical services within production areas should be liquid tight and capable of withstanding the cleaning products normally used in these environments.
  • Coated rigid conduit, stainless steel conduit and PVC conduit can be used, along with "liquid tight" flexible conduits. NEMA 4 and 4X enclosures may be used in wet areas. NEMA 12 may be used for powder handling or other process areas. NEMA 3R is not generally recommended because of its incapability of withstanding water from all directions.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

備用電力系統的三個層次：

  • UPS（不斷電系統，Uninterruptible Power Supply）：以電池維持數分鐘至 30 分鐘的供電，專為防止短暫停電造成控制系統數據丟失和設備誤動作。UPS 無法驅動大型馬達（如 HVAC 風機），只用於控制器、儀表、數據記錄系統。
  • 緊急發電機（Emergency Generator）：燃油發電機在停電後約 10-30 秒內啟動，可驅動大型設備（HVAC、冷凍機、攪拌器）。從停電到發電機接管的空窗期，需要 UPS 橋接。
  • Paralleling Equipment（並聯切換設備）：最高等級解決方案，允許在有計劃的電力切換（如年度電力維修）時，不中斷供電完成從正常電源到備用電源的切換。成本最高，但對 24/7 不間斷生產的 CDMO 至關重要。

NEMA 防護等級（電氣設備防護標準）：

  • NEMA 3R：防雨、有限防水，不能承受從所有方向噴水，不推薦用於生物製藥濕製程區域
  • NEMA 4：防噴水（任何方向），適用於一般製造區
