  • NEMA 4X：防噴水 + 防腐蝕（不鏽鋼），BSL-2+ 以上必用，能承受強力清洗劑
  • NEMA 12：防粉塵，適用於粉末處理區域（如原料藥稱量間）

比喻說明 Analogy

細胞培養停電 = 細胞的「窒息」事件：動物細胞培養（如 CHO 細胞培養 mAb）在 37°C、5% CO₂ 的精密控制環境中生長，代謝速率極高。一旦停電造成攪拌停止、pH 控制失效、氣體供應中斷，細胞在數十分鐘內就開始死亡，製程批次無法挽救。一個 2000L 生物反應器的 mAb 批次，市值可能超過 500 萬美元——UPS 和緊急發電機的投資相比之下微不足道。

「Open」vs「Closed」轉換 = 騎腳踏車換速的差異：「Open transition」（開路轉換）就像腳踏車換速時必須短暫停止踩踏，設備需要重新啟動；「Closed transition」（閉路轉換）就像無縫換速系統，動力不中斷。在細胞培養期間，即使幾秒鐘的電力中斷也可能造成控制系統重啟，導致批次數據記錄空缺，觸發偏差調查。

重點提示 Key Notes

停電後的重啟順序（Restart Sequencing）至關重要：緊急電力恢復後，系統必須按正確順序重啟——通常是：UPS 系統優先（已持續供電）→ HVAC 啟動（建立壓差和環境控制）→ 製程設備（確認環境達標後）→ 控制系統確認數據完整性。若順序錯誤（例如在 HVAC 恢復前啟動生物反應器），可能違反無菌生產的 GMP 要求，導致批次被拒絕放行。

環境監控系統（EMS）需要 UPS：EMS（含在線粒子計數器、溫濕度傳感器、壓差計）應接 UPS，以確保停電期間的環境數據記錄不中斷——這是 GMP 批次記錄完整性的要求。但環境「控制」設備（HVAC 風機等）因啟動電流太大，不適合接 UPS，由緊急發電機供電。

公式與計算 Formula

備用電力規劃評估框架：

關鍵負載分類：
Level 1（UPS 必需）：
  - 製程控制系統（DCS/PLC）
  - 環境監控系統（EMS）
  - 生命安全系統（緊急照明、疏散系統）
  - 關鍵數據記錄設備

Level 2（發電機 10-30 秒內接管）：
  - HVAC 系統（環境控制）
  - 生物反應器攪拌/控制
  - 冷凍/冷藏系統（-80°C 超低溫、2-8°C）
  - 廢水處理/生物滅活系統

Level 3（可接受短暫中斷）：
  - 一般照明
  - 辦公設備
  - 非關鍵製造設備

UPS 容量估算（簡化）：
UPS 容量（kVA）= 總關鍵負載（kW）/ 功率因數（≈0.9） × 安全係數（1.25）
持續時間 = 電池容量（kWh）/ 實際負載（kW）

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 停電風險評估情境：一家 CDMO 的 mAb 生產廠（3 台 2000L 生物反應器，每批市值 $3M USD）計畫評估備用電力投資：

  • UPS 系統（$50K 投資）：保護控制系統，防止停電造成批次數據記錄空缺和偏差報告；保護 EMS 數據連續性，維護 GMP 合規
  • 緊急發電機（$300K 投資）：保護所有 Level 2 設備，防止停電超過 30 秒造成的批次損失；每次停電事件的潛在損失（3 批 × $3M = $9M）遠高於設備投資
  • Closed Transition 並聯切換（$800K 追加投資）：消除計劃性電力維護期間的生產中斷，對年產 50+ 批次的大型 CDMO 可在 2 年內回收投資
  • 結論：對於高價值生物製藥 CDMO，UPS + 發電機是最低限度投資，Closed transition 是長期效益最佳的選項

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一個 CHO 細胞培養批次（14 天，正在第 10 天）發生 45 秒的停電。假設 UPS 保持了控制系統運行，但 HVAC 暫停。請問：(a) 批次是否一定需要報廢？(b) 應採取哪些步驟評估批次的可用性？
  2. 為什麼 NEMA 3R 不推薦用於生物製藥濕製程區域，但 NEMA 4X 卻是強制要求？從清潔驗證（Cleaning Validation）的角度分析這個設計決策。
  3. 生物製藥廠的電氣條管封堵（sealing of conduits and penetrations）在 BSL-2+ 以上是強制要求，但在 BSL-1 只是建議。這兩種情況在生物圍堵（biocontainment）上有何本質差異？

本章重點回顧 Chapter Summary

  • MEP 設計哲學：生物製藥廠的機械系統設計需同時滿足三個目標——保護產品品質（產品污染控制）、保護員工安全（生物安全/Biosafety）、保護公眾健康（生物圍堵/Biocontainment），三者有時相互衝突，必須通過系統性風險評估（結合風險因子與保護因子）進行多維度整合設計
  • HVAC 核心設計原則：空間分級應基於真實風險（非過度分類）；製程密閉性（Process Closure）是降低分級要求最有效的設計槓桿；換氣次數（ACH）是設計起點而非規範，需結合 CFD 模擬和混合因子（K）校正；BSL 等級決定排氣過濾（HEPA 要求）和氣流策略（循環 vs 一次通過）
  • 分級系統對照：ISPE Grade 5/6/7/8 + CNC+/CNC/UC 系統橋接了 ISO 14644-1、EU GMP（A/B/C/D）和 FDA（ISO 5-8）的不同監管框架；Grade 7 對應 ISO 7 / EU Grade B，30-60 ACH，HEPA 過濾；Grade 8 對應 ISO 8 / EU Grade C，15-60 ACH
  • 防火特殊考量：Pre-action 消防系統是潔淨室和生物安全區域的標準；灑水排放在含活性微生物的區域必須進行生物去活化處理（abatement）；下游純化區的乙醇/IPA 使用需要 LEL 偵測和防爆設計；高價值區域可選用 Clean agent 氣體滅火系統
  • 電氣與備用電力：細胞培養批次無法承受停電（停電 = 批次損失）——UPS 保護控制系統和 EMS 數據記錄，緊急發電機保護 HVAC 和製程設備，Closed Transition 切換設備消除計劃性停電的影響；所有 BSL-2+ 區域的電氣設備必須使用 NEMA 4X 防腐蝕防水規格，配管必須液密封堵
  • 永續性考量：HVAC 佔製藥廠總能耗的 60%；通過「精準分級、Idle Mode 節能模式、熱回收、避免過濾過度」可顯著降低能耗和碳排放，同時維持 GMP 合規
9+A1

Chapter 9+A1: Sustainability & Appendix 1

永續設計與附錄一 | p111-p121

Chapter 9 & Appendix 1: Sustainability + Supporting Information

第九章 永續性 ＋ 附錄一 補充資訊（環境分級技術參考）
ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 6 (2nd Ed.): Biopharmaceutical Manufacturing Facilities | p111 – p121

本章學習目標

  • 理解永續設計（Sustainable Design）在生物製藥廠中的七大核心策略，以及封閉製程（Closed Processing）如何同時降低能耗與環境等級需求。
  • 掌握 Appendix 1 中機械術語的精確定義：包含 CNC / CNC+ / Grade 5/7/8 的差異，以及 MERV、換氣率、通風效率等 HVAC 參數。
  • 學會 10.2 節的「風險導向環境分級（Risk-Based Environmental Classification）」兩步驟方法論：先評暴露風險、再折算防護層級，得出最低所需環境等級。
  • 運用 FMEA 方法論進行六步驟環境風險評估，能將書面方法轉化為設施設計決策，並理解此方法如何為 CDMO 節省數百萬的建設與運營成本。
Chapter 9 — Sustainability｜第九章 永續性

原文內容 Original Text

9.1 Sustainability in the Context of Biopharmaceutical Facility Design

Although the processing chemicals used as buffers can be a challenge to the environment and the risk of non-deactivated viruses should be given careful consideration in regard to disposal, biopharmaceutical drug substances can be considered sustainable, as they are cultured in a growth medium which promotes their growth through the use of enhanced natural means.

Sustainable facility design involves:

  • Designing layouts that are spatially efficient.
  • Designing layouts that consider passive solar design in the placing and orientation of individual blocks of the facility on the site to gain maximum advantage/ecological benefit of the climatic location.
  • Insulating the facility to ensure that expenditure on energy is kept to a minimum.
  • The minimization of heat loss and heat gain through an efficient building envelope should be balanced against the need for cooling load reduction considerations in pharmaceutical facilities.
  • Correct site orientation and sun screening to minimize heat gain for cooling and to maximize heat gain for heating.
  • Commissioning and monitoring the facility for ongoing energy savings.
  • Ensuring that the facility operation and maintenance is efficient by design.
  • Providing renewable energy sources as a strategy including sources that recycle or return energy to the community.
  • Using process heat sources rather than exhausting them.
  • Minimizing water consumption and considering grey water recycling.
  • Working in conjunction with the process to provide all of the above to the benefit of the stakeholders, company, personnel, and public at large.

Each of the above activities may be considered as a sustainable design basis or criterion when placed in the context of building designs that consider:

  • Adaptability and flexibility in use
  • The potential for re-use, given full life cycle/design life assessment from implementation to demolition

Closed processing can provide opportunities for a significant reduction in:

  • Energy use and consumption (by reductions in Grade)
  • Once through air requirements
  • Facility response
  • Facility and utility size

The use of modular continuous processing lines and the potential both for closed processing and the greater use of disposables could allow facility size reduction and adaptability and flexibility in the use of a facility. This is likely to provide both an environmental benefit and an operational cost benefit through reduced local taxes and reduced facility energy usage.

Simpler manufacturing formats for retrofitting available commercial industrial buildings may provide a cost benefit, when compared to new bespoke facility designs expected of open, batch type processing.

An ISPE Good Practice Guide on Sustainability [67] is in development and is intended to provide overall guidance on sustainability and related topic areas.

Sustainable facility design can provide significant contributions to sustainability in the following areas:

  • Application of green chemistry
  • Reduction in carbon and/or total greenhouse gas emissions (metric tons CO2 equivalent), downward trend in annual figures
  • Process intensification, reduced waste, improved yield
  • Waste minimization (e.g., reduced water usage), reduced total waste, downward trend in annual figures
  • Energy reduction (in GJ), downward trend in annual figures
  • Reduction in solvent usage (tons), reduction VOC emissions (tons), downward trend in annual figures
  • Reduction in waste water COD (mg/l)
  • Areas where policies have been instituted
  • Verification of a system, e.g., ISO 14001 [68]
  • Certification using an agreed environmental assessment method/system to meet a specified target
  • Performing a life cycle assessment using an agreed assessment methodology

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 永續性 (Sustainability) 的定義

永續設計 (Sustainable Facility Design)：設施在滿足當前製造需求的同時，將對環境的長期負面影響降至最低。在生物製藥廠，這並非選擇題，而是在法規壓力、碳稅、ESG 報告要求下的必答題。

重要的是，生物製藥的原料（生物培養基）本身就比化學合成更接近自然，因此其本質較具永續潛力——前提是設施設計也同步跟上。

關鍵指標：

  • 碳排放量（公噸 CO₂ 當量）
  • 能耗（GJ / 年）
  • 廢水 COD（mg/L）
  • 溶劑用量（噸 / 年）

比喻說明 — 永續藥廠 = 醫院節能改造

想像一家醫院在不降低病患安全前提下推動節能——不能關掉手術室空調，但可以優化走廊照明、回收廢熱加溫熱水，以及在辦公區域使用自然採光。

生物製藥廠的永續設計邏輯完全相同：無菌保證區域（Grade A/B）絕不妥協，但其他支援區域大有節能空間。封閉製程可讓核心區域降等（Grade C → CNC+），等同讓「手術室」縮小範圍，其餘空間就可以用普通節能建築標準設計。

重點提示 — 封閉製程是永續最強槓桿

本節最關鍵的洞察是：Closed Processing（封閉製程）是降低環境等級的技術前提，而環境等級降低直接轉化為能源與建設成本的大幅節省。

一個 Grade A/B 的無塵室每平方米每年能耗，可能是普通辦公室的 50–100 倍（主要來自 HVAC 的超高換氣率）。若封閉製程允許將某操作降至 Grade C 或 CNC+，等同於在該區域節省數十倍的能耗，同時減少設施面積、降低運維成本。

這也是 Section 10.2 風險導向分級方法論的核心價值所在。

實務應用 — CDMO 的 ESG 競爭力

大型製藥客戶（Big Pharma）在選擇 CDMO 夥伴時，ESG 評分已成為採購標準之一。具備以下永續設施特徵的 CDMO，在競標時有明顯優勢：

  • ISO 14001 環境管理認證
  • 生命週期評估（LCA）報告
  • 模組化/可彈性調整的廠房設計（支援多客戶、快速換產）
  • 封閉製程比例高（間接證明污染控制能力強，同時低能耗）

永續設計指標框架

能源強度指標 = 年總能耗 (GJ) / 產量 (kg API)

水耗指標 = 年用水量 (m³) / 批次數

廢棄物強度 = 年廢棄物總量 (kg) / 產量 (kg API)

碳排放 = 直接排放 (Scope 1)
       + 電力間接排放 (Scope 2)
       + 供應鏈排放 (Scope 3)

這些指標應逐年追蹤並呈現「下降趨勢（downward trend）」，以滿足 ISO 14001 持續改善要求。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼「封閉製程（Closed Processing）」能同時降低環境分級需求和能耗？兩者的關聯機制是什麼？
  2. 模組化連續製程（Modular Continuous Processing）如何同時達到永續性和商業靈活性兩個目標？
  3. 生物製藥廠廢水中的「非去活化病毒（non-deactivated viruses）」問題為何是永續性的挑戰？應如何處理？
Appendix 1 — Supporting Information｜附錄一 補充資訊（技術參考資料）

原文內容 Original Text

10.1 Mechanical Information

10.1.1 Aide Mémoire 07121104 Classifications

Grade F: a classified space that satisfies the German Aide Mémoire 07121104 [69] airborne viable microorganisms < 500 cfu/m³.

Grade E: a classified space that satisfies the German Aide Mémoire 07121104 [69] airborne viable microorganisms < 250 cfu/m³.

10.1.2 PIC/S and EMA Application of ISO 14644

Grade D: a classified space that satisfies EMA and PIC/S requirements to meet ISO-8 measured via airborne 0.5 μm and 5.0 μm particulate in the "at-rest" state only and airborne viable microorganisms < 200 cfu/m³.

Grade C: a classified space that satisfies EMA and PIC/S requirements to meet ISO-8 measured via airborne 0.5 μm and 5.0 μm particulate in the "in-operation" state and meet ISO-7 measured via airborne 0.5 μm and 5.0 μm particulate in the "at-rest" state (with a transition between states of 15 to 20 minutes) and airborne viable microorganisms < 100 cfu/m³.

Grade B: a classified space that satisfies EMA and PIC/S requirements to meet ISO-7 measured via airborne 0.5 μm and 5.0 μm particulate in the "in-operation" state and meet ISO-5 measured via airborne 0.5 μm and 5.0 μm particulate in the "at-rest" state (with a transition between states of 15 to 20 minutes) and airborne viable microorganisms < 10 cfu/m³.

Grade A: a classified space that satisfies EMA and PIC/S requirements to meet ISO-5 measured via airborne 0.5 μm particulate and ISO-4.8 measured via airborne 5.0 μm particulate in the "in-operation" and "at-rest" states and airborne viable microorganisms < 1 cfu/m³. These spaces are normally unidirectional flow with an air velocity of 0.20 to 0.45 m/s.

10.1.3 Revised ISPE Grades

Grade 8: a classified space that satisfies US FDA requirements for ISO-8 measured via airborne 0.5 μm particulate in the "in-operation" state, as well as EMA and PIC/S requirements to meet ISO-8 measured via airborne 0.5 μm and 5.0 μm particulate in the "in-operation" state and meet ISO-7 measured via airborne 0.5 μm and 5.0 μm particulate in the "at-rest" state (with a transition between states of 15 to 20 minutes) and airborne viable microorganisms < 100 cfu/m³.

Grade 7: a classified space that satisfies US FDA requirements for ISO-7 measured via airborne 0.5 μm particulate in the "in-operation" state, as well as EMA and PIC/S requirements to meet ISO-7 measured via airborne 0.5 μm and 5.0 μm particulate in the "in-operation" state and meet ISO-5 measured via airborne 0.5 μm and 5.0 μm particulate in the "at-rest" state (with a transition between states of 15 to 20 minutes) and airborne viable microorganisms < 10 cfu/m³.

Grade 5: a classified space that satisfies US FDA requirements for ISO-5 measured via airborne 0.5 μm particulate in the "in-operation" state, as well as EMA and PIC/S requirements to meet ISO-5 measured via airborne 0.5 μm particulate and ISO-4.8 measured via airborne 5.0 μm particulate in the "in-operation" and "at-rest" states, and airborne viable microorganisms < 1 cfu/m³. These spaces are normally unidirectional flow with an air velocity of 0.20 to 0.45 m/s.

Controlled Not Classified (CNC): areas where HVAC systems are specifically designed to reduce airborne contaminants below the level of the ambient environment and both temperature and Relative Humidity (RH) are controlled more tightly than in the ambient environment. Claims for environmental control in these areas are related to the design of the system and installation qualification is common. No claim is made or qualified for the specific control of particulate. Typical systems will have heating, cooling and filtration meeting MERV 13 or better. These areas are sometimes referred to as "pharmaceutical" or "clean" areas within pharmaceutical facilities.

Controlled Not Classified with Local Monitoring (CNC+): areas where HVAC systems are specifically designed to reduce airborne contaminants below the level and both temperature and RH are controlled more tightly than in the ambient environment. Claims for environmental control in these areas are related to both the design of the system and system performance, installation qualification and operational qualification is common. These areas are typically qualified to meet ISO 8 requirements at rest only to control temperature and humidity within a specified band and are monitored for viable particulate during operation to provide background information for investigations and to assure the adequacy of layers of closure. These areas are generally aligned with PIC/S designation "Grade D" and airborne viable microorganisms < 200 cfu/m³.

Temperature Controlled: areas where HVAC systems are specifically designed to control both temperature and (where applicable) Relative Humidity (RH) more tightly than in the ambient environment. Temperature and RH are typically qualified in these areas and temperature mapping is expected. This designation is typically found in warehouse spaces, cold rooms, logistics.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 環境等級分類體系完整對照

本節是整本指南的技術詞彙表，特別重要的是 ISPE 統合了三大法規體系（FDA / EMA / PIC/S）的等級定義。以下是完整對照：

重點提示 — CNC vs CNC+ 的關鍵差異

CNC 和 CNC+ 是本指南特有的創新等級概念，也是 CDMO 設計閉合製程區域時最常用到的兩個等級：

  • CNC（Controlled Not Classified）：只有溫濕度控制＋MERV 13 過濾，無微粒計數要求。適用於完全密閉、無產品暴露的操作區。
  • CNC+（帶本地監測）：增加了 ISO 8 靜態驗證＋運作中微生物監測。雖不是「正式分級」，但有 OQ 記錄和持續監控，作為封閉製程中最後一道背景保證。

從成本角度：Grade 8 換氣率約 20–30 ACH，CNC+ 可低至 15–20 ACH，CNC 更可低至 6–10 ACH。每 ACH 的差異在大型設施中，每年電費差距可達百萬台幣以上。

比喻說明 — 環境等級 = 防護口罩的等級選擇

就像選擇防護口罩：外科口罩（Grade D/CNC+）→ N95（Grade C/Grade 8）→ PAPR（Grade B/Grade 7）→ 全身正壓防護衣（Grade A/Grade 5）。

重點不是「越貴越好」，而是依危險程度（暴露風險）選擇最匹配的防護等級——這正是 10.2 節風險導向分級的核心邏輯。如果你的操作本身是「密閉的」（等同於沒有飛沫傳播），那麼連外科口罩都不需要——這就是 CNC 等級的意義。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. Grade 7（ISPE）對應 EU GMP 的哪個等級？其靜態和運作中的 ISO 等級各是什麼？
  2. CNC+ 和 Grade D（PIC/S）有何關聯？為何 CNC+ 雖然「未正式分級」卻仍需要 OQ 和微生物監測？
  3. 為什麼 Grade A 的氣流速度要求是「單向流 0.20–0.45 m/s」？這與亂流等級在污染控制機制上有何本質差異？

原文內容 Original Text — 機械術語（續）

Gaseous Decontamination: one of a number of technologies that disseminate a biocidal gas to produce a minimum 3 log (and as much as 6 log) reduction in viable organisms in the environment. These technologies diffuse at the molecular level and can pass through a HEPA filter.

Fogging Decontamination: one of a number of technologies that disseminate a biocidal agent as very small particle size to produce a minimum 3 log (and as much as 6 log) reduction in viable organisms in the environment. These technologies cannot pass through a HEPA filter efficiently (greater than 20% loss).

Containment: equipment, systems or construction intended to prevent the escape of products, materials or organisms.

Biological Containment: an organized system of equipment, and construction intended to prevent the escape of organisms. Biological containment is usually identified according to the biological safety designation of the organism(s) being contained.

Containment Boundary: the imaginary line in the construction of systems or facilities on which the various components of a containment barrier are aligned. Spaces within this boundary are normally considered as contaminated with the contained material or organism.

Containment Barrier: construction that is impervious or highly resistant to the passage of micro-organisms. Solid materials make up the majority of containment barriers, but HEPA and ULPA filters are also considered containment barriers.

Global Recirculation: re-use (recirculation) of conditioned air leaving a room to serve any room of similar type or function.

Local Recirculation: re-use (recirculation) of conditioned air leaving a room only to serve that room or suite of rooms with similar biological and contamination risks.

N+1 Redundancy: a system where the failure of any single major component will not result in a reduction in capacity below the design requirement.

XX% N+1 Redundancy: a system where the failure of any single major component will result in XX% of the design required capacity remaining.

Decontamination Capable HVAC: an HVAC system that is arranged to recirculate gaseous decontamination agent for effective decontamination of a space and the air system(s) serving it.

Decontamination Compatible HVAC: an HVAC system where exposed components are resistant to gaseous decontamination agents.

Decontamination Capable Exhaust: an exhaust system that is arranged to allow recirculation of gaseous decontamination agent for effective decontamination of filter and fans as well as exhaust of decontamination agent from a served space.

Pre and Post-Viral Separation (Viral+ and Viral−): the separation of pre-viral and post-viral product or upstream (bioreaction and harvest) from downstream (purification) is not precise. Most processes utilize multiple process steps to reduce the concentration of organisms or DNA/RNA from the culture, creating the final product. In the case of vaccines, the viral contaminants may never be removed. The convention is to separate air systems that serve these two open processing areas to reduce the chance of contamination of the final product; however, this may not be scientifically supportable. Similar to earlier evaluations, the ability of the product or organisms to become airborne should be considered. This separation is affected by process closure, the achievement of closure obviates the need for HVAC separation.

Multiple Efficiency Reporting Value (MERV): the ASHRAE Standard 52.2 [70] method of testing filter efficiency by challenging filters with particles of multiple sizes and integrating the efficiency into a single number rating. The higher the MERV number the more efficient the filter. MERV 14/15 is approximately equivalent to a 95% efficient filter.

Air Change Rate (Ventilation Rate): the volume of air supplied to a room (per hour) divided by the volume of the room. This is a purely numerical evaluation used as a rule of thumb in cleanroom design.

Particle Generation Rate: the number of particles of a target size released into a room (per hour) by processes, people, or in the supply air.

Dilution Ventilation: Reduction in airborne contamination via mixing of clean incoming air with contaminated air within the room and removal of an equivalent amount to exhaust or recirculation via treatment (e.g. filtration).

Displacement Ventilation: reduction in airborne contamination via "plug flow" of clean incoming air forcing contaminated air within the room to exhaust or recirculation via treatment (e.g., filtration).

Ventilation Efficiency (Effectiveness): the ability of an HVAC system to dilute contaminants when compared to ideal dilution. A ventilation effectiveness of 1.0 indicates that a room is able to dilute contaminants as effectively as is indicated by an ideal dilution calculation. Displacement ventilation may have an effectiveness as high as 3.0 to 4.0.

Recovery: a test defined in ISO 14644-3 [63] intended to show a cleanroom's ability to "cleanup" from an operational particulate specification to a lower (cleaner) classification.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 氣態除汙 vs 霧化除汙

氣態除汙（Gaseous Decontamination，如 VHP/H₂O₂ 氣體）：分子層級擴散，可通過 HEPA 過濾器，因此可對整個送風系統進行去汙（含管道和過濾器本體）。這是 BSL-2/3 生物廠房或有病毒暴露風險的生物製藥廠使用的主流技術。

霧化除汙（Fogging，如過氧化氫霧化）：粒子較大，無法有效穿過 HEPA 過濾器（損失 >20%），僅能對房間本體去汙，不能覆蓋 HVAC 系統。

選擇時機判斷：若需要同時對房間和 HVAC 去汙（如隔離器驗證後的整體再清潔），必須選擇氣態技術。

核心概念 — Viral+ / Viral− 分區原理

生物製藥生產分為「病毒清除前（Viral+）」和「病毒清除後（Viral−）」兩個區域：

  • Viral+ 區域：上游製程（細胞培養、收穫），含有活性病毒和細胞的空間
  • Viral− 區域：下游純化後，理論上病毒已被去除或滅活

傳統做法是將兩者的 HVAC 系統完全分離，防止 Viral+ 空氣污染最終產品。但關鍵洞察是：若製程本身是封閉的，這種 HVAC 分離就沒有科學必要性——封閉系統內的病毒不會變成空氣污染物。這再次強調了「過程封閉性」對設施設計的根本影響。

HVAC 設計關鍵參數計算

換氣率 ACH = 送風量 (m³/h) ÷ 房間體積 (m³)

通風效率比較：
  稀釋通風（亂流）效率 ≈ 1.0
  置換通風（單向流）效率 ≈ 3.0–4.0

含義：
  置換通風達到相同清潔效果，
  只需稀釋通風 1/3 的換氣次數
  → 重大節能潛力

MERV 對應關係：
  MERV 13 ≈ 75–90% 效率 (≥1μm)
  MERV 14 ≈ 90–95% 效率
  HEPA   ≈ 99.97% 效率 (≥0.3μm)

重點提示 — N+1 備援的實際含義

N+1 備援（N+1 Redundancy）是 GMP 廠房設計的基本安全原則：任一主要元件故障，系統總容量仍維持 100%。

XX% N+1 備援則是較實際的版本：例如「50% N+1 備援」表示任一元件故障後，系統仍維持 50% 容量——對非無菌製造區域可能可接受，但對 Grade A/B 空間通常需要 100% N+1。

CDMO 設計時的商業考量：N+1 備援增加初始建設成本，但可防止因設備故障導致的批次失敗（每批生物製藥價值可達數千萬台幣）。需用 ROI 模型評估最適備援策略。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一個使用 VHP（氣態過氧化氫）除汙的 BSL-2 生物廠房，其 HVAC 系統需要哪種設計規格？（Decontamination Capable vs Compatible 的差異）
  2. 若某細胞培養操作採用密封的一次性生物反應器（完全封閉），是否還需要 Viral+/Viral− 的 HVAC 分隔？請說明理由。
  3. 「置換通風（Displacement Ventilation）」的通風效率為何高達 3.0–4.0？這在 Grade A 單向流設計中如何體現？
10.2 Methods of Environmental Classification through Risk Assessment｜風險導向環境分級方法論

原文內容 Original Text

10.2 Methods of Environmental Classification through Risk Assessment

In a risk-based approach to area classification, increasing exposure risk (based on process sensitivity, bio-safety, or the presence of downstream mitigations) should be considered in light of established layers of protection, in order to determine the appropriate space classification for an operation. There are numerous methods to do this analysis. Tables 10.1 and 10.2 are an example of one possible approach to risk assessment.

In stage 1, the risk of contamination is determined based on the stage of the process and the inherent risk to contamination of the process. The risk may derive from a lack of isolation from the ambient environment, high energy in adjacent processes (high risk of aerosol contaminants), the presence of growth media in the process, or the inherent fragility of the organism or protein. The product of these two factors yields an exposure risk ranking (given here on a 1 to 5 scale of Low, Med-Low, Medium, Med-High, and High).

In the second step, this exposure risk is adjusted by evaluating the layers of protection available to shield the process from contamination. The more layers of protection available to prevent contamination the less critical the ambient environment is to product quality. The risk of failure of the protection should be included in this evaluation; for example, a silicone tube has a higher risk of failure than a stainless steel tube; therefore, the layers of protection it provides would be less.

This example equates the levels of protection, approximately, with log reduction of contaminants provided by that layer. This concept is leveraged from sterile processing where log reductions in contamination are the standard for rating process closure. This concept is also well aligned with the environmental classifications, where each succeeding lower classification number is one order of magnitude cleaner than its predecessor. This example equates the five levels of risk with five classifications (Grade 5, Grade 7, Grade 8, CNC+, and CNC) as discussed in the following section.

Notes:
  1. A fully hermetic system should provide > 4 log reduction in contaminants or 4 layers of protection.
  2. An open micro-environment can typically provide a > 1 to 2 log reduction in contaminants, or 1 to 2 layers of protection.
  3. A closed micro-environment can provide a > 3 log reduction in contaminants, or 3 layers of protection.
  4. The log reductions proposed herein are derived from sterile and containment equipment performance.
  5. The risk of failure should be included in the evaluation (e.g., stainless steel piping would rank as greater protection than a plastic tube).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 風險導向分級的邏輯框架

這是本指南最具實踐價值的工具之一。傳統方法是「照本宣科」套用法規等級；風險導向方法則要求：

最終所需環境等級 = f（暴露風險, 防護層數）

核心邏輯：
• 暴露風險高 → 需要更嚴格的環境等級
• 防護層數多 → 可以降低對環境等級的要求
• 兩者相互抵消，得出最低必要等級

這種方法讓設施設計者有科學依據去主張「我的製程雖然是高風險步驟，但因為有4層保護，所以只需要 CNC 等級環境」——這在監管溝通中是強有力的論據。

比喻說明 — 風險分級 = 防災等級評估

想像建築結構工程師評估一棟建築需要多強的防震規格：地震風險等級（暴露風險）× 結構防護措施（防護層數）= 所需建築規範等級。

台北市（高地震區）+ 純木造結構（0 層防護）→ 需要最嚴格規範（Grade 5 等效）。
台北市（高地震區）+ 鋼骨+隔震墊+制震器（4 層防護）→ 標準規範即可（CNC 等效）。
宜蘭外海（低地震區）+ 任何結構 → 寬鬆規範（CNC）。

關鍵洞察：不是地點危險就必然要最貴的設計——防護措施可以「對沖」風險。

重點提示 — 理解 Table 10.2 的閱讀方式

Table 10.2 是一個「查表工具」：

  1. 先從 Table 10.1 確定暴露風險等級（High / Med-High / Medium / Med-Low / Low）
  2. 再數算有多少層防護（0 = 完全開放；4 = 完全密封系統）
  3. 查表得出最低所需環境等級

關鍵結論：即使是「High」暴露風險（如開放式生物反應器進料），只要有 4 層保護，環境等級可低至 CNC——而非直覺上的 Grade 5。這是節省建設成本的關鍵槓桿。

反之，「Low」風險但零防護（如完全暴露的純化操作），只需 CNC——說明這個步驟本身就不需要高等級環境。

防護層數的對數等效計算

防護等效關係（近似）：
  0 層防護 → 完全暴露（0 log 減少）
  1-2 層  → 開放微環境（RABS等）
             1–2 log 污染減少
  3 層    → 封閉微環境（隔離器等）
             >3 log 污染減少
  4 層    → 完全密封系統
             >4 log 污染減少

材料可靠性影響（Note 5）：
  不鏽鋼管路 > 矽膠管路
  （不鏽鋼失效率低 → 保護層「信用值」更高）

環境等級間距 = 1 個數量級：
  Grade 5 (ISO 5) → Grade 7 (ISO 7) 約 100x 差異
  Grade 7 (ISO 7) → Grade 8 (ISO 8) 約 10x 差異
  → 每升一個等級 ≈ 1 log 更乾淨

實務應用 — CDMO 的分級效益計算

以一個 500 m² 的純化操作區為例：

  • 傳統保守做法（Grade C / Grade 8）：HVAC 換氣率 20–30 ACH，建設成本高 +30%，年電費高 +200萬
  • 封閉製程 + 風險評估（CNC+）：換氣率 15 ACH，建設成本降低，年電費節省 200萬以上
  • 完全密封系統（CNC）：換氣率 6–10 ACH，最大節省

15 年廠房生命週期內，正確的風險導向分級可節省 3,000萬台幣以上的能源和建設成本，同時完全符合法規要求。這份文件（Appendix 1, Section 10.2）就是你向客戶或監管機構解釋為何選擇較低等級的技術正當性文件。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一個「最終純化（Final Purification）」步驟，使用密封的不鏽鋼管路系統（3 層保護）。根據 Table 10.2，應分配哪個環境等級？請逐步走過邏輯。
  2. 為何不鏽鋼管路提供的保護「信用值」高於矽膠管路？在風險評估中如何量化這個差異？
  3. 若一家 CDMO 想將某個操作區從 Grade 8 降至 CNC+，其風險評估報告需要論證哪幾個要素？（提示：從 Table 10.1 和 10.2 倒推）

原文內容 Original Text

10.2.1 Other Approaches to Risk Assessment

FMEA is one of the most popular methods of risk assessment and prioritization. Most companies have a standard approach (evaluating the probability, impact and detectability of an environmental control failure) that is fully applicable to this type of assessment. Given the consistency of the factors that must be considered, as discussed in the preceding, an approach with a fixed taxonomy can be used to promote a consistent evaluation of risk and resultant environmental controls. The following is an example of one such approach and method.

Figure 10.1: Example Environmental Risk Assessment Figure
[Risk assessment tool figure referenced in source — shows a multi-factor FMEA framework for environmental risk evaluation]

The above tool is used in a multi-step process when performing an environmental risk assessment to determine area biosafety and cleanliness classifications:

Step 1:

Look at every room or function in the facility to consider the risk associated with the activities in that room.

Step 2:

Look at every activity and sub activity (e.g., charging, processing, discharging) in the room.

Step 3:

Look at every activity and sub-activity and assign a risk associated with its sensitivity to the room environment. Consider the level of energy, the level of openness, the sensitivity of the process itself (presence of growth media, hand manipulation, etc.)

Look for the presence of organisms requiring biosafety.

Examine both the impact of contamination as well as the probability of contamination at that step.

Step 4:

Look at the layers of protection against the above sensitivity to the room environment.

Step 5:

Look at both the impact of contamination at the stage in the process and the presence of downstream processing that can further mitigate the environmental risk.

Step 6:

Take the product of the preceding factors and determine a level of environmental control required. Gowning may be a factor included in this determination.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — FMEA 在環境分級中的應用

FMEA（Failure Mode and Effects Analysis，失效模式與效應分析）是品質風險管理（QRM）的核心工具，ICH Q9 推薦使用。將其應用於環境分級時，三個評分維度為：

  • 嚴重性（Severity）：若環境控制失效，對產品品質的衝擊有多大？
  • 發生率（Probability）：環境控制失效的可能性有多高？
  • 可偵測性（Detectability）：若發生，能否及時發現並採取措施？

三者相乘得出 RPN（風險優先數），RPN 高者需要更嚴格的環境控制；RPN 低者可降低等級要求。

比喻說明 — 六步驟如同「安全審查清單」

這六個步驟就像航空公司飛行員的飛行前清單（Pre-flight Checklist）——每一步都有明確目的，必須依序執行，不能跳過：

  • 步驟 1–2：把「飛行計畫」分解到每個細節（每個房間的每個操作）
  • 步驟 3：評估每個細節的「危險性」（能量大小、開放程度、生長培養基存在）
  • 步驟 4–5：盤點「安全設備」（防護層數、下游去除步驟）
  • 步驟 6：根據以上得出「本次飛行需要幾名空服員」（所需環境等級）

關鍵是：每個房間、每個操作步驟都要獨立評估——一個大房間裡可能同時有需要 Grade 8 的操作和只需 CNC 的操作。

重點提示 — 步驟 5 中「下游緩解」的重要性

步驟 5 中「下游製程的緩解作用（downstream mitigation）」是一個常被忽視但極有價值的因素：

如果某個可能被污染的操作，其下游有多道去除步驟（例如：Protein A 純化 + 病毒去除過濾 + UF/DF），那麼即使在這個步驟引入了少量環境污染，後續製程也能清除它——因此環境要求可以降低。

反之，若某步驟是「最後一道關卡」（如最終配製充填），下游沒有任何過濾去除，環境要求就必須最嚴格。

這正是為何 API 步驟（最終填充前）在 Table 10.1 中被標示為「High」暴露風險的原因。

六步驟決策框架總結

Step 1: 列出所有房間/功能區
         ↓
Step 2: 分解每個房間內的每個操作
         （充填、加料、排放等子活動）
         ↓
Step 3: 評估每個操作的暴露敏感性
         · 能量水平（aerosol 生成風險）
         · 開放程度
         · 生長培養基的存在
         · 生物安全等級要求
         · 污染衝擊 × 污染概率
         ↓
Step 4: 計算防護層數
         （密封容器、隔離器、封閉管路等）
         ↓
Step 5: 評估下游緩解措施
         （後續純化步驟能否清除污染）
         ↓
Step 6: 查 Table 10.2
         → 確定最低所需環境等級
         （+ 考量人員更衣要求）

實務應用 — 如何將這份報告用於監管溝通

在 FDA Pre-approval Inspection (PAI) 或 EMA GMP 稽查中，若稽查員質疑某區域的環境等級選擇，這套六步驟 FMEA 文件就是你的技術防禦工事：

  • 文件化每個操作的暴露風險評分（附理由）
  • 文件化防護層數計算（含材料可靠性分析）
  • 文件化下游緩解措施清單
  • 最終等級選擇的邏輯鏈（從 Table 10.1 → Table 10.2 → 選定等級）

這份文件一旦在設計階段完成並獲批，就成為你設施設計的「科學正當性依據（Scientific Justification）」，在後續所有監管溝通中都可以引用。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 請用六步驟框架，評估以下場景：
    一個密閉的 Protein A 管柱純化步驟（全程不鏽鋼管路，無人工開放操作，下游還有病毒去除過濾和 UF/DF）。你的建議環境等級是什麼？
  2. 為何「更衣（Gowning）」會被列入步驟 6 的考量因素？它在保護邏輯中扮演什麼角色（是保護產品，還是保護操作人員，還是兩者都是）？
  3. 若同一個房間裡有兩個操作：一個需要 Grade 8，另一個只需要 CNC，整個房間應該定什麼等級？有沒有可能用分區方式解決？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • 永續設計的核心槓桿是封閉製程（Closed Processing）：封閉製程允許降低環境等級，等級降低直接轉化為數十倍的能耗節省和大幅降低建設成本，同時改善 ESG 表現。
  • ISPE 統合了三大法規體系（FDA / EMA / PIC/S）的等級定義：Grade 5 = Grade A, Grade 7 = Grade B, Grade 8 = Grade C, CNC+ ≈ Grade D。掌握這個對應表，可以在跨法規溝通時避免混亂。
  • CNC 和 CNC+ 是生物製藥封閉製程最常用的環境等級：它們不是「次等」的無等級空間，而是有完整 IQ/OQ 文件支持的設計控制空間，在閉合製程設計中具有重大成本優勢。
  • 風險導向分級的兩步驟邏輯：Step 1 從製程階段和污染敏感性確定暴露風險等級；Step 2 根據防護層數（0–4層）折算出最低所需環境等級，查 Table 10.2 得出答案。
  • FMEA 六步驟是監管溝通的技術防禦工事：完整的六步驟文件讓低於傳統保守等級的設計選擇有科學正當性，在 FDA PAI 和 EMA 稽查中可作為強力支持文件。
  • 下游緩解（Downstream Mitigation）是降低等級的重要論據：若某操作後有多道純化去除步驟，環境要求可合理降低；反之，「最終關卡」操作的環境要求必須最嚴格。

Chapter A2+A3: References & Glossary

本章學習目標

  • 能夠識別並說明本指南所引用的關鍵法規與指引文件（ICH、FDA、EU GMP、WHO等）的用途與重要性。
  • 掌握 ISPE Baseline Guide Vol.6 詞彙表中所有縮寫的全稱與中文意義。
  • 深度理解 Closed System（密閉系統）、Open System（開放式系統）、Axenic State（純淨狀態）、Bioburden-Free（無微生物負荷）等核心定義。
  • 能夠解釋 CQA、CPP、BSL、SIP、CIP、RABS 等術語在生物製藥廠房設計與 GMP 合規中的實務意義。
  • 利用快速參考摘要表，作為日常 GMP 術語查閱工具。

導師解析 — 核心法規文件的重要性

ICH Q7/Q7A — API GMP 準則

本指引規範了活性醫藥成分（API）的 GMP 要求，是全球藥廠共同遵守的基準。對生物製藥而言，雖然 API 多為大分子蛋白質，但此指引確立了生產環境控制、設備確效、批次記錄等核心概念，為後續生物製藥特定指引（如 ICH Q11）奠定基礎。

ICH Q11 — 原料藥開發與製造

Q11 是 Q7 的延伸，專門針對「生技／生物製品」的原料藥（drug substance）開發，包括細胞培養、發酵、純化等程序。此指引要求廠商建立設計空間（Design Space）並說明工藝開發的科學依據，與 ISPE Vol.6 的設施設計邏輯緊密連動。

21 CFR Part 211 — FDA 完成劑型 GMP

21 CFR Part 211 是 FDA 對完成劑型藥品（finished pharmaceuticals）的核心法規要求，涵蓋廠房設計、設備、人員、生產與製程控制、品管等全面要求。生物製藥廠若打算在美國銷售產品，必須確保所有設施設計與操作程序符合 Part 211 的最低要求。重點：Part 211 是法規底線，而 ISPE 指引是最佳實務；在合規上，法規永遠優先。

ICH Q9 — 品質風險管理（QRM）

Q9 建立了製藥業通用的風險管理框架，包括 FMEA（失效模式效應分析）、HACCP（危害分析重要管制點）等工具。ISPE Vol.6 全書的設施設計決策（密閉系統、環境分級、HVAC 設計等）均以 QRM 為核心依據，若不理解 Q9，就無法理解為何某些空間需要更嚴格的環境控制。

比喻：法規文件的層次關係

把這些文件想像成建築法規的體系：ICH Q7/Q11 是「建築法規總則」（適用所有建築），21 CFR Part 211 是「消防安全強制規範」（必須遵守），ICH Q9 是「風險評估工具手冊」，而 ISPE Vol.6 則是「高端實驗室建築設計最佳實務指南」。後者告訴你怎麼蓋得最好，但前者告訴你最低必須做到什麼。

練習思考

  1. ICH Q8(R2)（製藥開發）與 ICH Q9（品質風險管理）在設施設計決策中各自扮演什麼角色？
  2. 若一家生物製藥廠同時申請 FDA（美國）和 EMA（歐盟）許可，需要同時遵守 21 CFR Part 211 和哪個歐盟文件？

52. ISPE Baseline Pharmaceutical Engineering Guide, Volume 3 — Sterile Product Manufacturing Facilities, Second Edition, September 2011, www.ispe.org.

導師解析 — ISPE、EU GMP、WHO 與生物安全文件

ISPE Vol.5（C&Q）— 確效的語言基礎

ISPE Vol.6 全書中所有關於系統確效的分類（如 Direct Impact / No Impact，後演變為 QRM Verification）均源自 Vol.5。因此，當 Vol.6 描述「封閉系統不是影響要項（Critical Aspect）」，背後的判定邏輯就是 Vol.5 C&Q 的框架。CDMO 工程師必須將兩者搭配閱讀。

EU GMP Annex 2 — 生物製品製造的歐盟專屬要求

EU GMP Annex 2 專門規範生物製品（包括細胞培養、發酵、血液製品、單株抗體等）的製造要求，是歐盟市場准入的必要條件。此附錄的「草案版」在本書出版時已引入「製程密閉度」和「環境控制策略」的概念，直接影響了 ISPE Vol.6 的設施設計建議。

EU GMP Annex 1 — 無菌製品的標準

Annex 1 是全球無菌製造設施的「聖經」，規定了 A/B/C/D 四個環境等級（Grade A/B/C/D）、浮游菌、沉降菌、接觸碟等環境監測標準。ISPE Vol.6 的環境分級章節與 Annex 1 緊密對應，兩者必須同時參照。

NIH/CDC 生物安全指引 — BSL 等級的法源依據

NIH Guidelines 和 CDC/NIH 聯合出版的《Biosafety in Microbiological and Biomedical Laboratories (BMBL)》是定義 BSL 1-4 生物安全等級的權威文件。ISPE Vol.6 的圍堵策略（Containment Strategy）和設施設計均依賴這些指引來確定微生物的危害等級，以決定所需的物理圍堵措施。若處理 BSL-2 以上的微生物，廠房設計必須符合相應圍堵要求，這不只是 GMP，更是生物安全法律義務。

ISO 14644-1 — 潔淨室空氣分級標準

ISO 14644-1 以科學化的粒子計數方式定義 ISO Class 1-9，是歐美日藥廠環境監測的通用語言。FDA 採用 ISO 5/7/8 對應其傳統的 Class 100/10,000/100,000；EU GMP 則採用 Grade A/B/C/D 但同樣參照 ISO 標準測試方法。ISPE Vol.6 的環境章節以 ISO 14644 為基礎，橋接兩套體系。

實務應用 — CDMO 雙向申請場景

一家台灣 CDMO 同時為美國客戶（FDA 監管）和歐盟客戶（EMA 監管）生產生物製劑。需同時遵守：21 CFR Part 211（FDA）、EU GMP Annex 1 & 2（EMA）、ISO 14644-1（環境分級）、ICH Q9/Q10（品質體系）、NIH/CDC 生物安全指引（BSL 評估）。本附錄的參考文獻清單，就是建立多市場合規矩陣的起點。

完整參考文獻清單（Selected — p121-p127）

原文 — Complete Reference List

導師解析 — 文件體系總覽

六大文件來源體系

  • ICH（國際人用藥品技術要求協和會）：Q7/Q8/Q9/Q10/Q11 構成品質體系骨幹，三方（美、歐、日）共同認可。
  • FDA 法規：21 CFR Part 210/211 是美國市場的強制性法規底線。
  • EU GMP EudraLex Vol.4：Annex 1（無菌）、Annex 2（生物）是歐盟市場准入關鍵。
  • ISPE Baseline Guide 系列：設施設計的最佳實務，Vol.3（無菌）、Vol.5（C&Q）、Vol.7（風險）與本書緊密連動。
  • ISO 14644 系列：潔淨室技術標準，橋接 FDA 和 EU GMP 的環境測試方法。
  • NIH/CDC 生物安全指引：決定 BSL 等級及物理圍堵要求的科學依據。

Appendix 3 — Glossary（附錄三：詞彙表）
12.1 Acronyms and Abbreviations（縮寫對照表）

原文 — Acronyms & Abbreviations

導師解析 — 關鍵縮寫深入說明

BSL（生物安全等級）— 圍堵設計的起點

BSL 1-4 是依據微生物對人體的危害程度分級，決定廠房圍堵等級的關鍵輸入：

  • BSL-1：低危害，標準微生物操作（一般實驗室）
  • BSL-2：中度危害（多數生物製藥細胞株，如 CHO、大腸桿菌），需負壓、高壓滅菌器、BSC
  • BSL-3：嚴重危害，可致命但有治療方法（如結核桿菌），需雙重門、專用排氣
  • BSL-4：極高危害，無治療方法（如伊波拉病毒），需正壓太空衣或隔離式設施

大多數生物製藥廠運作在 BSL-1/2 級別；了解 BSL 等級是設施設計圍堵章節的先決條件。

CNC / CNC+ — 生物製藥特有的環境分類

CNC（Controlled Not Classified，受控但未分級）是 ISPE Vol.6 特有的環境類型，介於一般空間（UC）與 ISO 分級潔淨室之間：

  • 有 HVAC 控制（溫度、濕度、換氣次數），但未達 ISO 14644 的正式分級標準
  • 適用於封閉系統操作（如密閉管路、密閉生物反應器），因製程本身提供足夠的污染屏障
  • CNC+ 則額外加裝本地監測設備（如粒子計數器），提升環境數據可見度

CHO（中國倉鼠卵巢細胞株）

CHO 是生物製藥業最廣泛使用的哺乳動物表達系統，約 70% 的治療性蛋白質（包括多數 MAb）由 CHO 細胞生產。了解 CHO 細胞特性（對 pH、溶氧、溫度敏感）有助於理解生物反應器設計要求。

MAb（單株抗體）— 生物製藥的旗艦產品

MAb（Monoclonal Antibody，單株抗體）是目前全球銷售額最高的生物製藥產品類別（包括抗腫瘤、自體免疫疾病治療藥物）。MAb 生產流程（細胞培養 → 收穫 → 蛋白A純化 → 病毒去除過濾 → 製劑）是本 ISPE Vol.6 設施設計的主要應用場景。

SIP vs CIP — 兩個必須區分的概念

CIP（就地清洗，Clean-In-Place）：使用清洗液（NaOH、酸液等）在不拆卸設備的情況下清除污垢和殘留。目標是減少生物負荷（bioburden reduction）。

SIP（就地滅菌，Steam-In-Place）：使用飽和蒸汽（通常 121°C / 15 分鐘）在不拆卸設備的情況下達到滅菌（sterile = 零生物負荷）。目標是消滅所有活微生物。

順序：CIP 先行，SIP 其後。就像洗碗（CIP）後才能送去高壓消毒（SIP）。

比喻：MCB vs WCB

把 MCB（Master Cell Bank，主細胞庫）想像成細胞的「原版母帶」，WCB（Working Cell Bank，工作細胞庫）是「複製品」。每次生產批次使用 WCB 的一小管，MCB 永遠作為備份保存。若 WCB 受污染，可從 MCB 重新展開（re-derive）。MCB 的保存條件和特性確認是生物製藥廠最重要的資產保護措施之一。

12.2 Definitions — Part 1: A through C（定義：A 至 C）

原文 — Definitions: A–C

Adventitious Agents（外源性污染微生物）

Adventitious agents are microorganisms that have been unintentionally introduced into the manufacturing process of a biological product. Adventitious agents include bacteria, fungi, mycoplasmas, rickettsia, protozoa, parasites, Transmissible Spongiform Encephalopathy (TSE) agents, and viruses.

Airborne Total Particulate（空浮總粒子）

A measurement of airborne particles in a specified size range (typically determined by mass mean diameter) as recorded by a Discrete Particle Counter (DPC). Since the vast majority of particle counters are incapable of distinguishing between viable and non-viable particulate, this measurement is erroneously called "non-viable".

Air Change Rate / Ventilation Rate（換氣次數）

The volume of air supplied to a room (per hour) divided by the volume of the room. This is a purely numerical evaluation used as a rule of thumb in cleanroom design.

Aseptic Operations（無菌操作）

Processes that are devoid of measurable (detectable) bioburden. Aseptic operations generally require sterilization of the environment, equipment and process solutions to achieve the sterile state prior to use.

Aseptic Transfer（無菌移送）

Material transfer where the risk of contamination from the environment has been mitigated.

Axenic State（純淨狀態）

A culture that includes the intended living organism but is entirely free of all other contaminating organisms.

Bioburden-Free（無微生物負荷）

A condition where bioburden is not detectable. Bioreactors used in cell culture or fermentation operations should be sterile prior to use for consistent and reproducible performance. Biosafety Cabinets (BSCs), RABs and isolators should provide an environment free of bioburden for consistent and reproducible aseptic operations. Sterile product manufacturing testing and qualification guidelines are by necessity more stringent and prescriptive than that of active pharmaceutical ingredient manufacturing and therefore are not required.

Bioprocessing（生物製造加工）

Biologics manufacturing. Includes all operations used in the manufacture of biologics including upstream processes such as inoculum preparation, cell culture/fermentation processes, harvest and clarification processes such as sedimentation and filtration processes, downstream processing such as chromatography and filtration processes.

Briefly Exposed（短暫暴露）

Open processes containing process and/or product components that are rendered closed by means of an appropriate closing process. Examples of briefly exposed processes include open buffer or media preparations where the solution is "briefly" exposed to the environment prior to closing by sterile filtration and/or thermal sanitization. Briefly exposed operations may be performed in Controlled Not Classified (CNC) or low bioburden environments if measures used to close the process are appropriate to mitigate risk of contamination from the environment.

Carryover（殘留攜帶）

Contaminants detected in process streams arising from insufficient removal of contaminating components from previous manufacturing steps or batches. Maximum allowable carryover residues should be estimated and meet defined criteria. Carryover is typically a result of insufficient cleaning, sanitization, rinsing and/or conditioning.

導師解析 — A至C 關鍵術語

Adventitious Agents — 生物製藥的頭號風險

外源性污染微生物（尤其是病毒，包括 TSE 朊病毒）是生物製藥安全性的核心挑戰，因為：

  • 原料（動物源血清、原料細胞）可能攜帶潛伏病毒
  • TSE 朊病毒具有異常的抗滅菌性（一般 121°C 蒸汽滅菌無法完全消滅）
  • ICH Q5A 專門規範生物製品的病毒安全測試要求

設施設計需包含「病毒去除/不活化步驟」（如低 pH 不活化、奈米過濾）並設置病毒隔離區域。

Airborne Total Particulate — 「非活性」粒子的迷思

本定義特別提醒：粒子計數器無法區分活性（有菌）和非活性（無菌）粒子，因此常見的「非活性粒子計數」其實是「總粒子計數」。活性微生物監測需要另外的方法（如沉降碟、接觸碟）。這是設計環境監測計畫時必須理解的基本限制。

Axenic State（純淨狀態）— 與 Sterile 的差異

Axenic（純淨）強調「只有目標生物，沒有任何污染生物」，常用於描述細胞培養或發酵過程中的理想狀態。與 Sterile（無菌）的差異：

  • Sterile（無菌）：完全無任何活的微生物，包括目標生物
  • Axenic（純淨）：只有目標生物存在，無雜菌，但目標生物本身是活的

發酵槽在接種後的理想狀態是 Axenic（純培養），而不是 Sterile。

Bioburden-Free（無微生物負荷）— 不等於無菌

Bioburden-Free 的技術定義是「以現有檢測方法，生物負荷無法被偵測到」。這意味著：

  • 它是一個偵測限度的概念，而非絕對的零
  • 用於描述環境（BSC 內部、RABs 內部）應達到的狀態
  • 比較保守的「功能性」說法，相對於更嚴格的「Sterile（無菌）」

這也是為何 ISPE Vol.6 不要求所有生物製程空間都達到無菌等級，而是依照製程開放程度設計相應的環境。

比喻：Briefly Exposed 就像開蓋的鍋子

「短暫暴露」就像燉湯時短暫掀蓋加料，隨後立刻蓋回（無菌過濾或熱滅菌「關閉」製程）。關鍵是：暴露時間要短、後續的密閉步驟必須充分驗證。若暴露時間太長或滅菌步驟不足以消滅潛在污染，就需要升級環境等級。

Carryover（殘留攜帶）— 多產品廠的核心風險

對於同時生產多種生物製品的 CDMO 而言，Carryover 是最重要的跨批次污染風險。ISPE Baseline Guide Vol.7（Risk-MaPP）提供了評估最大允許殘留量（MACO）的方法學。設計良好的 CIP 程序、適當的沖洗確效和殘留測試是管控 Carryover 的關鍵。

12.2 Definitions — Part 2: Closed / Open System & Process Closure（密閉與開放系統）

原文 — Closed System, Open Process & Related Terms

Classified Space（分級潔淨空間）

Areas where HVAC systems are specifically designed to reduce airborne contaminants below a specified level as defined in ISO 14644-1 (tested per ISO 14644-2 and ISO 14644-3) and both temperature and Relative Humidity (RH) are controlled more tightly than in the ambient environment. These areas must be performance verified / qualified. These areas may be tested to meet ISO requirements for airborne 0.5 µm particulate and viable organisms in the "in-operation" state to meet US FDA requirements or they may be tested to meet ISO requirements for both airborne 0.5 µm and 5.0 µm particulate as well as viable organisms in both the "in-operation" state as well as the "at-rest" state to meet EMA and PIC/S requirements. Where EMA and PIC/S requirements are to be satisfied the transition between these two states should take place in 15 to 20 minutes.

Closed System（密閉系統）

A process system that is designed and operated such that the product is never exposed to the surrounding environment. Additions to and draws from closed systems must be performed in a completely closed fashion. Sterile filters may be used to provide effective barriers from contaminants in the environment. A system is closed (or isolated from the environment) when the risk of contamination to the product or process cannot be mitigated by housing the operation in a bioburden-free or particulate-free environment. In Quality Risk Management (QRM) Verification, the environment does not represent a Critical Aspect of a closed process. A closed process is one that has been validated to show that there are sufficient layers of protection to mitigate the risk of contamination from the environment. The detection of a contaminant from the environment in an otherwise closed system indicates a breach of the closed system and therefore constitutes a system failure. Examples of closed systems include sterile single use bags supplied with integrated aseptic connection devices.

Functionally Closed（功能性密閉）

Process systems that may be opened but are "rendered closed" by a cleaning, sanitization and/or sterilization process that is appropriate or consistent with the process requirements. These systems shall remain closed during production within the system. A functionally closed process must be validated to show that sufficient layers of protection have been implemented to mitigate the risk of contamination from the environment. Transfers into or from these systems must also be validated as closed. Examples include process vessels that may be cleaned in place and steamed in place between uses.

Open Process（開放式製程）

A process that is not closed and therefore requires appropriate environmental controls to mitigate the risk of contamination from the environment. Under QRM verification, the environment within the RABs and/or BSCs represents a critical aspect of the open process. Open sterile and aseptic operations must be performed in an environment where the probability of contamination is acceptably low. Open bioburden-controlled processing may be performed in a Grade 7 or 8 environment as appropriate for the unit operation.

Critical Control Point — CCP（關鍵管制點）

A step where control is required to prevent or eliminate a product safety or quality hazard or reduce it to an acceptable level.

Critical Process Parameter — CPP（關鍵製程參數）

A measurable input (input material attribute or operating parameter) or output (process state variable or output material attribute) of a process step that must be controlled to achieve the desired product quality and process consistency.

Critical Quality Attribute — CQA（關鍵品質屬性）

Physical, chemical, biological or microbiological properties or characteristics that need to be controlled (directly or indirectly) to ensure product quality (ISPE PQLI Guide). Physical, chemical, biological or microbiological properties or characteristics that should be within an appropriate limit, range, or distribution to ensure the desired product quality (ICH Q8(R2)).

Cross-Contamination / Crossover（交叉污染）

Contamination of the product or processing area by components or contaminants found in a neighboring product or processing area. Cross contamination typically occurs between open processes. Recirculating HVAC can be a source of cross contamination if improperly designed.

導師解析 — 密閉/開放系統與 CQA/CPP

密閉系統的三個關鍵判定條件

ISPE Vol.6 的「密閉系統」定義比直覺更嚴格，必須同時滿足：

  1. 設計密閉：產品永不暴露於周圍環境
  2. 操作密閉：所有進出（取樣、添加、排放）均以密閉方式進行
  3. 確效密閉：已驗證（validated）系統能提供足夠的保護層

符合這三個條件，環境才「不是」製程的 Critical Aspect——也就是說，該空間的環境等級可以降低（如使用 CNC 而非 ISO 7/8）。

密閉系統違規的後果

「若在原本密閉的系統中偵測到來自環境的污染物，即構成系統失效（system failure）。」這個定義說明了密閉系統違規（breach）的嚴重性——這不只是偏差（deviation），而是整個密閉系統設計假設的崩潰，需要徹底的根本原因調查和設計評審。

三種密閉程度的環境要求對比

比喻：密閉系統 vs 開放系統如同保溫瓶 vs 敞口杯

密閉系統就像保溫瓶：無論外界環境多髒，裡面的飲料都不受影響（只要蓋子確實蓋緊且已清潔滅菌）。開放系統就像敞口的水杯：一旦置於不乾淨的環境中，就必然受到污染風險。因此開放系統操作就必須在潔淨室（像把水杯放在極度潔淨的無塵房間）中進行。

CQA vs CPP — 生物製藥 QbD 的核心語言

這兩個概念是 ICH Q8/Q10 品質體系的核心，也是 ISPE Vol.6 設施設計的驅動力：

  • CQA（關鍵品質屬性）：定義「我需要保護什麼」，例如蛋白質的糖型分佈、生物活性、純度。CQA 直接關係到患者安全。
  • CPP（關鍵製程參數）：定義「我需要控制什麼」，例如細胞培養的 pH、溶氧、溫度。CPP 是控制 CQA 的手段。

設施設計邏輯：CQA → 找出影響 CQA 的 CPP → 設計能有效監控和控制 CPP 的設施和系統。

練習思考

  1. 一個配置了 CIP/SIP 的不鏽鋼生物反應器，是屬於 Closed、Functionally Closed 還是 Open 系統？其所在空間需要什麼環境等級？
  2. 單株抗體的 CQA 可能包括哪些屬性？對應的設施設計要求是什麼？
  3. 為什麼說「密閉系統違規」比一般偏差更嚴重？
12.2 Definitions — Part 3: Environmental Monitoring, Classification & Remaining Terms

原文 — Environmental & Remaining Definitions

ISO 14644 — Classification（環境分級）

This standard classifies spaces following a decimal system according to the concentration of particulate in a series of size ranges, specifically: 0.1, 0.2, 0.3, 0.5, 1.0, and 5.0 µm. An ISO class designation indicates that particulate within the space are within limits as defined by the formula Cn = 10N × (0.1/D)2.08 where Cn is the particle count, N is the ISO class, and D is the particle mean diameter in µm.

ISO 14644-1 Air Quality Classes Table

Note: 1 cubic meter = 35.3 cubic feet. FDA measures only 0.5 µm (in-operation). EMA/PIC/S measures both 0.5 µm and 5.0 µm (at-rest and in-operation).

FDA Application of ISO Classifications
  • ISO 5: 3,520 particles/m³ (0.5 µm), in-operation. Normally with unidirectional flow (0.20–0.45 m/s)
  • ISO 6: 35,200 particles/m³, in-operation
  • ISO 7: 352,000 particles/m³, in-operation
  • ISO 8: 3,520,000 particles/m³, in-operation
  • ISO 9: 35,200,000 particles/m³ (not in FDA guidance but found in FDA-regulated facilities)
Local Protected Environments（本地保護環境）

Local protected environments may be used for open processes. Examples include Biosafety Cabinets (BSCs), Unidirectional Down Flow Hoods (UDFHs), isolators and Restricted Access Barriers (RABs). When used, it is critical that the local environment be protected from unexpected breach. Only a bioburden-free environment should be used for open aseptic operations.

Low Bioburden (operation)（低微生物負荷操作）

Process where a limited and controlled level of measurable bioburden is acceptable under specific conditions. (e.g. WFI, chromatography operations).

MERV (Multiple Efficiency Reporting Value)（過濾效率值）

The ASHRAE Standard 52.2 method of testing filter efficiency by challenging filters with particles of multiple sizes and integrating the efficiency into a single number rating. The higher the MERV number the more efficient the filter. MERV 14/15 is approximately equivalent to a 95% (ASHRAE) efficient filter.

Risk Assessment（風險評估）

Systematic process of organizing information to support risk decisions. This includes identification of risk(s) and evaluation of the nature, severity and likelihood of those risk(s).

Sanitization（衛生消毒）

Operation that reduces the level of bioburden.

Sterile（無菌）/ Sterilization（滅菌）

Sterile: Devoid of life. Zero bioburden. Free of bioburden.

Sterilization: Form of sanitization that results in a bioburden-free (sterile) condition. Methods include thermal sterilization (121°C/15 minutes or higher), sterile filtration (0.2 µm or better), chemical sterilization (e.g., VHP, chlorine dioxide, ozone) or irradiation (e.g. gamma, UV).

Uncontrolled — UC（非受控區域）

Areas where the HVAC systems may be present, but no claim is made or qualified for the specific control of particulate, temperature or humidity. These areas are sometimes referred to as "general" or "comfort controlled" areas within pharmaceutical facilities such as office and technical space.

Ventilation Efficiency (Effectiveness)（換氣效率）

The ability of an HVAC system to dilute contaminants when compared to ideal dilution. A Ventilation Effectiveness of 1.0 indicates ideal dilution. Displacement ventilation may have an effectiveness as high as 3.0 to 4.0.

導師解析 — 環境監測與分級深度解析

ISO 分級 vs EU GMP 等級 — 雙軌體系對應

全球生物製藥廠必須同時理解兩套環境分級語言：

FDA vs EMA 差異：FDA 只要求在「動態（in-operation）」下測試 0.5µm 粒子；EMA/PIC/S 另外要求「靜態（at-rest）」以及 5µm 粒子的數據，且兩個狀態的轉換應在 15-20 分鐘內完成。

ISO 分級公式

C_n = 10^N × (0.1 / D)^2.08

其中：
  C_n = 最大允許粒子濃度 (粒子/m³)
  N   = ISO 等級數 (1-9)
  D   = 粒子平均直徑 (µm)

例：ISO 5 等級，0.5 µm 粒子：
  C_n = 10^5 × (0.1/0.5)^2.08
      = 100,000 × (0.2)^2.08
      ≈ 3,520 粒子/m³  ✓（與表格一致）

15-20 分鐘恢復時間 — EMA 獨有要求

EU GMP 要求從「動態」到「靜態」的環境恢復（recovery）時間必須在 15-20 分鐘內完成，這可透過 ISO 14644-3 的「恢復測試（recovery test）」驗證。此要求直接影響 HVAC 設計的換氣次數（ACH）和氣流速度。台灣 CDMO 若申請歐盟市場必須在確效報告中包含此測試數據。

Sterilization 方法選擇原則

不同滅菌方法各有適用場景：

  • 熱滅菌（SIP, 121°C/15min）：最可靠，用於不鏽鋼設備、管路；需確效 F₀ 值
  • 無菌過濾（0.2µm）：用於不耐熱溶液（培養基、蛋白質溶液）
  • VHP（過氧化氫蒸汽）：用於環境表面、隔離器去污；需確效殺孢效果（6-log D-value)
  • UV 輻射：用於空氣、表面；穿透力弱，僅限暴露面
  • γ 射線：用於一次性使用物品（如 SU 袋）；無法現場使用

比喻：MERV 就像口罩的過濾等級

MERV 值就像口罩的 N 數（N95、N99）：數字越高，過濾效率越強。MERV 14/15 ≈ 95% 過濾效率，約等於一般潔淨室的 bag filter；HEPA 則是 99.97% 以上（超過 MERV 評分上限）。選擇 MERV 等級需在過濾效能和系統壓降（energy cost）之間取得平衡。

練習思考

  1. 一個配置 VHP 去污系統的隔離器（Isolator）內部，應達到什麼 ISO 等級？使用什麼方法確效？
  2. FDA 監管和 EMA 監管的廠房在環境監測方面有哪兩個主要差異？
  3. 使用 0.2µm 過濾器進行無菌過濾，可以去除病毒嗎？為什麼需要額外的病毒去除步驟？
快速參考摘要表 — 15 個最重要術語

以下 15 個術語是 ISPE Baseline Guide Vol.6 中頻率最高、最具實務影響力的核心概念，建議熟記其縮寫與一行中文定義。

本節重點回顧 — Section Summary

  • 附錄二的 70 個參考文獻構成一個完整的國際法規生態系統：ICH Q7/Q9/Q10/Q11 建立品質體系基礎，21 CFR Part 211 和 EU GMP Annex 1/2 設定市場准入要求，ISO 14644 系列提供環境分級技術標準，NIH/CDC 生物安全指引決定圍堵等級。
  • 密閉系統（Closed System）是 Vol.6 最重要的設計概念：已驗證密閉的系統不需要高等級潔淨室（CNC 即可），但密閉違規即視為「系統失效」，需要根本原因分析。
  • CQA（關鍵品質屬性）和 CPP（關鍵製程參數）是設施設計的驅動力；設施設計的本質是「建立能有效監控和保護 CPP，從而確保 CQA 的物理環境」。
  • BSL（生物安全等級）決定廠房圍堵策略的起點，這是 GMP 之外的生物安全法律義務，二者必須同時遵守。
  • ISO 分級（FDA：只測動態 0.5µm；EMA：測靜態+動態、0.5µm+5µm，15-20 分鐘恢復時間）的雙軌差異在進行多市場廠房確效時必須特別注意。
  • 15 個核心術語（CQA、CPP、BSL、CNC、SIP、CIP、Closed System、Axenic State、Bioburden-Free、RABS、QRM、VHP、WFI、MCB/WCB、Classified Space）是與任何監管機構溝通生物製藥廠設計的共同語言。
